# ========================================
# FILE: .\print_tree.py
# ========================================

# print_tree.py
from pathlib import Path

def print_directory_tree(root_dir: Path, current_dir: Path, prefix: str = "", ignore_dirs=None):
    if ignore_dirs is None:
        # Explicitly omit environments, caches, and raw data indexing paths
        ignore_dirs = {
            ".git", 
            "__pycache__", 
            "agent_env", 
            "venv", 
            ".venv", 
            "node_modules", 
            "data", 
            "index", 
            "index_data"
        }
        
    try:
        # Gather and sort files so folders appear cleanly structured
        paths = sorted(list(current_dir.iterdir()), key=lambda p: (p.is_file(), p.name.lower()))
    except PermissionError:
        # Handle system folders or restricted files gracefully
        return

    for i, path in enumerate(paths):
        if path.name in ignore_dirs:
            continue
            
        is_last = (i == len(paths) - 1)
        connector = "└── " if is_last else "├── "
        
        print(f"{prefix}{connector}{path.name}")
        
        # Recurse if the path is a directory
        if path.is_dir():
            new_prefix = prefix + ("    " if is_last else "│   ")
            print_directory_tree(root_dir, path, new_prefix, ignore_dirs)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    project_root = Path(".")
    print(f"\n📁 {project_root.resolve().name}/")
    print_directory_tree(project_root, project_root)

# ========================================
# FILE: .\backend\config\task_config.py
# ========================================

import json
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, Any
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict


@dataclass
class TaskThresholds:
    """Configuration for task generation thresholds"""
    # Fan-out thresholds (function calls too many others)
    fan_out_medium: int = 5
    fan_out_high: int = 10
    fan_out_critical: int = 20
    
    # Fan-in thresholds (function called by too many)
    fan_in_medium: int = 5
    fan_in_high: int = 10
    fan_in_critical: int = 20
    
    # LLM task generation settings
    llm_enabled: bool = True
    llm_max_tasks: int = 10
    llm_model: str = "qwen2.5-coder:3b"


class TaskConfig:
    """Configuration manager for task generation"""
    
    def __init__(self, project_id: str):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.config_dir = Path("data/config")
        self.config_file = self.config_dir / f"{project_id}_task_config.json"
        self._ensure_dir()
        self.thresholds = self._load()
    
    def _ensure_dir(self):
        self.config_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    
    def _load(self) -> TaskThresholds:
        """Load config from disk or create default"""
        if self.config_file.exists():
            try:
                data = json.loads(self.config_file.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
                return TaskThresholds(**data)
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"Error loading config: {e}")
                return TaskThresholds()
        return TaskThresholds()
    
    def save(self) -> None:
        """Save config to disk"""
        self.config_file.write_text(
            json.dumps(asdict(self.thresholds), indent=2),
            encoding="utf-8"
        )
    
    def get(self) -> TaskThresholds:
        """Get current thresholds"""
        return self.thresholds
    
    def update(self, updates: Dict[str, int]) -> None:
        """Update thresholds and save"""
        for key, value in updates.items():
            if hasattr(self.thresholds, key):
                setattr(self.thresholds, key, value)
        self.save()
    
    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Convert to dictionary for API response"""
        return asdict(self.thresholds)

# FILE: .\backend\models\refactor.py

from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from typing import List, Optional, Dict, Any
from enum import Enum


class RefactorType(str, Enum):
    ADD_PARAMETER = "add_parameter"
    REMOVE_PARAMETER = "remove_parameter"
    RENAME_FUNCTION = "rename_function"
    EXTRACT_METHOD = "extract_method"
    INLINE_FUNCTION = "inline_function"


class ChangeType(str, Enum):
    FUNCTION_DEFINITION = "function_definition"
    CALLER_UPDATE = "caller_update"
    IMPORT_UPDATE = "import_update"
    CLASS_UPDATE = "class_update"


@dataclass
class Parameter:
    name: str
    type_hint: Optional[str] = None
    default_value: Optional[str] = None
    is_required: bool = True

    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "name": self.name,
            "type_hint": self.type_hint,
            "default_value": self.default_value,
            "is_required": self.is_required
        }

    @classmethod
    def from_dict(cls, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> "Parameter":
        return cls(
            name=data["name"],
            type_hint=data.get("type_hint"),
            default_value=data.get("default_value"),
            is_required=data.get("is_required", True)
        )


@dataclass
class CallSite:
    file_path: str
    line_number: int
    calling_function: str
    arguments: List[str]
    source_line: str
    argument_count: int

    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "file_path": self.file_path,
            "line_number": self.line_number,
            "calling_function": self.calling_function,
            "arguments": self.arguments,
            "source_line": self.source_line,
            "argument_count": self.argument_count
        }


@dataclass
class FunctionDetail:
    name: str
    file_path: str
    line_start: int
    line_end: int
    source_code: str
    parameters: List[Parameter]
    return_type: Optional[str] = None
    decorators: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    is_async: bool = False
    is_method: bool = False
    class_name: Optional[str] = None
    docstring: Optional[str] = None
    callers: List[CallSite] = field(default_factory=list)

    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "name": self.name,
            "file_path": self.file_path,
            "line_start": self.line_start,
            "line_end": self.line_end,
            "source_code": self.source_code,
            "parameters": [p.to_dict() for p in self.parameters],
            "return_type": self.return_type,
            "decorators": self.decorators,
            "is_async": self.is_async,
            "is_method": self.is_method,
            "class_name": self.class_name,
            "docstring": self.docstring,
            "callers": [c.to_dict() for c in self.callers]
        }


@dataclass
class FileChange:
    file_path: str
    line_start: int
    line_end: int
    before: str
    after: str
    change_type: ChangeType
    description: str

    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "file_path": self.file_path,
            "line_start": self.line_start,
            "line_end": self.line_end,
            "before": self.before,
            "after": self.after,
            "change_type": self.change_type.value,
            "description": self.description
        }


@dataclass
class RefactoringPlan:
    id: str
    target_function: str
    refactor_type: RefactorType
    changes: List[FileChange]
    affected_files: List[str]
    confidence: float
    requires_review: bool
    warning: Optional[str] = None

    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "id": self.id,
            "target_function": self.target_function,
            "refactor_type": self.refactor_type.value,
            "changes": [c.to_dict() for c in self.changes],
            "affected_files": self.affected_files,
            "confidence": self.confidence,
            "requires_review": self.requires_review,
            "warning": self.warning
        }
        
# Add is_public_api method to FunctionDetail
def is_public_api(self) -> bool:
    """Check if function is likely a public API"""
    # Not starting with underscore (unless it's __init__ etc)
    if self.name.startswith('_') and not self.name.startswith('__'):
        return False
    # Has docstring often indicates public API
    if self.docstring:
        return True
    # Is a method without underscore prefix
    return not self.name.startswith('_')

FunctionDetail.is_public_api = is_public_api

from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from datetime import datetime
from enum import Enum
from typing import Optional, List, Dict, Any


class TaskStatus(str, Enum):
    PENDING = "pending"
    IN_PROGRESS = "in_progress"
    DONE = "done"
    IGNORED = "ignored"
    DEFERRED = "deferred"


class TaskPriority(str, Enum):
    CRITICAL = "critical"
    HIGH = "high"
    MEDIUM = "medium"
    LOW = "low"


class TaskCategory(str, Enum):
    HIGH_COUPLING = "high_coupling"      # Fan-out: calls too many functions
    HIGH_USAGE = "high_usage"             # Fan-in: called by too many
    COMPLEXITY = "complexity"             # Too complex/long function
    CIRCULAR_DEP = "circular_dependency"  # Circular import or call cycle
    GOD_CLASS = "god_class"               # Class does too much
    DEAD_CODE = "dead_code"               # No callers, no usage
    MAINTAINABILITY = "maintainability"   # Code smell / tech debt (ADD THIS)
    PERFORMANCE = "performance"           # Performance issues (ADD THIS)
    SECURITY = "security"                 # Security vulnerabilities (ADD THIS)
    RELIABILITY = "reliability"           # Reliability issues (ADD THIS)
    ARCHITECTURE = "architecture"         # Architecture issues (ADD THIS)


@dataclass
class TaskEvidence:
    """Evidence supporting a task recommendation"""
    symbol: str
    metric_type: str
    metric_value: int
    file_path: str
    line_range: Optional[tuple] = None
    callers: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    callees: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    source: str = "rule_based"

    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "symbol": self.symbol,
            "metric_type": self.metric_type,
            "metric_value": self.metric_value,
            "file_path": self.file_path,
            "line_range": self.line_range,
            "callers": self.callers[:10],
            "callees": self.callees[:10],
            "source": self.source 
        }


@dataclass
class AnalysisTask:
    """A task generated by the AI review agent"""
    id: str
    title: str
    description: str
    category: TaskCategory
    priority: TaskPriority
    status: TaskStatus
    evidence: List[TaskEvidence]
    suggested_fix: Optional[str] = None
    impact_analysis: Optional[str] = None
    created_at: datetime = field(default_factory=datetime.now)
    updated_at: datetime = field(default_factory=datetime.now)
    notes: Optional[str] = None

    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "id": self.id,
            "title": self.title,
            "description": self.description,
            "category": self.category.value,
            "priority": self.priority.value,
            "status": self.status.value,
            "evidence": [e.to_dict() for e in self.evidence],
            "suggested_fix": self.suggested_fix,
            "impact_analysis": self.impact_analysis,
            "created_at": self.created_at.isoformat(),
            "updated_at": self.updated_at.isoformat(),
            "notes": self.notes
        }

# FILE: .\backend\routers\agent.py
# ========================================

from fastapi import APIRouter, Query
from fastapi.responses import StreamingResponse
from pathlib import Path

from backend.services.context.context_builder import ContextBuilder
from backend.services.agent.prompt_builder import PromptBuilder
from backend.services.llm.ollama_client import OllamaClient
from backend.services.project_service import ProjectService
from config import INDEX_DIR

router = APIRouter(prefix="/api/agent", tags=["Agent"])

# FIXED: Use consistent index path resolution
project = ProjectService().get_active_project()
INDEX_PATH = INDEX_DIR / project["project_id"]

# Instantiate services
context_builder = ContextBuilder(INDEX_PATH)
prompt_builder = PromptBuilder()
llm_client = OllamaClient()


@router.get("/stream")
async def stream_agent_response(
    question: str = Query(..., description="The user query or code question"),
    symbol_name: str = Query(None, description="Target symbol if explicitly extracted")
):
    """
    Asynchronously streams repository context analysis back to the development chat frame.
    """
    def token_generator():
        context_data = None
        intent = "explain_symbol"

        if symbol_name:
            context_data = context_builder.build(symbol_name, intent="explain_symbol")

        if not context_data:
            intent = "general_query"
            context_data = {
                "message": "No direct codebase symbol matches resolved for this request context."
            }

        full_prompt = prompt_builder.build(
            intent=intent,
            crawler_review_data=context_data,
            question=question,
            history=[]
        )

        for token in llm_client.generate_stream(full_prompt):
            yield token

    return StreamingResponse(token_generator(), media_type="text/plain")

# FILE: .\backend\routers\agent_query.py

from fastapi import APIRouter

from backend.services.agent.intent_classifier import IntentClassifier
from backend.services.agent.entity_extractor import EntityExtractor

router = APIRouter(
    prefix="/agent",
    tags=["Agent Query"]
)

classifier = IntentClassifier()
extractor = EntityExtractor()


@router.post("/classify")
def classify(payload: dict):

    question = payload.get("question", "")

    intent = classifier.classify(question)
    symbol = extractor.extract_symbol(question)

    return {
        "question": question,
        "intent": intent.value,
        "symbol": symbol
    }

# FILE: .\backend\routers\index.py

from fastapi import APIRouter

from backend.services.project_service import ProjectService
from backend.services.indexing.index_service import IndexService
from backend.services.indexing.serializer import IndexSerializer
from config import DATA_DIR

router = APIRouter(prefix="/index", tags=["Indexing"])

project_service = ProjectService(f"{DATA_DIR}/projects.json")
serializer = IndexSerializer(f"{DATA_DIR}/index")


@router.post("/build/{project_id}")
def build_index(project_id: str):
    # 1. Load project config
    project = project_service.get_project(project_id)

    # 2. Create index service
    index_service = IndexService(project)

    # 3. Build index
    result = index_service.build_index()
    
    # DEBUG: Print counts safely (removed problematic prints)
    print(f"Index built for {project_id}")
    print(f"  Files: {len(result.get('files', []))}")
    print(f"  Symbols: {len(result.get('symbols', []))}")
    print(f"  Imports: {len(result.get('imports', []))}")

    # 4. Save index
    manifest = serializer.save(project_id, result)

    return {
        "status": "success",
        "project_id": project_id,
        "manifest": manifest
    }


@router.get("/status/{project_id}")
def index_status(project_id: str):
    import os

    path = f"{DATA_DIR}/index/{project_id}/manifest.json"

    if not os.path.exists(path):
        return {
            "project_id": project_id,
            "indexed": False
        }

    return {
        "project_id": project_id,
        "indexed": True
    }

# backend/routers/refactor.py

from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException, Depends, status
from typing import Optional, List, Dict, Any
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field

from backend.models.refactor import (
    RefactorType, Parameter, RefactoringPlan, ChangeType
)
from backend.services.refactor.code_analyzer import CodeAnalyzer
from backend.services.refactor.impact_scanner import ImpactScanner, ImpactLevel
from backend.services.refactor.change_engine import ChangeEngine
from backend.services.project_service import ProjectService
from backend.services.refactor.llm_refactor_engine import LLMRefactorEngine

router = APIRouter(prefix="/api/refactor", tags=["refactoring"])


# Request/Response Models
class ParameterRequest(BaseModel):
    """Request model for parameter operations"""
    name: str
    type_hint: Optional[str] = None
    default_value: Optional[str] = None
    is_required: bool = True


class AddParameterRequest(BaseModel):
    """Request for adding a parameter"""
    function_name: str
    new_parameter: ParameterRequest
    default_value: Optional[str] = None
    position: Optional[int] = None


class RemoveParameterRequest(BaseModel):
    """Request for removing a parameter"""
    function_name: str
    parameter_name: str


class RenameFunctionRequest(BaseModel):
    """Request for renaming a function"""
    function_name: str
    new_name: str


class RefactorPlanResponse(BaseModel):
    """Response model for refactoring plan"""
    id: str
    target_function: str
    refactor_type: str
    changes: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    affected_files: List[str]
    confidence: float
    requires_review: bool
    warning: Optional[str] = None


class ImpactAnalysisResponse(BaseModel):
    """Response model for impact analysis"""
    impact_level: str
    affected_files: List[str]
    total_callers: int
    breaking_changes: bool
    warnings: List[str]
    suggestions: List[str]
    complexity_score: float


class FunctionDetailResponse(BaseModel):
    """Response model for function details"""
    name: str
    file_path: str
    line_start: int
    line_end: int
    parameters: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    return_type: Optional[str]
    decorators: List[str]
    is_async: bool
    is_method: bool
    class_name: Optional[str]
    docstring: Optional[str]
    caller_count: int
    source_code_preview: str
    
class ExtractMethodRequest(BaseModel):
    function_name: str
    start_line: int
    end_line: int
    new_method_name: str

class InlineFunctionRequest(BaseModel):
    function_name: str

def get_project_id() -> str:
    """Get current project ID"""
    project_service = ProjectService()
    active_project = project_service.get_active_project()
    if not active_project:
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
            detail="No active project selected"
        )
    return active_project["project_id"]


@router.get("/analyze/function/{function_name}", response_model=FunctionDetailResponse)
async def analyze_function(
    function_name: str,
    project_id: str = Depends(get_project_id)
):
    """
    Get detailed information about a function including parameters and callers.
    """
    analyzer = CodeAnalyzer(project_id)
    func_detail = analyzer.get_function_detail(function_name)
    
    if not func_detail:
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND,
            detail=f"Function '{function_name}' not found"
        )
    
    # Create preview (first 200 chars)
    preview = func_detail.source_code[:200] + "..." if len(func_detail.source_code) > 200 else func_detail.source_code
    
    return FunctionDetailResponse(
        name=func_detail.name,
        file_path=func_detail.file_path,
        line_start=func_detail.line_start,
        line_end=func_detail.line_end,
        parameters=[p.to_dict() for p in func_detail.parameters],
        return_type=func_detail.return_type,
        decorators=func_detail.decorators,
        is_async=func_detail.is_async,
        is_method=func_detail.is_method,
        class_name=func_detail.class_name,
        docstring=func_detail.docstring,
        caller_count=len(func_detail.callers),
        source_code_preview=preview
    )


@router.post("/impact/add-parameter", response_model=ImpactAnalysisResponse)
async def analyze_add_parameter_impact(
    request: AddParameterRequest,
    project_id: str = Depends(get_project_id)
):
    """
    Analyze impact of adding a new parameter to a function.
    """
    scanner = ImpactScanner(project_id)
    
    new_param = Parameter(
        name=request.new_parameter.name,
        type_hint=request.new_parameter.type_hint,
        default_value=request.new_parameter.default_value,
        is_required=request.new_parameter.is_required
    )
    
    impact = scanner.analyze_add_parameter(
        request.function_name,
        new_param,
        request.default_value
    )
    
    return ImpactAnalysisResponse(
        impact_level=impact.impact_level.value,
        affected_files=impact.affected_files,
        total_callers=impact.total_callers,
        breaking_changes=impact.breaking_changes,
        warnings=impact.warnings,
        suggestions=impact.suggestions,
        complexity_score=impact.complexity_score
    )


@router.post("/impact/remove-parameter", response_model=ImpactAnalysisResponse)
async def analyze_remove_parameter_impact(
    request: RemoveParameterRequest,
    project_id: str = Depends(get_project_id)
):
    """
    Analyze impact of removing a parameter from a function.
    """
    scanner = ImpactScanner(project_id)
    
    impact = scanner.analyze_remove_parameter(
        request.function_name,
        request.parameter_name
    )
    
    return ImpactAnalysisResponse(
        impact_level=impact.impact_level.value,
        affected_files=impact.affected_files,
        total_callers=impact.total_callers,
        breaking_changes=impact.breaking_changes,
        warnings=impact.warnings,
        suggestions=impact.suggestions,
        complexity_score=impact.complexity_score
    )

async def analyze_rename_function_impact(

    )


@router.post("/plan/add-parameter", response_model=RefactorPlanResponse)
async def generate_add_parameter_plan(
    request: AddParameterRequest,
    project_id: str = Depends(get_project_id)
):
    """
    Generate a refactoring plan for adding a parameter.
    """
    engine = ChangeEngine(project_id)
    
    new_param = Parameter(
        name=request.new_parameter.name,
        type_hint=request.new_parameter.type_hint,
        default_value=request.new_parameter.default_value,
        is_required=request.new_parameter.is_required
    )
    
    plan = engine.generate_add_parameter(
        request.function_name,
        new_param,
        request.default_value,
        request.position
    )
    
    return RefactorPlanResponse(
        id=plan.id,
        target_function=plan.target_function,
        refactor_type=plan.refactor_type.value,
        changes=[c.to_dict() for c in plan.changes],
        affected_files=plan.affected_files,
        confidence=plan.confidence,
        requires_review=plan.requires_review,
        warning=plan.warning
    )


@router.post("/plan/remove-parameter", response_model=RefactorPlanResponse)
async def generate_remove_parameter_plan(
    request: RemoveParameterRequest,
    project_id: str = Depends(get_project_id)
):
    """

    """
    engine = ChangeEngine(project_id)

    return RefactorPlanResponse(
        id=plan.id,

    )

@router.get("/search/functions")
async def search_functions(
    query: str,
    limit: int = 20,
    project_id: str = Depends(get_project_id)
):
    """
    Search for functions by name.
    """
    analyzer = CodeAnalyzer(project_id)
    symbols = analyzer._load_symbols()
    
    results = []
    for sym in symbols:
        if sym.get("type") in ["function", "method"]:
            name = sym.get("name", "")
            if query.lower() in name.lower():
                results.append({
                    "name": name,
                    "file": sym.get("file", ""),
                    "type": sym.get("type"),
                    "parent": sym.get("parent")
                })
                if len(results) >= limit:
                    break
    
    return {"functions": results, "total": len(results)}

async def get_available_refactorings():
    """

    }
    
    
@router.post("/plan/extract-method", response_model=RefactorPlanResponse)
async def generate_extract_method_plan(
    request: ExtractMethodRequest,
    project_id: str = Depends(get_project_id)
):
    """Generate a refactoring plan for extracting a method (uses LLM)"""
    engine = LLMRefactorEngine(project_id)
    
    plan = engine.generate_extract_method(
        request.function_name,
        request.start_line,
        request.end_line,
        request.new_method_name
    )
    
    if not plan:
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,
            detail="Failed to generate extract method plan"
        )
    
    return RefactorPlanResponse(
        id=plan.id,
        target_function=plan.target_function,
        refactor_type=plan.refactor_type.value,
        changes=[c.to_dict() for c in plan.changes],
        affected_files=plan.affected_files,
        confidence=plan.confidence,
        requires_review=plan.requires_review,
        warning=plan.warning
    )


@router.post("/plan/inline-function", response_model=RefactorPlanResponse)
async def generate_inline_function_plan(
    request: InlineFunctionRequest,
    project_id: str = Depends(get_project_id)
):
    """Generate a refactoring plan for inlining a function (uses LLM)"""
    engine = LLMRefactorEngine(project_id)
    
    plan = engine.generate_inline_function(request.function_name)
    
    if not plan:
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,
            detail="Failed to generate inline function plan"
        )
    
    return RefactorPlanResponse(
        id=plan.id,
        target_function=plan.target_function,
        refactor_type=plan.refactor_type.value,
        changes=[c.to_dict() for c in plan.changes],
        affected_files=plan.affected_files,
        confidence=plan.confidence,
        requires_review=plan.requires_review,
        warning=plan.warning
    )


@router.post("/suggest/{function_name}")
async def suggest_refactorings(
    function_name: str,
    project_id: str = Depends(get_project_id)
):
    """Get AI suggestions for refactoring a function"""
    engine = LLMRefactorEngine(project_id)
    
    suggestions = engine.suggest_refactorings(function_name)
    
    return {"function_name": function_name, "suggestions": suggestions}

from fastapi import APIRouter

from backend.services.project_service import ProjectService
from backend.services.search.search_service import SymbolSearchService
from config import INDEX_DIR

router = APIRouter(prefix="/search", tags=["Search"])
project = ProjectService().get_active_project()
search_service = SymbolSearchService(INDEX_DIR / project["project_id"])


@router.get("/symbols")

    return search_service.search(q)

# FILE: .\backend\routers\task_board.py
# ========================================

from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException
from typing import List, Optional
from pydantic import BaseModel
from fastapi.responses import HTMLResponse
from pathlib import Path

from backend.services.project_service import ProjectService
from backend.services.indexing.index_service import IndexService
from backend.services.graph.call_graph_service import CallGraphService
from backend.services.analysis.crawler_review_service import CrawlerReviewService
from backend.services.task.task_generator import TaskGenerator
from backend.services.task.task_storage import TaskStorage
from backend.services.llm.ollama_client import OllamaClient
from backend.models.task import TaskStatus, TaskCategory, TaskPriority, AnalysisTask, TaskEvidence
from backend.config.task_config import TaskConfig
from backend.services.task.background_task_manager import BackgroundTaskManager
from config import DATA_DIR, INDEX_DIR

router = APIRouter(prefix="/api/task-board", tags=["Task Board"])

bg_manager = BackgroundTaskManager()

class TaskUpdateRequest(BaseModel):
    status: str
    notes: Optional[str] = None


def _get_services():
    """Helper to initialize services for current project"""
    project = ProjectService().get_active_project()
    project_id = project["project_id"]
    index_path = INDEX_DIR / project_id

    index_service = IndexService(project)
    graph_service = CallGraphService(index_path)
    crawler_service = CrawlerReviewService(index_service, graph_service)
    task_storage = TaskStorage(project_id, DATA_DIR)
    task_generator = TaskGenerator(crawler_service, graph_service, project_id)  # Added project_id

    return {
        "project": project,
        "project_id": project_id,
        "graph_service": graph_service,
        "crawler_service": crawler_service,
        "task_storage": task_storage,
        "task_generator": task_generator
    }


@router.get("/tasks")
def list_tasks(status: Optional[str] = None) -> List[dict]:
    """List all tasks, optionally filtered by status"""
    services = _get_services()
    tasks = services["task_storage"].load_tasks()

    if status:
        tasks = [t for t in tasks if t["status"] == status]

    return tasks


@router.post("/tasks/generate")
def generate_tasks() -> dict:
    """Generate new tasks from current codebase analysis"""
    services = _get_services()

    new_tasks = services["task_generator"].generate_tasks()

    existing_tasks = services["task_storage"].load_tasks()
    existing_ids = {t["id"] for t in existing_tasks}

    added = []
    for task in new_tasks:
        if task.id not in existing_ids:
            existing_tasks.append(task.to_dict())
            added.append(task.id)

    # Convert dicts back to AnalysisTask objects
    all_tasks = []
    for t_dict in existing_tasks:
        # Reconstruct evidence
        evidence_objects = []
        for e in t_dict.get("evidence", []):
            evidence_objects.append(TaskEvidence(
                symbol=e["symbol"],
                metric_type=e["metric_type"],
                metric_value=e["metric_value"],
                file_path=e["file_path"],
                line_range=e.get("line_range"),
                callers=e.get("callers", []),
                callees=e.get("callees", [])
            ))
        
        all_tasks.append(AnalysisTask(
            id=t_dict["id"],
            title=t_dict["title"],
            description=t_dict["description"],
            category=TaskCategory(t_dict["category"]),
            priority=TaskPriority(t_dict["priority"]),
            status=TaskStatus(t_dict["status"]),
            evidence=evidence_objects,
            suggested_fix=t_dict.get("suggested_fix"),
            impact_analysis=t_dict.get("impact_analysis"),
            created_at=t_dict["created_at"],
            updated_at=t_dict["updated_at"],
            notes=t_dict.get("notes")
        ))

    services["task_storage"].save_tasks(all_tasks)

    return {
        "message": f"Generated {len(added)} new tasks",
        "total_tasks": len(existing_tasks),
        "new_task_ids": added
    }


@router.get("/tasks/{task_id}")
def get_task(task_id: str) -> dict:
    """Get a single task with full details"""
    services = _get_services()
    tasks = services["task_storage"].load_tasks()

    for task in tasks:
        if task["id"] == task_id:
            return task

    raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Task not found")


@router.patch("/tasks/{task_id}")
def update_task(task_id: str, update: TaskUpdateRequest) -> dict:
    """Update task status (done/ignored/deferred/in_progress)"""
    services = _get_services()

    try:
        status = TaskStatus(update.status)
    except ValueError:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"Invalid status: {update.status}")

    success = services["task_storage"].update_task_status(task_id, status, update.notes)

    if not success:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Task not found")

    return {"message": "Task updated", "task_id": task_id, "status": update.status}


@router.get("/tasks/{task_id}/explanation")
def get_task_explanation(task_id: str) -> dict:
    """Get AI-generated impact analysis for a task"""
    services = _get_services()
    tasks = services["task_storage"].load_tasks()

    task = None
    for t in tasks:
        if t["id"] == task_id:
            task = t
            break

    if not task:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Task not found")

    evidence = task.get("evidence", [])
    if evidence:
        symbol = evidence[0].get("symbol") if isinstance(evidence[0], dict) else evidence[0].symbol
    else:
        symbol = "unknown"

    chain = services["graph_service"].get_call_chain(symbol, max_depth=2)

    llm = OllamaClient()
    prompt = f"""
You are a senior software engineer. Analyze this task and provide impact analysis.

TASK: {task.get('title')}
DESCRIPTION: {task.get('description')}

EVIDENCE:
- Symbol: {symbol}
- Metric: {evidence[0].get('metric_type') if evidence else 'N/A'}
- Value: {evidence[0].get('metric_value') if evidence else 'N/A'}

CALL CHAIN ANALYSIS:
- Callers (incoming): {chain.get('callers', [])[:10]}
- Callees (outgoing): {chain.get('callees', [])[:10]}

Provide:
1. RISK ASSESSMENT (High/Medium/Low)
2. IMPACT SCOPE (which parts of system affected)
3. RECOMMENDED APPROACH
4. ESTIMATED EFFORT (S/M/L)
"""

    analysis = llm.generate(prompt)

    return {
        "task_id": task_id,
        "impact_analysis": analysis,
        "call_chain": chain
    }


@router.get("/summary")
def get_summary() -> dict:
    """Get task board summary statistics"""
    services = _get_services()
    tasks = services["task_storage"].load_tasks()

    status_counts = {}
    priority_counts = {}
    category_counts = {}

    for task in tasks:
        status = task.get("status", "unknown")
        priority = task.get("priority", "unknown")
        category = task.get("category", "unknown")

        status_counts[status] = status_counts.get(status, 0) + 1
        priority_counts[priority] = priority_counts.get(priority, 0) + 1
        category_counts[category] = category_counts.get(category, 0) + 1

    return {
        "total_tasks": len(tasks),
        "by_status": status_counts,
        "by_priority": priority_counts,
        "by_category": category_counts
    }
    
@router.get("/ui", response_class=HTMLResponse)
def task_board_ui():
    """Serve the task board HTML interface"""
    html_path = Path("frontend/templates/task_board.html")
    if html_path.exists():
        return html_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    return "<h1>Task Board UI not found</h1>"

@router.get("/config")
def get_config(project_id: str = None) -> dict:
    """Get current task generation configuration"""
    if not project_id:
        project = ProjectService().get_active_project()
        project_id = project["project_id"]
    
    config = TaskConfig(project_id)
    return config.to_dict()


@router.put("/config")
def update_config(config_data: dict, project_id: str = None) -> dict:
    """Update task generation configuration"""
    if not project_id:
        project = ProjectService().get_active_project()
        project_id = project["project_id"]
    
    config = TaskConfig(project_id)
    
    # Filter only valid threshold keys
    valid_keys = [
        'fan_out_medium', 'fan_out_high', 'fan_out_critical',
        'fan_in_medium', 'fan_in_high', 'fan_in_critical',
        'llm_enabled', 'llm_max_tasks', 'llm_model'
    ]
    
    updates = {k: v for k, v in config_data.items() if k in valid_keys}
    config.update(updates)
    
    return config.to_dict()


@router.post("/tasks/generate-with-config")
def generate_tasks_with_config(include_llm: bool = True) -> dict:
    """Generate tasks using current configuration"""
    services = _get_services()
    
    # Recreate task generator with current config
    from backend.services.task.task_generator import TaskGenerator
    task_generator = TaskGenerator(
        services["crawler_service"], 
        services["graph_service"],
        services["project_id"]
    )
    
    new_tasks = task_generator.generate_tasks(include_llm=include_llm)
    
    existing_tasks = services["task_storage"].load_tasks()
    existing_ids = {t["id"] for t in existing_tasks}
    
    # Keep existing tasks, add only new ones
    for task in new_tasks:
        if task.id not in existing_ids:
            existing_tasks.append(task.to_dict())
    
    # Save all tasks
    all_tasks = []
    for t_dict in existing_tasks:
        evidence_objects = []
        for e in t_dict.get("evidence", []):
            from backend.models.task import TaskEvidence
            evidence_objects.append(TaskEvidence(
                symbol=e["symbol"],
                metric_type=e["metric_type"],
                metric_value=e["metric_value"],
                file_path=e["file_path"],
                line_range=e.get("line_range"),
                callers=e.get("callers", []),
                callees=e.get("callees", [])
            ))
        
        from backend.models.task import AnalysisTask, TaskCategory, TaskPriority
        all_tasks.append(AnalysisTask(
            id=t_dict["id"],
            title=t_dict["title"],
            description=t_dict["description"],
            category=TaskCategory(t_dict["category"]),
            priority=TaskPriority(t_dict["priority"]),
            status=t_dict["status"],
            evidence=evidence_objects,
            suggested_fix=t_dict.get("suggested_fix"),
            impact_analysis=t_dict.get("impact_analysis"),
            created_at=t_dict["created_at"],
            updated_at=t_dict["updated_at"],
            notes=t_dict.get("notes")
        ))
    
    services["task_storage"].save_tasks(all_tasks)
    
    rule_count = len([t for t in new_tasks if "task_coupling" in t.id or "task_usage" in t.id])
    llm_count = len([t for t in new_tasks if "task_llm" in t.id])
    
    return {
        "message": f"Generated {len(new_tasks)} new tasks",
        "rule_based_tasks": rule_count,
        "llm_discovered_tasks": llm_count,
        "total_tasks": len(existing_tasks)
    }
    

@router.post("/tasks/generate-async")
def generate_tasks_async(include_llm: bool = True) -> dict:
    """Start background task generation and return job ID"""
    project = ProjectService().get_active_project()
    project_id = project["project_id"]
    
    job_id = bg_manager.start_generation(project_id, include_llm)
    
    return {
        "job_id": job_id,
        "status": "started",
        "message": "Task generation started in background. Check /tasks/generate-status/{job_id} for progress."
    }

        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Job not found")
    
    return {
        "job_id": job["id"],
        "status": job["status"],
        "started_at": job.get("started_at"),
        "completed_at": job.get("completed_at"),
        "result": job.get("result"),
        "error": job.get("error")
    }


@router.get("/tasks/generate-active")

        "active_jobs": bg_manager.get_active_jobs()
    }
    
    
@router.post("/tasks/generate-ai-only")
def generate_ai_only_tasks() -> dict:
    """Generate ONLY AI-discovered tasks (no rule-based)"""
    services = _get_services()
    
    # Create task generator with current config
    from backend.services.task.task_generator import TaskGenerator
    task_generator = TaskGenerator(
        services["crawler_service"], 
        services["graph_service"],
        services["project_id"]
    )
    
    # Generate only AI tasks
    new_tasks = task_generator.generate_ai_only_tasks()
    
    # Load existing tasks
    existing_tasks = services["task_storage"].load_tasks()
    existing_ids = {t["id"] for t in existing_tasks}
    
    # Add only new AI tasks (don't regenerate rule-based)
    added_count = 0
    for task in new_tasks:
        if task.id not in existing_ids:
            existing_tasks.append(task.to_dict())
            added_count += 1
    
    # Save all tasks
    all_tasks = []
    for t_dict in existing_tasks:
        evidence_objects = []
        for e in t_dict.get("evidence", []):
            from backend.models.task import TaskEvidence
            evidence_objects.append(TaskEvidence(
                symbol=e["symbol"],
                metric_type=e["metric_type"],
                metric_value=e["metric_value"],
                file_path=e["file_path"],
                line_range=e.get("line_range"),
                callers=e.get("callers", []),
                callees=e.get("callees", []),
                source=e.get("source", "rule_based")
            ))
        
        from backend.models.task import AnalysisTask, TaskCategory, TaskPriority, TaskStatus
        all_tasks.append(AnalysisTask(
            id=t_dict["id"],
            title=t_dict["title"],
            description=t_dict["description"],
            category=TaskCategory(t_dict["category"]),
            priority=TaskPriority(t_dict["priority"]),
            status=TaskStatus(t_dict["status"]) if isinstance(t_dict["status"], str) else t_dict["status"],
            evidence=evidence_objects,
            suggested_fix=t_dict.get("suggested_fix"),
            impact_analysis=t_dict.get("impact_analysis"),
            created_at=t_dict["created_at"],
            updated_at=t_dict["updated_at"],
            notes=t_dict.get("notes")
        ))
    
    services["task_storage"].save_tasks(all_tasks)
    
    return {
        "message": f"Added {added_count} new AI-discovered tasks",
        "ai_tasks_generated": len(new_tasks),
        "ai_tasks_added": added_count,
        "total_tasks": len(existing_tasks)
    }


@router.post("/tasks/generate-ai-only-async")
def generate_ai_only_async() -> dict:
    """Start background generation of ONLY AI-discovered tasks"""
    project = ProjectService().get_active_project()
    project_id = project["project_id"]
    
    job_id = bg_manager.start_ai_only_generation(project_id)
    
    return {
        "job_id": job_id,
        "status": "started",
        "message": "AI-only task generation started in background. Results will be added to existing tasks."
    }

# FILE: .\backend\services\project_service.py

from pathlib import Path
import json


class ProjectService:
    def __init__(self, projects_file=None):
        if projects_file is None:
            self.projects_file = (
                Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2]
                / "data"
                / "projects.json"
            )
        else:
            self.projects_file = Path(projects_file)

        self._projects_cache = None

    def _load_projects(self):
        if self._projects_cache:
            return self._projects_cache

        if not self.projects_file.exists():
            raise FileNotFoundError("projects.json not found")

        data = json.loads(self.projects_file.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
        self._projects_cache = data["projects"]
        return self._projects_cache

    def get_project(self, project_id: str):
        projects = self._load_projects()

        for p in projects:
            if p["project_id"] == project_id:
                return p

        raise ValueError(f"Project not found: {project_id}")

    def list_projects(self):
        return self._load_projects()
    
    def get_active_project(self):
        projects = self._load_projects()

        for project in projects:
            if project.get("active", False):
                return project

        raise ValueError("No active project found in projects.json")
    
    def get_index_path_for_project(self, project_id: str = None) -> Path:
        """Get the index path for a project"""
        from config import INDEX_DIR
        
        if project_id is None:
            project = self.get_active_project()
            project_id = project["project_id"]
        
        return INDEX_DIR / project_id

# ========================================
# FILE: .\backend\services\agent\chat_engine.py
# ========================================

from backend.services.agent.intent_classifier import IntentClassifier
from backend.services.agent.entity_extractor import EntityExtractor
from backend.services.agent.execution_engine import ExecutionEngine
from backend.services.agent.conversation_memory import ConversationMemory
from backend.services.agent.reference_resolver import ReferenceResolver
from backend.services.llm.ollama_client import OllamaClient


class ChatEngine:

    def __init__(self):

        self.intent_classifier = IntentClassifier()

        self.entity_extractor = EntityExtractor()

        self.execution_engine = ExecutionEngine()

        self.memory = ConversationMemory()

        self.reference_resolver = ReferenceResolver()

        self.llm = OllamaClient(
            model="qwen2.5-coder:3b"
        )

    def chat(
        self,
        question: str
    ):

        # ---------------------------------
        # Store user message
        # ---------------------------------

        self.memory.remember(
            role="user",
            content=question
        )

        intent = self.intent_classifier.classify(
            question
        )

        extracted_symbol = self.entity_extractor.extract_symbol(
            question
        )

        if extracted_symbol:

            symbol = extracted_symbol

        else:

            if self.reference_resolver.should_use_memory(
                question
            ):

                symbol = self.memory.get_last_symbol()

            else:

                symbol = None

        print("=" * 60)
        print("Question:", question)
        print("Resolved Symbol:", symbol)
        print("=" * 60)

        # ---------------------------------
        # General chat
        # ---------------------------------

        if symbol is None:

            prompt = f"""
You are an expert software engineering assistant.

Question:

{question}
"""

            answer = self.llm.generate(prompt)

            self.memory.remember(
                role="assistant",
                content=answer
            )

            return {

                "question": question,

                "intent": "general_chat",

                "symbol": None,

                "answer": answer

            }

        # ---------------------------------
        # Project-aware execution
        # ---------------------------------

        result = self.execution_engine.execute(

            intent=intent,

            symbol=symbol,

            question=question,

            history=self.memory.get_recent_history()

        )

        self.memory.remember(

            role="assistant",

            content=result.get("answer"),

            symbol=result.get("symbol"),

            intent=result.get("intent")

        )

        return {

            "question": question,

            "intent": result.get("intent"),

            "symbol": result.get("symbol"),

            "answer": result.get("answer"),

            "context_used": result.get("context_used"),

            "metrics": result.get("metrics")

        }

# ========================================
# FILE: .\backend\services\agent\context_compressor.py
# ========================================

class ContextCompressor:

    def compress(self, context: dict, intent: str):

        compressed = dict(context)

        if intent == "explain_symbol":
            compressed["calls"] = context.get("calls", [])[:20]
            compressed["related_symbols"] = context.get("related_symbols", [])[:10]

            reasoning = context.get("reasoning", {})

            compressed["reasoning"] = {
                "callers_chain": reasoning.get("callers_chain", [])[:5],
                "callees_chain": reasoning.get("callees_chain", [])[:5],
            }

        elif intent == "find_callers":

            compressed = {
                "symbol": context.get("symbol"),
                "called_by": context.get("called_by", []),
                "reasoning": context.get("reasoning", {}),
            }

        return compressed

# ========================================
# FILE: .\backend\services\agent\conversation_memory.py
# ========================================

from collections import deque


class ConversationMemory:

    def __init__(self, max_messages=20):

        self.max_messages = max_messages

        self.messages = deque(maxlen=max_messages)

        self.last_symbol = None

        self.last_intent = None

    def remember(
        self,
        role: str,
        content: str,
        symbol=None,
        intent=None
    ):

        self.messages.append({

            "role": role,

            "content": content

        })

        if symbol:

            self.last_symbol = symbol

        if intent:

            self.last_intent = intent

    def get_last_symbol(self):

        return self.last_symbol

    def get_last_intent(self):

        return self.last_intent

    def get_recent_history(
        self,
        limit=6
    ):

        return list(self.messages)[-limit:]

    def clear(self):

        self.messages.clear()

        self.last_symbol = None

        self.last_intent = None

# ========================================
# FILE: .\backend\services\agent\entity_extractor.py
# ========================================

import re

from backend.services.project_service import ProjectService
from config import INDEX_DIR
from backend.services.agent.symbol_resolver import SymbolResolver


class EntityExtractor:

    def __init__(self):
        project = ProjectService().get_active_project()
        self.resolver = SymbolResolver(
            INDEX_DIR / project["project_id"]
        )

    def extract_symbol(
        self,
        question: str
    ):

        patterns = [
            r"where\s+is\s+([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*)\(?\)?\s+called",
            r"who\s+calls\s+([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*)",
            r"explain\s+([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*)",
            r"what\s+does\s+([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*)",
            r"can\s+i\s+delete\s+([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*)",
            r"safe\s+to\s+remove\s+([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*)"
        ]

        candidate = None

        for pattern in patterns:

            match = re.search(
                pattern,
                question,
                re.IGNORECASE
            )

            if match:

                candidate = match.group(1)

                break

        # -------------------------
        # Regex match succeeded
        # -------------------------

        if candidate:

            resolved = self.resolver.resolve(
                candidate
            )

            if resolved:

                return resolved

        # -------------------------
        # Fallback scan
        # -------------------------

        return self.resolver.resolve_from_text(
            question
        )

# ========================================
# FILE: .\backend\services\agent\execution_engine.py
# ========================================

from backend.services.context.context_builder import ContextBuilder
from backend.services.llm.ollama_client import OllamaClient
from backend.services.agent.prompt_builder import PromptBuilder
from backend.services.agent.reasoning_engine import ReasoningEngine
from backend.services.graph.call_graph_service import CallGraphService
from backend.services.cache.context_cache import ContextCache
from backend.services.agent.context_compressor import ContextCompressor
from backend.services.project_service import ProjectService
from config import INDEX_DIR
import time


class ExecutionEngine:

    def __init__(self):
        project = ProjectService().get_active_project()
        self.context_builder = ContextBuilder(INDEX_DIR / project["project_id"])
        self.graph_service = CallGraphService(INDEX_DIR / project["project_id"])
        self.prompt_builder = PromptBuilder()
        # self.llm = OllamaClient(model="qwen2.5-coder:7b")
        self.llm = OllamaClient(model="qwen2.5-coder:3b")
        self.reasoning_engine = ReasoningEngine(self.graph_service)
        self.cache = ContextCache(ttl_seconds=300)
        self.compressor = ContextCompressor()
        

    def execute(self, intent: str, symbol: str, question: str = None, history=None):
        start = time.perf_counter()

        # 1. Build cached context
        cache_key = f"{intent}:{symbol}"

        context = self.cache.get(cache_key)

        if context is None:
            context = self.context_builder.build(
                symbol_name=symbol,
                intent=intent
            )

            if context is not None:
                self.cache.set(cache_key, context)

        if context is None:
            return {
                "error": "Symbol not found"
            }

        print("=" * 60)
        print("Intent:", intent)
        print("Context keys:", list(context.keys()))
        print(
            "Context chars:",
            len(str(context))
        )
        print("=" * 60)
        
        t1 = time.perf_counter()
        print(f"Context: {t1 - start:.3f}s")

        reasoning_key = f"reasoning:{symbol}"

        reasoning_context = self.cache.get(reasoning_key)
        if not reasoning_context:
            reasoning_context = self.reasoning_engine.build_reasoning_context(symbol)
            self.cache.set(reasoning_key, reasoning_context)
            
        t2 = time.perf_counter()
        print(f"Reasoning: {t2 - t1:.3f}s")

        context = {
            **context,
            "reasoning": reasoning_context
        }

        # 2. FAST PATH (NO LLM)
        if intent == "find_callers":
            return {
                "symbol": symbol,
                "intent": intent,
                "answer": context.get("called_by", []),
                "context_used": context
            }

        # 3. LLM PATH
        compressed_context = self.compressor.compress(
            context=context,
            intent=intent
        )
        
        prompt = self.prompt_builder.build(
            intent=intent,
            symbol_data=compressed_context,
            question=question,
            history=history or []
        )
        print("=" * 60)
        print("Prompt length:", len(prompt))
        print("Compressed context chars:", len(str(compressed_context)))
        print("=" * 60)
        
        t3 = time.perf_counter()
        print(f"Prompt: {t3 - t2:.3f}s")

        response = self.llm.generate(prompt)

        t4 = time.perf_counter()

        print(f"LLM: {t4 - t3:.3f}s")
        print(f"TOTAL: {t4 - start:.3f}s")
        print("=" * 60)

        return {
            "symbol": symbol,
            "intent": intent,
            "answer": response,
            "context_used": compressed_context,
            "metrics": {
                "context_ms": round((t1 - start) * 1000, 1),
                "reasoning_ms": round((t2 - t1) * 1000, 1),
                "prompt_ms": round((t3 - t2) * 1000, 1),
                "llm_ms": round((t4 - t3) * 1000, 1),
                "total_ms": round((t4 - start) * 1000, 1),
                "context_chars": len(str(context)),
                "prompt_chars": len(prompt),
                "model": "qwen2.5-coder:3b"
            }
        }

# FILE: .\backend\services\agent\intent_classifier.py
# ========================================

import re

from backend.services.agent.query_models import Intent


class IntentClassifier:

    def classify(self, question: str):

        q = question.lower().strip()

        # -----------------------------------
        # Find Callers
        # -----------------------------------

        caller_patterns = [

            r"where.*called",
            r"who.*calls",
            r"called by",
            r"find callers?",
            r"show callers?",
            r"list callers?"

        ]

        for pattern in caller_patterns:

            if re.search(pattern, q):

                return Intent.FIND_CALLERS

        # -----------------------------------
        # Dependency Analysis
        # -----------------------------------

        dependency_patterns = [

            r"depends on",
            r"\buses\b",
            r"\breferences\b",
            r"what.*uses",
            r"what.*references",
            r"dependencies?",
            r"external dependencies?"

        ]

        for pattern in dependency_patterns:

            if re.search(pattern, q):

                return Intent.DEPENDENCY_ANALYSIS

        # -----------------------------------
        # Impact Analysis
        # -----------------------------------

        impact_patterns = [

            r"can.*delete",
            r"safe.*remove",
            r"safe.*delete",
            r"should.*remove",
            r"should.*delete",
            r"can.*refactor",
            r"safe.*modify",
            r"what.*depends",
            r"impact",
            r"what.*break",
            r"what happens if",
            r"remove.*will",
            r"delete.*will"

        ]

        for pattern in impact_patterns:

            if re.search(pattern, q):

                return Intent.IMPACT_ANALYSIS

        # -----------------------------------
        # Explain Symbol
        # -----------------------------------

        explain_patterns = [

            r"what.*does",
            r"explain",
            r"describe",
            r"summarize",
            r"tell me about",
            r"walk me through",
            r"overview",
            r"give me an overview",
            r"how.*works",
            r"how.*implemented",
            r"how.*written",
            r"how.*designed",
            r"purpose of",
            r"what is",
            r"why.*exist",
            r"why.*used"

        ]

        for pattern in explain_patterns:

            if re.search(pattern, q):

                return Intent.EXPLAIN_SYMBOL

        # -----------------------------------
        # Unknown
        # -----------------------------------

        return Intent.UNKNOWN

# ========================================
# FILE: .\backend\services\agent\prompt_builder.py
# ========================================

from typing import Dict, Any, List
from backend.services.agent.prompt_templates.registry import PromptRegistry


class PromptBuilder:
    """
    Central prompt construction layer for the agent.
    """

    def __init__(self):
        pass

    def build(
        self,
        intent: str,
        crawler_review_data: Dict[str, Any],
        question: str,
        history: List[Dict[str, str]] = None
    ) -> str:

        template = PromptRegistry.get(intent)

        base_instructions = self._system_instructions()

        # ---------------------------
        # TEMPLATE HANDLING (NEW CORE LOGIC)
        # ---------------------------

        if template:
            system_block = template.system()
            task_block = template.task()
            format_block = template.output_format()
        else:
            system_block = base_instructions
            task_block = self._fallback_task(intent)
            format_block = ""

        history_block = self._build_history(history or [])

        context_block = self._build_context(crawler_review_data)

        return f"""
{system_block}

{task_block}

{format_block}

# RECENT CONVERSATION

{history_block}

# CURRENT USER QUESTION

{question}

# CODE CONTEXT

{context_block}

# IMPORTANT RULES

- The recent conversation is additional context.
- The current user question has highest priority.
- Use the conversation history to resolve references like:
    - it
    - this
    - that method
    - summarize it
    - explain further
    - make it shorter
- Never invent symbols.
- Only use symbols present in the supplied context.
- If uncertain, say "unknown from context".
"""

    # -------------------------------------------------

    def _system_instructions(self):

        return """
You are a senior software engineering assistant.

You help developers understand a local codebase.

You are a reasoning engine.

You do not invent APIs or functions.

You answer only from supplied context.
"""

    # -------------------------------------------------

    def _fallback_task(self, intent: str):

        if str(intent) == "explain_symbol":

            return "TASK: Explain the requested symbol."

        if str(intent) == "find_callers":

            return "TASK: Identify callers and call chains."

        if str(intent) == "impact_analysis":

            return """
TASK: Assess modification or deletion impact.
Include callers, dependencies, and risks.
"""

        if str(intent) == "dependency_analysis":

            return """
TASK: Analyze dependencies (incoming and outgoing).
"""

        if str(intent) == "codebase_review":
            return """
    TASK: Review codebase structure and suggest improvements.
    Focus on architecture, design, and maintainability.
    """

        return "TASK: General code analysis."

    # -------------------------------------------------

    def _build_history(
        self,
        history
    ):

        if not history:
            return "No previous conversation."

        lines = []

        for item in history:

            role = item.get("role", "unknown")
            content = item.get("content", "")

            lines.append(f"{role.upper()}: {content}")

        return "\n\n".join(lines)

    # -------------------------------------------------

    def _build_context(
        self,
        symbol_data
    ):

        if not symbol_data:
            return "No symbol context found."

        lines = []

        lines.append(f"Symbol: {symbol_data.get('symbol')}")
        lines.append(f"Type: {symbol_data.get('type')}")
        lines.append(f"File: {symbol_data.get('file')}")
        lines.append(f"Parent: {symbol_data.get('parent')}")

        calls = symbol_data.get("calls", [])
        if calls:
            lines.append("\nDirect Calls:")
            lines.append(", ".join(calls[:20]))

        related = symbol_data.get("related_symbols", [])
        if related:
            lines.append("\nRelated Symbols:")
            lines.append(", ".join(related[:10]))

        callers = symbol_data.get("called_by", [])
        if callers:
            lines.append("\nCalled By:")
            for caller in callers[:10]:
                lines.append(str(caller))

        reasoning = symbol_data.get("reasoning", {})
        if reasoning:
            lines.append("\nReasoning:")

            for item in reasoning.get("callers_chain", [])[:10]:
                lines.append(f"{item['from']} -> {item['to']}")

            for item in reasoning.get("callees_chain", [])[:10]:
                lines.append(f"{item['from']} -> {item['to']}")

        return "\n".join(lines)

from enum import Enum


class Intent(Enum):

    EXPLAIN_SYMBOL = "explain_symbol"

    FIND_CALLERS = "find_callers"

    FIND_CALLEES = "find_callees"

    IMPACT_ANALYSIS = "impact_analysis"

    FIND_FILE = "find_file"
    
    DEPENDENCY_ANALYSIS = "dependency_analysis"

    UNKNOWN = "unknown"

# ========================================
# FILE: .\backend\services\agent\query_router.py
# ========================================

class QueryRouter:

    def route(self, intent, symbol):

        if intent.value == "find_callers":
            return {
                "action": "call_graph.get_dependents",
                "symbol": symbol
            }

        if intent.value == "find_callees":
            return {
                "action": "call_graph.get_dependencies",
                "symbol": symbol
            }

        if intent.value == "explain_symbol":
            return {
                "action": "context_builder.build",
                "symbol": symbol
            }

        return None

# ========================================
# FILE: .\backend\services\agent\reasoning_engine.py
# ========================================

from collections import deque


class ReasoningEngine:
    """
    Expands symbol context using call graph relationships.
    Enables multi-hop reasoning for debugging questions.
    """

    def __init__(self, graph_service):
        self.graph = graph_service

    def build_reasoning_context(self, symbol: str, max_depth: int = 2):
        """
        Expands:
        - callers
        - callees
        - indirect chains
        """

        visited = set()
        queue = deque([(symbol, 0)])

        callers_map = self.graph.build_graph().get("called_by", {})
        calls_map = self.graph.build_graph().get("calls", {})

        result = {
            "root": symbol,
            "callers_chain": [],
            "callees_chain": []
        }

        while queue:
            node, depth = queue.popleft()

            if node in visited or depth > max_depth:
                continue

            visited.add(node)

            # callers
            for caller in callers_map.get(node, []):
                result["callers_chain"].append({
                    "from": caller,
                    "to": node,
                    "depth": depth + 1
                })
                queue.append((caller, depth + 1))

            # callees
            for callee in calls_map.get(node, []):
                result["callees_chain"].append({
                    "from": node,
                    "to": callee,
                    "depth": depth + 1
                })
                queue.append((callee, depth + 1))

        return result

# ========================================
# FILE: .\backend\services\agent\reference_resolver.py
# ========================================

import re


class ReferenceResolver:

    def __init__(self):

        self.reference_patterns = [

            r"\bit\b",
            r"\bthis\b",
            r"\bthat\b",
            r"\bthis method\b",
            r"\bthat method\b",
            r"\bthis function\b",
            r"\bthat function\b",
            r"\bthis class\b",
            r"\bthat class\b",
            r"\bthe method\b",
            r"\bthe function\b",
            r"\bthe class\b"

        ]

    def should_use_memory(
        self,
        question: str
    ):

        q = question.lower()

        for pattern in self.reference_patterns:

            if re.search(pattern, q):
                return True

        return False

# ========================================
# FILE: .\backend\services\agent\symbol_resolver.py
# ========================================

import json
import re
from pathlib import Path


class SymbolResolver:

    def __init__(self, index_path: Path):

        self.index_path = Path(index_path)

        self.symbols = self._load_symbols()

    def _load_symbols(self):

        file = self.index_path / "symbols.json"

        if not file.exists():
            return []

        return json.loads(
            file.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
        )

    def resolve(self, candidate: str):

        if not candidate:
            return None

        candidate = candidate.lower().strip()

        # Exact match

        for symbol in self.symbols:

            if symbol["name"].lower() == candidate:
                return symbol["name"]

        # Ignore spaces

        normalized = candidate.replace(" ", "_")

        for symbol in self.symbols:

            if symbol["name"].lower() == normalized:
                return symbol["name"]

        # Ignore underscores

        normalized = normalized.replace("_", "")

        for symbol in self.symbols:

            if symbol["name"].lower().replace("_", "") == normalized:
                return symbol["name"]

        return None

    def resolve_from_text(self, text: str):

        """
        Fallback scan.

        Looks through every word in the sentence
        and attempts to resolve it as a project symbol.
        """

        tokens = re.findall(
            r"[A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*",
            text
        )

        for token in tokens:

            resolved = self.resolve(token)

            if resolved:

                return resolved

        return None

        return ""

from .base import BasePromptTemplate


class CodebaseReviewTemplate(BasePromptTemplate):

    def system(self):
        return """
You are a senior software architect and code reviewer.

You analyze codebases for:
- design issues
- performance issues
- coupling problems
- missing abstractions
- maintainability risks

You are strict, practical, and opinionated.

You do NOT invent code that is not in context.
"""

    def task(self):
        return """
TASK:

Focus on:

1. Architecture issues
2. Function/class design problems
3. Unnecessary complexity
4. Tight coupling or bad dependencies
5. Missing abstractions
6. Performance concerns
7. Maintainability risks

Be specific. Reference actual symbols from context.
"""

    def output_format(self):
        return """
## Summary

## Architecture Observations

## Code Quality Issues

## Design Improvements

## Refactoring Suggestions

## Risk Assessment

## Priority Fix List
"""
