        """Return error analysis result"""
        return ImpactAnalysis(
            impact_level=ImpactLevel.CRITICAL,
            affected_files=[],
            affected_callers=[],
            total_callers=0,
            breaking_changes=True,
            warnings=[error_message],
            suggestions=["Verify function name and try again"],
            complexity_score=1.0
        )


# Add helper method to FunctionDetail (in your models/refactor.py)
def _add_is_public_api_method():
    """Monkey patch for FunctionDetail to add is_public_api method"""
    def is_public_api(self) -> bool:
        """Check if function is likely a public API"""
        # Not starting with underscore (unless it's __init__ etc)
        if self.name.startswith('_') and not self.name.startswith('__'):
            return False
        # Has docstring
        if self.docstring:
            return True
        # Is a method without underscore prefix
        return not self.name.startswith('_')
    
    # Add method to FunctionDetail if not exists
    if not hasattr(FunctionDetail, 'is_public_api'):
        FunctionDetail.is_public_api = is_public_api_method

# ========================================
# FILE: .\backend\services\refactor\llm_refactor_engine.py
# ========================================

# backend/services/refactor/llm_refactor_engine.py

import json
import re
from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional
from pathlib import Path

from backend.models.refactor import (
    RefactorType, Parameter, CallSite, FunctionDetail,
    FileChange, ChangeType, RefactoringPlan
)
from backend.services.refactor.code_analyzer import CodeAnalyzer
from backend.services.refactor.impact_scanner import ImpactScanner
from backend.services.llm.ollama_client import OllamaClient


class LLMRefactorEngine:
    
    def __init__(self, project_id: str = None):
        self.analyzer = CodeAnalyzer(project_id)
        self.scanner = ImpactScanner(project_id)
        self.llm = OllamaClient(model="qwen2.5-coder:3b")
    
    def generate_extract_method(
            self,
            function_name: str,
            start_line: int,
            end_line: int,
            new_method_name: str
        ) -> Optional[RefactoringPlan]:
    
        func_detail = self.analyzer.get_function_detail(function_name)
        if not func_detail:
            raise ValueError(f"Function '{function_name}' not found")
        
        # FIXED: Compare with function's actual line range, not source code length
        if start_line < func_detail.line_start or end_line > func_detail.line_end:
            raise ValueError(f"Invalid line range: {start_line}-{end_line}. Function spans lines {func_detail.line_start}-{func_detail.line_end}")
        
        if start_line >= end_line:
            raise ValueError(f"Start line {start_line} must be less than end line {end_line}")
        
        # Extract the code block using line numbers (not array indices)
        lines = func_detail.source_code.split('\n')
        start_idx = start_line - func_detail.line_start
        end_idx = end_line - func_detail.line_start
        
        block_lines = lines[start_idx:end_idx]
        block_code = '\n'.join(block_lines)
        context_before = '\n'.join(lines[:start_line - 1])[-500:]
        context_after = '\n'.join(lines[end_line:])[:500]
        
        prompt = self._build_extract_prompt(
            func_detail, block_code, context_before, context_after, 
            new_method_name, start_line, end_line
        )
        
        response = self.llm.generate(prompt)
        changes = self._parse_extract_response(response, func_detail, new_method_name)
        
        if not changes:
            return None
        
        return RefactoringPlan(
            id=f"extract_{function_name}_{start_line}_{end_line}",
            target_function=function_name,
            refactor_type=RefactorType.EXTRACT_METHOD,
            changes=changes,
            affected_files=list(set([c.file_path for c in changes])),
            confidence=0.7,
            requires_review=True,
            warning="Extract method changes logic - review carefully"
        )
    
    def generate_inline_function(self, function_name: str) -> Optional[RefactoringPlan]:
        
        func_detail = self.analyzer.get_function_detail(function_name)
        if not func_detail:
            raise ValueError(f"Function '{function_name}' not found")
        
        if len(func_detail.callers) == 0:
            raise ValueError(f"Function '{function_name}' has no callers to inline")
        
        prompt = self._build_inline_prompt(func_detail)
        response = self.llm.generate(prompt)
        changes = self._parse_inline_response(response, func_detail)
        
        if not changes:
            return None
        
        return RefactoringPlan(
            id=f"inline_{function_name}",
            target_function=function_name,
            refactor_type=RefactorType.INLINE_FUNCTION,
            changes=changes,
            affected_files=list(set([c.file_path for c in changes])),
            confidence=0.6,
            requires_review=True,
            warning="Inlining function changes call sites significantly - test thoroughly"
        )
    
    def suggest_refactorings(self, function_name: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        
        func_detail = self.analyzer.get_function_detail(function_name)
        if not func_detail:
            raise ValueError(f"Function '{function_name}' not found")
        
        prompt = self._build_suggest_prompt(func_detail)
        response = self.llm.generate(prompt)
        
        try:
            json_match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', response, re.DOTALL)
            if json_match:
                suggestions = json.loads(json_match.group(0))
                return suggestions.get('suggestions', [])
        except:
            pass
        
        return []
    
    def _build_extract_prompt(self, func_detail, block_code, context_before, context_after, new_method_name, start_line, end_line):
        prompt = 'You are refactoring Python code to extract a block into a new method.\n\n'
        prompt += f'TASK: Extract Method\n'
        prompt += f'SOURCE FUNCTION: {func_detail.name}\n'
        prompt += f'FILE: {func_detail.file_path}\n'
        prompt += f'CLASS: {func_detail.class_name or "Not in a class"}\n'
        prompt += f'LINES TO EXTRACT: {start_line}-{end_line}\n'
        prompt += f'NEW METHOD NAME: {new_method_name}\n\n'
        prompt += 'Return ONLY valid JSON. Do not include any other text.\n'
        prompt += 'IMPORTANT: In the "code" fields, escape all double quotes with backslash.\n'
        prompt += 'Example: "code": "def function():\\n    print(\\"hello\\")"\n\n'
        prompt += 'JSON structure:\n'
        prompt += '{\n'
        prompt += '  "new_method": {\n'
        prompt += '    "code": "def ' + new_method_name + '(self):\\n    pass",\n'
        prompt += '    "insert_at_line": ' + str(func_detail.line_end + 1) + ',\n'
        prompt += '    "parameters": [],\n'
        prompt += '    "return_value": "None"\n'
        prompt += '  },\n'
        prompt += '  "modified_function": {\n'
        prompt += '    "code": "async def ' + func_detail.name + '(self, start_url, worker_thread, crawl_mode=\\"Single Page\\", guest_mode=False):\\n    # call new method\\n    pass",\n'
        prompt += '    "line_start": ' + str(func_detail.line_start) + ',\n'
        prompt += '    "line_end": ' + str(func_detail.line_end) + '\n'
        prompt += '  }\n'
        prompt += '}\n'
        return prompt
    
    
    def _build_inline_prompt(self, func_detail):
        prompt = 'You are refactoring Python code to inline a function.\n\n'
        prompt += f'TASK: Inline Function\n'
        prompt += f'TARGET FUNCTION: {func_detail.name}\n'
        prompt += f'FILE: {func_detail.file_path}\n'
        prompt += f'CLASS: {func_detail.class_name or "Not in a class"}\n'
        prompt += f'CALLERS: {len(func_detail.callers)} total\n\n'
        prompt += 'FUNCTION TO INLINE:\n'
        prompt += f'```python\n{func_detail.source_code}\n```\n\n'
        prompt += 'EXAMPLE CALLERS (first 3 of ' + str(len(func_detail.callers)) + '):\n'
        
        for caller in func_detail.callers[:3]:
            prompt += f'\nCaller: {caller.calling_function}\n'
            prompt += f'File: {caller.file_path}:{caller.line_number}\n'
            prompt += f'Call line: {caller.source_line}\n'
            prompt += f'Arguments: {caller.arguments}\n'
        
        prompt += '\nReturn JSON with exactly this structure:\n'
        prompt += '{\n'
        prompt += '  "caller_changes": [\n'
        prompt += '    {\n'
        prompt += '      "file": "path/to/file.py",\n'
        prompt += '      "line_start": 128,\n'
        prompt += '      "line_end": 128,\n'
        prompt += f'      "before": "result = {func_detail.name}(url, mode)",\n'
        prompt += '      "after": "# Inlined code\\n    result = processed_data",\n'
        prompt += '      "new_variables": ["temp_result"]\n'
        prompt += '    }\n'
        prompt += '  ],\n'
        prompt += '  "remove_function": true,\n'
        prompt += f'  "function_definition_file": "{func_detail.file_path}",\n'
        prompt += f'  "function_line_start": {func_detail.line_start},\n'
        prompt += f'  "function_line_end": {func_detail.line_end}\n'
        prompt += '}\n\n'
        prompt += 'Only return valid JSON, no other text.'
        return prompt
    
    def _build_suggest_prompt(self, func_detail):
        prompt = 'Analyze this Python function and suggest refactorings.\n\n'
        prompt += f'Function name: {func_detail.name}\n'
        prompt += f'Parameters: {[p.name for p in func_detail.parameters]}\n'
        prompt += f'Number of callers: {len(func_detail.callers)}\n'
        prompt += f'Lines of code: {len(func_detail.source_code.split(chr(10)))}\n\n'
        prompt += 'Source code:\n'
        prompt += '```\n'
        prompt += func_detail.source_code[:1000]
        prompt += '\n```\n\n'
        prompt += 'Return ONLY valid JSON. Example format:\n'
        prompt += '{"suggestions": [{"type": "extract_method", "reason": "...", "affected_lines": "10-20", "difficulty": "Easy", "suggested_name": "_helper"}]}\n'
        return prompt
    
    
    def _parse_extract_response(self, response: str, func_detail: FunctionDetail, new_method_name: str) -> List[FileChange]:
    
        changes = []
        
        try:
            # Clean the response - remove markdown code blocks
            cleaned = response.strip()
            
            # Remove markdown code blocks
            if cleaned.startswith('```json'):
                cleaned = cleaned[7:]
            if cleaned.startswith('```'):
                cleaned = cleaned[3:]
            if cleaned.endswith('```'):
                cleaned = cleaned[:-3]
            
            cleaned = cleaned.strip()
            
            # Find JSON object
            json_match = re.search(r'\{[\s\S]*\}', cleaned)
            if not json_match:
                print(f"[LLMRefactor] No JSON found in response")
                return []
            
            json_str = json_match.group(0)
            
            # Fix common JSON issues in the code field
            # The code field contains unescaped quotes - we need to extract and fix it
            
            # Method 1: Extract code field separately and re-insert escaped
            code_match = re.search(r'"code":\s*"([^"]*(?:\\.[^"]*)*)"', json_str, re.DOTALL)
            if not code_match:
                # Try alternative approach - find the code field with line breaks
                code_pattern = r'"code":\s*"((?:[^"\\]|\\.)*)"'
                code_match = re.search(code_pattern, json_str, re.DOTALL)
            
            if code_match:
                # Extract the code content
                code_content = code_match.group(1)
                # Escape any problematic characters
                code_content = code_content.replace('\n', '\\n')
                code_content = code_content.replace('"', '\\"')
                # Replace in original string
                json_str = json_str[:code_match.start(1)] + code_content + json_str[code_match.end(1):]
            
            # Now try to parse JSON
            try:
                data = json.loads(json_str)
            except json.JSONDecodeError:
                # If still failing, try a more aggressive approach - extract using regex
                data = {}
                
                # Extract new_method
                new_method_match = re.search(r'"new_method":\s*\{([^}]*)\}', json_str, re.DOTALL)
                if new_method_match:
                    new_method_str = new_method_match.group(1)
                    
                    # Extract code
                    code_match = re.search(r'"code":\s*"([^"]*)"', new_method_str)
                    code = code_match.group(1) if code_match else ""
                    code = code.replace('\\n', '\n').replace('\\"', '"')
                    
                    # Extract insert_at_line
                    line_match = re.search(r'"insert_at_line":\s*(\d+)', new_method_str)
                    insert_line = int(line_match.group(1)) if line_match else func_detail.line_end + 1
                    
                    data['new_method'] = {
                        'code': code,
                        'insert_at_line': insert_line,
                        'parameters': [],
                        'return_value': 'None'
                    }
                
                # Extract modified_function
                mod_func_match = re.search(r'"modified_function":\s*\{([^}]*)\}', json_str, re.DOTALL)
                if mod_func_match:
                    mod_func_str = mod_func_match.group(1)
                    
                    # Extract code
                    code_match = re.search(r'"code":\s*"([^"]*)"', mod_func_str)
                    code = code_match.group(1) if code_match else func_detail.source_code
                    code = code.replace('\\n', '\n').replace('\\"', '"')
                    
                    # Extract line numbers
                    start_match = re.search(r'"line_start":\s*(\d+)', mod_func_str)
                    end_match = re.search(r'"line_end":\s*(\d+)', mod_func_str)
                    
                    data['modified_function'] = {
                        'code': code,
                        'line_start': int(start_match.group(1)) if start_match else func_detail.line_start,
                        'line_end': int(end_match.group(1)) if end_match else func_detail.line_end
                    }
            
            # Create changes from parsed data
            if 'modified_function' in data:
                mod_func = data['modified_function']
                new_code = mod_func.get('code', '')
                if new_code and new_code != func_detail.source_code:
                    changes.append(FileChange(
                        file_path=func_detail.file_path,
                        line_start=mod_func.get('line_start', func_detail.line_start),
                        line_end=mod_func.get('line_end', func_detail.line_end),
                        before=func_detail.source_code,
                        after=new_code,
                        change_type=ChangeType.FUNCTION_DEFINITION,
                        description=f"Extract block to '{new_method_name}' method"
                    ))
            
            if 'new_method' in data:
                new_method = data['new_method']
                new_code = new_method.get('code', '')
                if new_code:
                    insert_line = new_method.get('insert_at_line', func_detail.line_end + 1)
                    changes.append(FileChange(
                        file_path=func_detail.file_path,
                        line_start=insert_line,
                        line_end=insert_line,
                        before="",
                        after=f"\n{new_code}\n",
                        change_type=ChangeType.FUNCTION_DEFINITION,
                        description=f"Add new method '{new_method_name}'"
                    ))
            
            if not changes:
                print(f"[LLMRefactor] No valid changes extracted")
                
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[LLMRefactor] Parse error: {e}")
        
        return changes
    
    
    def _parse_inline_response(self, response: str, func_detail: FunctionDetail) -> List[FileChange]:
    
        changes = []
        
        try:
            # Try to find JSON in response - LLM might add extra text
            json_match = re.search(r'\{[\s\S]*\}', response)
            if not json_match:
                print(f"[LLMRefactor] No JSON found in response")
                print(f"Response preview: {response[:200]}")
                return []
            
            data = json.loads(json_match.group(0))
            
            # Process caller changes
            for caller_change in data.get('caller_changes', []):
                # Get the actual caller info
                for caller in func_detail.callers:
                    if caller.calling_function in caller_change.get('file', ''):
                        changes.append(FileChange(
                            file_path=caller.file_path,
                            line_start=caller.line_number,
                            line_end=caller.line_number,
                            before=caller.source_line,
                            after=caller_change.get('after', '# Inlined code'),
                            change_type=ChangeType.CALLER_UPDATE,
                            description=f"Inline call to '{func_detail.name}'"
                        ))
                        break
                else:
                    # Fallback: use provided values
                    changes.append(FileChange(
                        file_path=caller_change.get('file', func_detail.file_path),
                        line_start=caller_change.get('line_start', 1),
                        line_end=caller_change.get('line_end', 1),
                        before=caller_change.get('before', ''),
                        after=caller_change.get('after', ''),
                        change_type=ChangeType.CALLER_UPDATE,
                        description=f"Inline call to '{func_detail.name}'"
                    ))
            
            # Remove the function definition
            if data.get('remove_function', True):
                changes.append(FileChange(
                    file_path=func_detail.file_path,
                    line_start=func_detail.line_start,
                    line_end=func_detail.line_end,
                    before=func_detail.source_code,
                    after=f"# Function '{func_detail.name}' was inlined and removed",
                    change_type=ChangeType.FUNCTION_DEFINITION,
                    description=f"Remove inlined function '{func_detail.name}'"
                ))
            
        except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
            print(f"[LLMRefactor] JSON parse error: {e}")
            print(f"Attempted to parse: {response[:500]}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[LLMRefactor] Parse error: {e}")
        
        return changes

# ========================================
# FILE: .\backend\services\search\search_service.py
# ========================================

import json
from pathlib import Path


class SymbolSearchService:
    def __init__(self, index_path: str):
        self.index_path = Path(index_path)
        self.symbols = self._load_symbols()

    def _load_symbols(self):
        symbols_file = self.index_path / "symbols.json"

        if not symbols_file.exists():
            return []

        return json.loads(symbols_file.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))

    def search(self, query: str):
        query = query.lower().strip()

        results = []

        for sym in self.symbols:
            name = sym.get("name", "").lower()
            sym_type = sym.get("type", "").lower()

            # MATCH RULES
            if query in name:
                results.append(sym)
                continue

            if query == sym_type:
                results.append(sym)
                continue

        return {
            "query": query,
            "count": len(results),
            "results": results
        }

    def search_by_type(self, symbol_type: str):
        symbol_type = symbol_type.lower()

        return [
            s for s in self.symbols
            if s.get("type", "").lower() == symbol_type
        ]

# ========================================
# FILE: .\backend\services\task\background_task_manager.py
# ========================================

import threading
from typing import Dict, Optional, List
from datetime import datetime
import uuid

from backend.services.task.task_generator import TaskGenerator
from backend.services.task.task_storage import TaskStorage
from backend.services.analysis.crawler_review_service import CrawlerReviewService
from backend.services.graph.call_graph_service import CallGraphService
from backend.services.indexing.index_service import IndexService
from backend.config.task_config import TaskConfig
from backend.models.task import AnalysisTask
from config import DATA_DIR, INDEX_DIR


class BackgroundTaskManager:
    """Manages background task generation to prevent UI timeout"""
    
    _instance = None
    _jobs: Dict[str, Dict] = {}
    
    def __new__(cls):
        if cls._instance is None:
            cls._instance = super().__new__(cls)
            cls._instance._jobs = {}
        return cls._instance
    
    def start_generation(self, project_id: str, include_llm: bool = True) -> str:
        """Start background task generation and return job ID"""
        
        job_id = str(uuid.uuid4())[:8]
        
        self._jobs[job_id] = {
            "id": job_id,
            "project_id": project_id,
            "include_llm": include_llm,
            "status": "running",
            "started_at": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "completed_at": None,
            "result": None,
            "error": None
        }
        
        # Start background thread
        thread = threading.Thread(
            target=self._run_generation,
            args=(job_id, project_id, include_llm)
        )
        thread.daemon = True
        thread.start()
        
        return job_id
    
    def _run_generation(self, job_id: str, project_id: str, include_llm: bool):
        """Run task generation in background"""
        try:
            from datetime import datetime
            from backend.services.project_service import ProjectService
            from backend.models.task import TaskEvidence, AnalysisTask, TaskCategory, TaskPriority, TaskStatus
            
            # Get project config
            project = ProjectService().get_project(project_id)
            index_path = INDEX_DIR / project_id
            
            # Initialize services
            index_service = IndexService(project)
            graph_service = CallGraphService(index_path)
            crawler_service = CrawlerReviewService(index_service, graph_service)
            task_storage = TaskStorage(project_id, DATA_DIR)
            task_generator = TaskGenerator(crawler_service, graph_service, project_id)
            
            # Generate tasks
            new_tasks = task_generator.generate_tasks(include_llm=include_llm)
            
            # Load existing tasks
            existing_tasks = task_storage.load_tasks()
            existing_ids = {t["id"] for t in existing_tasks}
            
            # Add new tasks
            for task in new_tasks:
                if task.id not in existing_ids:
                    existing_tasks.append(task.to_dict())
            
            # Save all tasks - convert dicts back to AnalysisTask objects
            all_tasks = []
            for t_dict in existing_tasks:
                # Reconstruct evidence
                evidence_objects = []
                for e in t_dict.get("evidence", []):
                    evidence_objects.append(TaskEvidence(
                        symbol=e["symbol"],
                        metric_type=e["metric_type"],
                        metric_value=e["metric_value"],
                        file_path=e["file_path"],
                        line_range=e.get("line_range"),
                        callers=e.get("callers", []),
                        callees=e.get("callees", []),
                        source=e.get("source", "rule_based")  # ADD SOURCE
                    ))
                
                # Handle dates - convert string to datetime if needed
                created_at = t_dict.get("created_at")
                if isinstance(created_at, str):
                    created_at = datetime.fromisoformat(created_at)
                elif created_at is None:
                    created_at = datetime.now()
                
                updated_at = t_dict.get("updated_at")
                if isinstance(updated_at, str):
                    updated_at = datetime.fromisoformat(updated_at)
                elif updated_at is None:
                    updated_at = datetime.now()
                
                # Handle status
                status_value = t_dict.get("status", "pending")
                if isinstance(status_value, str):
                    try:
                        status = TaskStatus(status_value)
                    except ValueError:
                        status = TaskStatus.PENDING
                else:
                    status = status_value if hasattr(status_value, 'value') else TaskStatus.PENDING
                
                all_tasks.append(AnalysisTask(
                    id=t_dict["id"],
                    title=t_dict["title"],
                    description=t_dict["description"],
                    category=TaskCategory(t_dict["category"]),
                    priority=TaskPriority(t_dict["priority"]),
                    status=status,
                    evidence=evidence_objects,
                    suggested_fix=t_dict.get("suggested_fix"),
                    impact_analysis=t_dict.get("impact_analysis"),
                    created_at=created_at,
                    updated_at=updated_at,
                    notes=t_dict.get("notes")
                ))
            
            task_storage.save_tasks(all_tasks)
            
            rule_count = len([t for t in new_tasks if "task_coupling" in t.id or "task_usage" in t.id])
            llm_count = len([t for t in new_tasks if "task_llm" in t.id])
            
            self._jobs[job_id]["status"] = "completed"
            self._jobs[job_id]["completed_at"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
            self._jobs[job_id]["result"] = {
                "rule_based_tasks": rule_count,
                "llm_discovered_tasks": llm_count,
                "total_tasks": len(existing_tasks)
            }
            
        except Exception as e:
            import traceback
            traceback.print_exc()
            self._jobs[job_id]["status"] = "failed"
            self._jobs[job_id]["completed_at"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
            self._jobs[job_id]["error"] = str(e)
    
    def get_job_status(self, job_id: str) -> Optional[Dict]:
        """Get status of a background job"""
        return self._jobs.get(job_id)
    
    def get_active_jobs(self) -> List[Dict]:
        """Get all active (running) jobs"""
        return [j for j in self._jobs.values() if j["status"] == "running"]
    
    def start_ai_only_generation(self, project_id: str) -> str:
        """Start background generation of ONLY AI-discovered tasks"""
        from datetime import datetime
        
        job_id = str(uuid.uuid4())[:8]
        
        self._jobs[job_id] = {
            "id": job_id,
            "project_id": project_id,
            "type": "ai_only",
            "status": "running",
            "started_at": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "completed_at": None,
            "result": None,
            "error": None
        }
        
        # Start background thread
        thread = threading.Thread(
            target=self._run_ai_only_generation,
            args=(job_id, project_id)
        )
        thread.daemon = True
        thread.start()
        
        return job_id
    
    def _run_ai_only_generation(self, job_id: str, project_id: str):
        """Run AI-only task generation in background"""
        try:
            from backend.services.project_service import ProjectService
            from datetime import datetime
            
            project = ProjectService().get_project(project_id)
            index_path = INDEX_DIR / project_id
            
            from backend.services.indexing.index_service import IndexService
            from backend.services.graph.call_graph_service import CallGraphService
            from backend.services.analysis.crawler_review_service import CrawlerReviewService
            from backend.services.task.task_storage import TaskStorage
            from backend.services.task.task_generator import TaskGenerator
            from backend.models.task import TaskEvidence, AnalysisTask, TaskCategory, TaskPriority, TaskStatus
            
            # Initialize services
            index_service = IndexService(project)
            graph_service = CallGraphService(index_path)
            crawler_service = CrawlerReviewService(index_service, graph_service)
            task_storage = TaskStorage(project_id, DATA_DIR)
            task_generator = TaskGenerator(crawler_service, graph_service, project_id)
            
            # Generate ONLY AI tasks
            new_tasks = task_generator.generate_ai_only_tasks()
            
            # Load existing tasks
            existing_tasks = task_storage.load_tasks()
            existing_ids = {t["id"] for t in existing_tasks}
            
            # Add only new AI tasks
            added_count = 0
            for task in new_tasks:
                if task.id not in existing_ids:
                    existing_tasks.append(task.to_dict())
                    added_count += 1
            
            # Save all tasks - convert dicts back to objects
            all_tasks = []
            for t_dict in existing_tasks:
                # Handle evidence
                evidence_objects = []
                for e in t_dict.get("evidence", []):
                    evidence_objects.append(TaskEvidence(
                        symbol=e["symbol"],
                        metric_type=e["metric_type"],
                        metric_value=e["metric_value"],
                        file_path=e["file_path"],
                        line_range=e.get("line_range"),
                        callers=e.get("callers", []),
                        callees=e.get("callees", []),
                        source=e.get("source", "rule_based")
                    ))
                
                # Handle dates - they might be strings or datetime objects
                created_at = t_dict.get("created_at")
                if isinstance(created_at, str):
                    created_at = datetime.fromisoformat(created_at)
                elif created_at is None:
                    created_at = datetime.now()
                
                updated_at = t_dict.get("updated_at")
                if isinstance(updated_at, str):
                    updated_at = datetime.fromisoformat(updated_at)
                elif updated_at is None:
                    updated_at = datetime.now()
                
                # Handle status
                status_value = t_dict.get("status", "pending")
                if isinstance(status_value, str):
                    try:
                        status = TaskStatus(status_value)
                    except ValueError:
                        status = TaskStatus.PENDING
                else:
                    status = status_value if hasattr(status_value, 'value') else TaskStatus.PENDING
                
                all_tasks.append(AnalysisTask(
                    id=t_dict["id"],
                    title=t_dict["title"],
                    description=t_dict["description"],
                    category=TaskCategory(t_dict["category"]),
                    priority=TaskPriority(t_dict["priority"]),
                    status=status,
                    evidence=evidence_objects,
                    suggested_fix=t_dict.get("suggested_fix"),
                    impact_analysis=t_dict.get("impact_analysis"),
                    created_at=created_at,
                    updated_at=updated_at,
                    notes=t_dict.get("notes")
                ))
            
            task_storage.save_tasks(all_tasks)
            
            self._jobs[job_id]["status"] = "completed"
            self._jobs[job_id]["completed_at"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
            self._jobs[job_id]["result"] = {
                "ai_tasks_generated": len(new_tasks),
                "ai_tasks_added": added_count,
                "total_tasks": len(existing_tasks)
            }
            
        except Exception as e:
            import traceback
            traceback.print_exc()
            self._jobs[job_id]["status"] = "failed"
            self._jobs[job_id]["completed_at"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
            self._jobs[job_id]["error"] = str(e)

# ========================================
# FILE: .\backend\services\task\llm_task_discovery.py
# ========================================

import json
from pathlib import Path
import re
from typing import List, Dict
from datetime import datetime
import uuid

from backend.services.llm.ollama_client import OllamaClient
from backend.models.task import (
    AnalysisTask, TaskCategory, TaskPriority, 
    TaskStatus, TaskEvidence
)


class LLMTaskDiscovery:
    """Discovers tasks using LLM analysis of codebase"""
    
    def __init__(self, crawler_service, graph_service, config):
        self.crawler = crawler_service
        self.graph = graph_service
        self.config = config
        self.llm = OllamaClient(model=config.llm_model)
    
    def discover_tasks(self, max_tasks: int = None) -> List[AnalysisTask]:
        """Discover tasks by analyzing codebase with LLM"""
        
        if not self.config.llm_enabled:
            return []
        
        max_tasks = max_tasks or self.config.llm_max_tasks
        
        # Build context for LLM
        review_context = self.crawler.build_review_context()
        hotspots = review_context.get("hotspots", [])[:20]  # Top 20 hotspots
        arch_summary = review_context.get("architecture_summary", {})
        
        prompt = self._build_discovery_prompt(hotspots, arch_summary, max_tasks)
        
        try:
            response = self.llm.generate(prompt)
            tasks = self._parse_llm_response(response)
            return tasks[:max_tasks]
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"LLM task discovery failed: {e}")
            return []
    
    def _build_discovery_prompt(self, hotspots: List[Dict], arch_summary: Dict, max_tasks: int) -> str:
        """Build prompt for LLM to discover tasks"""
        
        hotspots_text = ""
        for h in hotspots[:10]:
            hotspots_text += f"- {h['symbol']}: {h['type']} = {h['count']}\n"
        
        return f"""You are a senior software architect analyzing a Python codebase.

ARCHITECTURE SUMMARY:
- Total functions: {arch_summary.get('total_nodes', 0)}
- Total dependencies: {arch_summary.get('total_edges', 0)}
- Average fan-out: {arch_summary.get('avg_fan_out', 0):.1f}
- Max fan-out: {arch_summary.get('max_fan_out', 0)}
- Max fan-in: {arch_summary.get('max_fan_in', 0)}

TOP HOTSPOTS (rule-based detection):
{hotspots_text}

Based on this analysis, suggest {max_tasks} specific, actionable improvements.

Focus on issues that rule-based detection might miss:
1. Design pattern violations or anti-patterns
2. Potential race conditions or async issues
3. Security vulnerabilities
4. Performance bottlenecks (N+1 queries, inefficient loops)
5. Error handling gaps
6. Code duplication opportunities
7. Wrong abstraction levels
8. Missing validation or sanitization
9. Thread safety concerns
10. Resource leaks (file handles, connections)

Return ONLY valid JSON in this exact format:
{{
  "tasks": [
    {{
      "title": "Brief title (max 60 chars)",
      "description": "Detailed explanation of the issue (2-3 sentences)",
      "category": "architecture|maintainability|performance|security|reliability",
      "priority": "critical|high|medium|low",
      "suggested_fix": "Specific code change recommendation",
      "symbol_hint": "Optional: specific function/class name if relevant"
    }}
  ]
}}

Do not include any text outside the JSON."""
    
    def _parse_llm_response(self, response: str) -> List[AnalysisTask]:
        """Parse LLM response into AnalysisTask objects"""
        
        tasks = []
        
        # Extract JSON from response
        json_match = re.search(r'\{[\s\S]*"tasks"[\s\S]*\}', response)
        if not json_match:
            print("No JSON found in LLM response")
            return []
        
        try:
            data = json.loads(json_match.group())
            raw_tasks = data.get("tasks", [])
            
            for raw in raw_tasks:
                # Map category string to TaskCategory enum
                category_str = raw.get("category", "maintainability")
                category_map = {
                    "architecture": TaskCategory.ARCHITECTURE,
                    "maintainability": TaskCategory.MAINTAINABILITY,
                    "performance": TaskCategory.PERFORMANCE,
                    "security": TaskCategory.SECURITY,
                    "reliability": TaskCategory.RELIABILITY,
                    "complexity": TaskCategory.COMPLEXITY
                }
                category = category_map.get(category_str, TaskCategory.MAINTAINABILITY)
                
                # Map priority string
                priority_str = raw.get("priority", "medium")
                priority_map = {
                    "critical": TaskPriority.CRITICAL,
                    "high": TaskPriority.HIGH,
                    "medium": TaskPriority.MEDIUM,
                    "low": TaskPriority.LOW
                }
                priority = priority_map.get(priority_str, TaskPriority.MEDIUM)
                
                # Create evidence with symbol hint if provided
                symbol_hint = raw.get("symbol_hint", "unknown")
                evidence = TaskEvidence(
                    symbol=symbol_hint,
                    metric_type="llm_discovered",
                    metric_value=0,
                    file_path="unknown",
                    source="llm"
                )
                
                task = AnalysisTask(
                    id=f"task_llm_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]}",
                    title=raw.get("title", "LLM Suggested Task")[:60],
                    description=raw.get("description", ""),
                    category=category,
                    priority=priority,
                    status=TaskStatus.PENDING,
                    evidence=[evidence],
                    suggested_fix=raw.get("suggested_fix", ""),
                    created_at=datetime.now(),
                    updated_at=datetime.now()
                )
                tasks.append(task)
                
        except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
            print(f"Failed to parse LLM response: {e}")
            print(f"Response excerpt: {response[:500]}")
        
        return tasks
    
    def generate_only_llm_tasks(self, max_tasks: int = None) -> List[AnalysisTask]:
        """
        Generate ONLY LLM-discovered tasks, no rule-based tasks.
        Useful for getting AI suggestions without rule-based noise.
        """
        if not self.config.llm_enabled:
            return []
        
        max_tasks = max_tasks or self.config.llm_max_tasks
        
        # Build lighter context for AI-only generation
        review_context = self.crawler.build_review_context()
        hotspots = review_context.get("hotspots", [])[:10]  # Fewer hotspots for context
        arch_summary = review_context.get("architecture_summary", {})
        
        prompt = self._build_ai_only_prompt(hotspots, arch_summary, max_tasks)
        
        try:
            response = self.llm.generate(prompt)
            tasks = self._parse_llm_response(response)
            return tasks[:max_tasks]
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"AI-only task discovery failed: {e}")
            return []

    def _build_ai_only_prompt(self, hotspots: List[Dict], arch_summary: Dict, max_tasks: int) -> str:
        """Build prompt for AI-only task generation with code context"""
        
        # Get actual code snippets for top hotspots
        code_context = ""
        for h in hotspots[:5]:
            symbol = h.get("symbol")
            if symbol:
                # Try to get actual source code
                symbol_info = self.crawler._extract_symbols(self.crawler.index_service.get_index()).get(symbol, {})
                file_path = symbol_info.get("file", "")
                if file_path and Path(file_path).exists():
                    try:
                        lines = Path(file_path).read_text(encoding="utf-8").splitlines()
                        # Get first 30 lines of the function (simplified - would need line numbers)
                        code_context += f"\n### {symbol} in {file_path}\n```python\n"
                        # This is simplified - you'd need actual line ranges from symbols
                        code_context += "\n".join(lines[:50]) + "\n```\n"
                    except:
                        pass
        
        return f"""You are a senior software engineer. Analyze this code and provide SPECIFIC, ACTIONABLE tasks.

    CONTEXT:
    - Total functions: {arch_summary.get('total_nodes', 0)}
    - Top hotspots: {hotspots[:5] if hotspots else 'None'}

    CODE SAMPLES:
    {code_context}

    Generate {max_tasks} specific tasks. Each task must include:

    1. EXACT file path and line numbers
    2. CURRENT code snippet (what's wrong)
    3. REPLACEMENT code snippet (the fix)
    4. Why the fix improves the code

    Return ONLY valid JSON:
    {{
    "tasks": [
        {{
        "title": "Fix [specific issue] in [function name]",
        "description": "What is wrong and why",
        "file_path": "exact/path/to/file.py",
        "line_start": 42,
        "line_end": 56,
        "current_code": "def get():\n    return data",
        "replacement_code": "def get():\n    for item in data:\n        yield item",
        "category": "performance|maintainability|security",
        "priority": "critical|high|medium|low"
        }}
    ]
    }}"""

# ========================================
# FILE: .\backend\services\task\task_generator.py
# ========================================

import uuid
from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional
from datetime import datetime

from backend.models.task import (
    AnalysisTask, TaskCategory, TaskPriority, 
    TaskStatus, TaskEvidence
)
from backend.services.analysis.crawler_review_service import CrawlerReviewService
from backend.services.graph.call_graph_service import CallGraphService
from backend.config.task_config import TaskConfig
from backend.services.task.llm_task_discovery import LLMTaskDiscovery


class TaskGenerator:
    """Generates actionable tasks from codebase analysis"""

    def __init__(self, crawler_service: CrawlerReviewService, graph_service: CallGraphService, project_id: str):
        self.crawler = crawler_service
        self.graph = graph_service
        self.config = TaskConfig(project_id)
        self.llm_discovery = LLMTaskDiscovery(crawler_service, graph_service, self.config.get())

    def generate_tasks(self, include_llm: bool = True) -> List[AnalysisTask]:
        """Generate all tasks from current analysis"""
        review_context = self.crawler.build_review_context()
        hotspots = review_context.get("hotspots", [])
        symbols = review_context.get("symbols", {})

        tasks = []

        # Rule-based tasks from hotspots
        for hotspot in hotspots:
            task = self._create_task_from_hotspot(hotspot, symbols)
            if task:
                tasks.append(task)

        # LLM-discovered tasks
        if include_llm and self.config.get().llm_enabled:
            llm_tasks = self.llm_discovery.discover_tasks()
            tasks.extend(llm_tasks)

        return tasks

    def _create_task_from_hotspot(self, hotspot: Dict[str, Any], symbols: Dict) -> Optional[AnalysisTask]:
        """Create a task from a hotspot detection using configured thresholds"""
        hotspot_type = hotspot.get("type")
        symbol_name = hotspot.get("symbol")
        count = hotspot.get("count", 0)

        if hotspot_type == "fan_out":
            return self._create_coupling_task(symbol_name, count, symbols)
        elif hotspot_type == "fan_in":
            return self._create_usage_task(symbol_name, count, symbols)

        return None

    def _get_priority_from_threshold(self, count: int, medium: int, high: int, critical: int) -> TaskPriority:
        """Determine priority based on configured thresholds"""
        if count > critical:
            return TaskPriority.CRITICAL
        elif count > high:
            return TaskPriority.HIGH
        elif count > medium:
            return TaskPriority.MEDIUM
        else:
            return TaskPriority.LOW

    def _create_coupling_task(self, symbol_name: str, fan_out_count: int, symbols: Dict) -> AnalysisTask:
        """Create task for high coupling using configured thresholds"""
        symbol_info = symbols.get(symbol_name, {})
        
        priority = self._get_priority_from_threshold(
            fan_out_count,
            self.config.get().fan_out_medium,
            self.config.get().fan_out_high,
            self.config.get().fan_out_critical
        )

        evidence = TaskEvidence(
            symbol=symbol_name,
            metric_type="fan_out",
            metric_value=fan_out_count,
            file_path=symbol_info.get("file", "unknown"),
            callees=symbol_info.get("calls", [])[:20],
            source="rule_based"
        )

        suggested_fix = f"""Reduce coupling in {symbol_name} by extracting helper functions.

This function calls {fan_out_count} other functions. Move related calls into separate helper functions prefixed with '_'. Test each helper individually."""

        return AnalysisTask(
            id=f"task_coupling_{symbol_name}_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
            title=f"High coupling in {symbol_name}",
            description=f"Function '{symbol_name}' calls {fan_out_count} other functions. This indicates too many responsibilities.",
            category=TaskCategory.HIGH_COUPLING,
            priority=priority,
            status=TaskStatus.PENDING,
            evidence=[evidence],
            suggested_fix=suggested_fix
        )

    def _create_usage_task(self, symbol_name: str, fan_in_count: int, symbols: Dict) -> AnalysisTask:
        """Create task for high usage using configured thresholds"""
        symbol_info = symbols.get(symbol_name, {})
        
        priority = self._get_priority_from_threshold(
            fan_in_count,
            self.config.get().fan_in_medium,
            self.config.get().fan_in_high,
            self.config.get().fan_in_critical
        )

        evidence = TaskEvidence(
            symbol=symbol_name,
            metric_type="fan_in",
            metric_value=fan_in_count,
            file_path=symbol_info.get("file", "unknown"),
            callers=symbol_info.get("called_by", [])[:20],
            source="rule_based" 
        )

        suggested_fix = f"""Add an abstraction layer around {symbol_name}.

This function is called by {fan_in_count} other functions. Create an interface/abstract class, then update callers to depend on the abstraction instead of the concrete function."""

        return AnalysisTask(
            id=f"task_usage_{symbol_name}_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
            title=f"High usage of {symbol_name}",
            description=f"Function '{symbol_name}' is called by {fan_in_count} other functions. Changes here will break many dependents.",
            category=TaskCategory.HIGH_USAGE,
            priority=priority,
            status=TaskStatus.PENDING,
            evidence=[evidence],
            suggested_fix=suggested_fix
        )
    
    def generate_ai_only_tasks(self) -> List[AnalysisTask]:
        """Generate ONLY AI-discovered tasks (no rule-based)"""
        if not self.config.get().llm_enabled:
            return []
        
        return self.llm_discovery.generate_only_llm_tasks()   
        
        
        

# ========================================
# FILE: .\backend\services\task\task_storage.py
# ========================================

import json
from pathlib import Path
from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional
from datetime import datetime

from backend.models.task import AnalysisTask, TaskStatus, TaskCategory, TaskPriority, TaskEvidence


class TaskStorage:
    """Persistent storage for tasks (JSON file-based)"""

    def __init__(self, project_id: str, data_dir: Path):
        self.project_id = project_id
        self.tasks_file = data_dir / "tasks" / f"{project_id}.json"
        self._ensure_dir()

    def _ensure_dir(self):
        """Ensure tasks directory exists"""
        self.tasks_file.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    def save_tasks(self, tasks: List[AnalysisTask]) -> None:
        """Save all tasks to disk"""
        data = {
            "project_id": self.project_id,
            "last_updated": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "tasks": [t.to_dict() for t in tasks]
        }
        self.tasks_file.write_text(json.dumps(data, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")

    def load_tasks(self) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Load tasks from disk as dicts"""
        if not self.tasks_file.exists():
            return []
        data = json.loads(self.tasks_file.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
        return data.get("tasks", [])

    def _dict_to_task(self, task_dict: Dict[str, Any]) -> AnalysisTask:
        """Convert a dictionary back to an AnalysisTask object"""
        # Reconstruct evidence objects
        evidence_objects = []
        for e in task_dict.get("evidence", []):
            evidence_objects.append(TaskEvidence(
                symbol=e["symbol"],
                metric_type=e["metric_type"],
                metric_value=e["metric_value"],
                file_path=e["file_path"],
                line_range=e.get("line_range"),
                callers=e.get("callers", []),
                callees=e.get("callees", []),
                source=e.get("source", "rule_based")
            ))
        
        # Handle created_at and updated_at
        created_at = task_dict.get("created_at")
        if isinstance(created_at, str):
            created_at = datetime.fromisoformat(created_at)
        
        updated_at = task_dict.get("updated_at")
        if isinstance(updated_at, str):
            updated_at = datetime.fromisoformat(updated_at)
        
        # Handle status - could be string or enum
        status_value = task_dict.get("status")
        if isinstance(status_value, str):
            try:
                status = TaskStatus(status_value)
            except ValueError:
                status = TaskStatus.PENDING
        else:
            status = status_value if hasattr(status_value, 'value') else TaskStatus.PENDING
        
        return AnalysisTask(
            id=task_dict["id"],
            title=task_dict["title"],
            description=task_dict["description"],
            category=TaskCategory(task_dict["category"]),
            priority=TaskPriority(task_dict["priority"]),
            status=status,
            evidence=evidence_objects,
            suggested_fix=task_dict.get("suggested_fix"),
            impact_analysis=task_dict.get("impact_analysis"),
            created_at=created_at,
            updated_at=updated_at,
            notes=task_dict.get("notes")
        )

    def update_task_status(self, task_id: str, status: TaskStatus, notes: Optional[str] = None) -> bool:
        """Update a single task's status"""
        tasks_dicts = self.load_tasks()
        
        for task_dict in tasks_dicts:
            if task_dict["id"] == task_id:
                task_dict["status"] = status.value if hasattr(status, 'value') else str(status)
                task_dict["updated_at"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
                if notes:
                    task_dict["notes"] = notes
                
                # Convert all dicts back to AnalysisTask objects
                analysis_tasks = []
                for td in tasks_dicts:
                    analysis_tasks.append(self._dict_to_task(td))
                
                self.save_tasks(analysis_tasks)
                return True
        return False

# ========================================
# FILE: .\frontend\static\js\ai_refactor_agent.js

// AI Refactoring Agent - No conflicts with task_board.js

const AI_REFACTOR_STORAGE_KEY = 'ai_refactor_suggestions';

class AIRefactorAgent {
    constructor() {
        this.apiBase = '/api/refactor';
        this.suggestions = [];
        this.isAnalyzing = false;
        this.init();
    }

    init() {
        this.loadSavedSuggestions();
        this.attachEventListeners();
        this.updateBadgeCount();
    }

    attachEventListeners() {
        const analyzeBtn = document.getElementById('analyzeCodebaseBtn');
        if (analyzeBtn) {
            analyzeBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.analyzeCodebase());
        }

        const refreshBtn = document.getElementById('refreshAISuggestionsBtn');
        if (refreshBtn) {
            refreshBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.loadSavedSuggestions());
        }

        const clearBtn = document.getElementById('clearAISuggestionsBtn');
        if (clearBtn) {
            clearBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.clearSuggestions());
        }
    }

    async analyzeCodebase() {
        if (this.isAnalyzing) return;

        this.isAnalyzing = true;
        this.showStatus('🤖 AI is analyzing your codebase for refactorings...');

        try {
            const functions = await this.getAllFunctions();

            this.showStatus(`📊 Found ${functions.length} functions. Analyzing...`);

            const suggestions = [];
            const functionsToAnalyze = functions.slice(0, 15);

            for (let i = 0; i < functionsToAnalyze.length; i++) {
                const func = functionsToAnalyze[i];
                this.showStatus(`🔍 Analyzing ${i + 1}/${functionsToAnalyze.length}: ${func.name}...`);

                try {
                    const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/suggest/${encodeURIComponent(func.name)}`, {
                        method: 'POST'
                    });

                    if (response.ok) {
                        const data = await response.json();
                        if (data.suggestions && data.suggestions.length > 0) {
                            suggestions.push({
                                function_name: func.name,
                                file: func.file,
                                type: func.type,
                                parent: func.parent,
                                suggestions: data.suggestions,
                                analyzed_at: new Date().toISOString()
                            });
                        }
                    }
                } catch (e) {
                    console.error(`Error analyzing ${func.name}:`, e);
                }

                await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 500));
            }

            this.suggestions = suggestions;
            this.saveSuggestions();
            this.renderSuggestions();
            this.updateBadgeCount();
            this.showStatus(`✅ Analysis complete! Found ${suggestions.length} functions with suggestions.`, 'success');

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Analysis failed:', error);
            this.showStatus('❌ Analysis failed. Please try again.', 'error');
        } finally {
            this.isAnalyzing = false;
            setTimeout(() => this.hideStatus(), 3000);
        }
    }

    async getAllFunctions() {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/search/functions?query=&limit=100`);
            const data = await response.json();
            return data.functions || [];
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Error fetching functions:', error);
            return [];
        }
    }

    showStatus(message, type = 'info') {
        const statusDiv = document.getElementById('aiStatus');
        const messageDiv = statusDiv?.querySelector('.status-message');

        if (statusDiv) {
            statusDiv.style.display = 'block';
            if (messageDiv) {
                messageDiv.textContent = message;
                messageDiv.className = `status-message status-${type}`;
            }
        }
    }

    hideStatus() {
        const statusDiv = document.getElementById('aiStatus');
        if (statusDiv) {
            setTimeout(() => {
                statusDiv.style.display = 'none';
            }, 2000);
        }
    }

    saveSuggestions() {
        localStorage.setItem(AI_REFACTOR_STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(this.suggestions));
        localStorage.setItem(`${AI_REFACTOR_STORAGE_KEY}_timestamp`, new Date().toISOString());
    }

    loadSavedSuggestions() {
        const saved = localStorage.getItem(AI_REFACTOR_STORAGE_KEY);
        if (saved) {
            this.suggestions = JSON.parse(saved);
            this.renderSuggestions();
            this.updateBadgeCount();
            const timestamp = localStorage.getItem(`${AI_REFACTOR_STORAGE_KEY}_timestamp`);
            if (timestamp) {
                this.showStatus(`📋 Loaded ${this.suggestions.length} suggestions from ${new Date(timestamp).toLocaleString()}`, 'info');
                setTimeout(() => this.hideStatus(), 2000);
            }
        } else {
            this.renderEmpty();
        }
    }

    clearSuggestions() {
        if (confirm('Clear all AI refactoring suggestions?')) {
            this.suggestions = [];
            localStorage.removeItem(AI_REFACTOR_STORAGE_KEY);
            localStorage.removeItem(`${AI_REFACTOR_STORAGE_KEY}_timestamp`);
            this.renderEmpty();
            this.updateBadgeCount();
            this.showStatus('🗑️ All suggestions cleared', 'info');
            setTimeout(() => this.hideStatus(), 1500);
        }
    }

    updateBadgeCount() {
        const badge = document.getElementById('aiGeneratedCount');
        if (badge) {
            const totalSuggestions = this.suggestions.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.suggestions.length, 0);
            badge.textContent = totalSuggestions;
        }
    }

    renderEmpty() {
        const container = document.getElementById('aiSuggestionsList');
        if (container) {
            container.innerHTML = `
                <div class="info-message">
                    💡 No refactoring suggestions yet.<br>
                    Click "Analyze Codebase" to get AI-powered recommendations.
                </div>
            `;
        }
    }

    renderSuggestions() {
        const container = document.getElementById('aiSuggestionsList');
        if (!container) return;

        if (!this.suggestions || this.suggestions.length === 0) {
            this.renderEmpty();
            return;
        }

        let totalSuggestions = 0;
        let html = '';

        for (const item of this.suggestions) {
            for (const suggestion of item.suggestions) {
                totalSuggestions++;
                html += this.renderSuggestionCard(item, suggestion);
            }
        }

        if (totalSuggestions === 0) {
            this.renderEmpty();
            return;
        }

        container.innerHTML = `
            <div class="suggestions-header">
                <span>🎯 Found ${totalSuggestions} refactoring suggestions</span>
            </div>
            ${html}
        `;

        this.attachCardHandlers();
        this.updateBadgeCount();
    }

    renderSuggestionCard(item, suggestion) {
        const difficultyClass = (suggestion.difficulty || 'medium').toLowerCase();
        const typeIcon = this.getTypeIcon(suggestion.type);
        const typeName = (suggestion.type || 'refactoring').replace(/_/g, ' ').toUpperCase();

        return `
            <div class="ai-suggestion-card" data-function="${item.function_name}" data-suggestion-type="${suggestion.type}">
                <div class="suggestion-header">
                    <div class="suggestion-type ${difficultyClass}">
                        ${typeIcon} ${typeName}
                    </div>
                    <div class="suggestion-difficulty ${difficultyClass}">
                        📊 ${suggestion.difficulty || 'Medium'} Difficulty
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="suggestion-function">
                    <strong>🎯 Function:</strong> ${item.function_name}
                    ${item.parent ? `<span class="class-name">(${item.parent})</span>` : ''}
                </div>
                <div class="suggestion-file">
                    <strong>📁 File:</strong> ${item.file?.split('/').pop() || 'Unknown'}
                </div>
                <div class="suggestion-reason">
                    <strong>💡 Reason:</strong> ${suggestion.reason || 'Improve code quality and maintainability'}
                </div>
                ${suggestion.affected_lines ? `
                <div class="suggestion-lines">
                    <strong>📍 Lines:</strong> ${suggestion.affected_lines}
                </div>
                ` : ''}
                <div class="suggestion-actions">
                    <button class="btn-preview" data-function="${item.function_name}" data-type="${suggestion.type}" data-suggestion='${this.escapeJson(JSON.stringify(suggestion))}'>
                        👁️ Preview Changes
                    </button>
                    <button class="btn-generate-plan" data-function="${item.function_name}" data-type="${suggestion.type}" data-suggestion='${this.escapeJson(JSON.stringify(suggestion))}'>
                        🔨 Generate Plan
                    </button>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    }

    escapeJson(str) {
        return str.replace(/'/g, "&#39;").replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
    }

    getTypeIcon(type) {
        const icons = {
            'extract_method': '📦',
            'inline_function': '🔄',
            'add_parameter': '➕',
            'remove_parameter': '➖',
            'rename_function': '✏️',
            'simplify_logic': '🧹'
        };
        return icons[type] || '🔧';
    }

    attachCardHandlers() {
        document.querySelectorAll('#aiSuggestionsList .btn-preview').forEach(btn => {
            btn.removeEventListener('click', this.handlePreview);
            btn.addEventListener('click', this.handlePreview.bind(this));
        });

        document.querySelectorAll('#aiSuggestionsList .btn-generate-plan').forEach(btn => {
            btn.removeEventListener('click', this.handleGenerate);
            btn.addEventListener('click', this.handleGenerate.bind(this));
        });
    }

    async handlePreview(event) {
        const btn = event.currentTarget;
        const functionName = btn.dataset.function;
        const type = btn.dataset.type;
        const suggestion = JSON.parse(btn.dataset.suggestion);
        await this.previewRefactoring(functionName, type, suggestion);
    }

    async handleGenerate(event) {
        const btn = event.currentTarget;
        const functionName = btn.dataset.function;
        const type = btn.dataset.type;
        const suggestion = JSON.parse(btn.dataset.suggestion);
        await this.generateAndShowPlan(functionName, type, suggestion);
    }

    async previewRefactoring(functionName, type, suggestion) {
        const modal = document.getElementById('taskModal');
        const modalBody = document.getElementById('modalBody');
        if (!modal || !modalBody) return;

        modalBody.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">Generating preview...</div>';
        modal.style.display = 'block';

        try {
            let plan = null;

            switch (type) {
                case 'extract_method':
                    const lines = suggestion.affected_lines?.split('-') || ['0', '0'];
                    plan = await this.callExtractMethod(functionName, parseInt(lines[0]), parseInt(lines[1]), suggestion.suggested_name || '_extracted');
                    break;
                case 'inline_function':
                    plan = await this.callInlineFunction(functionName);
                    break;
                default:
                    modalBody.innerHTML = '<div class="info-message">Preview not available for this refactoring type yet</div>';
                    return;
            }

            if (plan && plan.changes) {
                this.showPlanPreview(plan);
            } else {
                modalBody.innerHTML = '<div class="info-message">Failed to generate preview</div>';
            }
        } catch (error) {
            modalBody.innerHTML = `<div class="info-message">Error: ${error.message}</div>`;
        }
    }

    async generateAndShowPlan(functionName, type, suggestion) {
        const modal = document.getElementById('taskModal');
        const modalBody = document.getElementById('modalBody');
        if (!modal || !modalBody) return;

        modalBody.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">Generating refactoring plan...</div>';
        modal.style.display = 'block';

        try {
            let plan = null;

            switch (type) {
                case 'extract_method':
                    const lines = suggestion.affected_lines?.split('-') || ['0', '0'];
                    plan = await this.callExtractMethod(functionName, parseInt(lines[0]), parseInt(lines[1]), suggestion.suggested_name || '_extracted');
                    break;
                case 'inline_function':
                    plan = await this.callInlineFunction(functionName);
                    break;
                default:
                    modalBody.innerHTML = '<div class="info-message">Plan generation not available for this refactoring type yet</div>';
                    return;
            }

            if (plan) {
                this.showPlanPreview(plan);
            } else {
                modalBody.innerHTML = '<div class="info-message">Failed to generate plan</div>';
            }
        } catch (error) {
            modalBody.innerHTML = `<div class="info-message">Error: ${error.message}</div>`;
        }
    }

    async callExtractMethod(functionName, startLine, endLine, newMethodName) {
        const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/plan/extract-method`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                function_name: functionName,
                start_line: startLine,
                end_line: endLine,
                new_method_name: newMethodName
            })
        });
        return response.json();
    }

    async callInlineFunction(functionName) {
        const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/plan/inline-function`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ function_name: functionName })
        });
        return response.json();
    }

    showPlanPreview(plan) {
        const modalBody = document.getElementById('modalBody');
        if (!modalBody) return;

        let changesHtml = '';
        for (const change of plan.changes) {
            changesHtml += `
                <div class="plan-change">
                    <div class="change-file">📄 ${(change.file_path || '').split('/').pop()}</div>
                    <div class="change-description">${change.description || 'Code change'}</div>
                    <div class="diff-view">
                        <div class="diff-before">- ${(change.before || '').split('\n')[0].substring(0, 100)}</div>
                        <div class="diff-after">+ ${(change.after || '').split('\n')[0].substring(0, 100)}</div>
                    </div>
                    <button class="copy-change-btn" data-before="${this.escapeHtml(change.before || '')}" data-after="${this.escapeHtml(change.after || '')}">
                        📋 Copy Code Change
                    </button>
                </div>
            `;
        }

        modalBody.innerHTML = `
            <div class="plan-details">
                <h3>Refactoring Plan</h3>
                <div class="plan-meta">
                    <div>🎯 Target: ${plan.target_function || 'Unknown'}</div>
                    <div>📝 Type: ${plan.refactor_type || 'Unknown'}</div>
                    <div>🎯 Confidence: ${Math.round((plan.confidence || 0) * 100)}%</div>
                    <div>${plan.requires_review ? '⚠️ Requires Review' : '✅ Auto-approved'}</div>
                </div>
                <div class="plan-changes">
                    <h4>Changes (${plan.changes?.length || 0} files):</h4>
                    ${changesHtml}
                </div>
            </div>
        `;

        document.querySelectorAll('.copy-change-btn').forEach(btn => {
            btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                const text = `# BEFORE:\n${this.unescapeHtml(btn.dataset.before)}\n\n# AFTER:\n${this.unescapeHtml(btn.dataset.after)}`;
                navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
                btn.textContent = '✅ Copied!';
                setTimeout(() => {
                    btn.textContent = '📋 Copy Code Change';
                }, 2000);
            });
        });
    }

    escapeHtml(str) {
        if (!str) return '';
        return str.replace(/[&<>]/g, function (m) {
            if (m === '&') return '&amp;';
            if (m === '<') return '&lt;';
            if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
            return m;
        });
    }

    unescapeHtml(str) {
        if (!str) return '';
        return str.replace(/&amp;/g, '&').replace(/&lt;/g, '<').replace(/&gt;/g, '>');
    }
}

// Initialize when DOM is ready - no conflicts with task_board.js
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    window.aiRefactorAgent = new AIRefactorAgent();

    // Tab switching with proper CSS class handling
    const tabs = document.querySelectorAll('.tab-button');
    const contents = document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content');

    tabs.forEach(tab => {
        tab.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const tabId = tab.dataset.tab;

            // Remove active class from all tabs and contents
            tabs.forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
            contents.forEach(c => c.classList.remove('active'));

            // Add active class to clicked tab
            tab.classList.add('active');

            // Show corresponding content
            const targetContent = document.getElementById(`${tabId}Tab`);
            if (targetContent) {
                targetContent.classList.add('active');
            }
        });
    });

    // Log to confirm initialization
    console.log('AI Refactor Agent initialized, tabs:', tabs.length);
});

# ========================================
# FILE: .\frontend\static\js\ai_refactor_modal.js
# ========================================

// AI Refactoring Agent - Modal Version
const AI_REFACTOR_MODAL_STORAGE_KEY = 'ai_refactor_suggestions_modal';

class AIRefactorModalAgent {
    constructor() {
        this.apiBase = '/api/refactor';
        this.suggestions = [];
        this.isAnalyzing = false;
        this.init();
    }

    init() {
        this.loadSavedSuggestions();
        this.attachEventListeners();
    }

    attachEventListeners() {
        const analyzeBtn = document.getElementById('analyzeCodebaseBtn');
        if (analyzeBtn) {
            analyzeBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.analyzeCodebase());
        }

        const refreshBtn = document.getElementById('refreshAISuggestionsBtn');
        if (refreshBtn) {
            refreshBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.loadSavedSuggestions());
        }

        const clearBtn = document.getElementById('clearAISuggestionsBtn');
        if (clearBtn) {
            clearBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.clearSuggestions());
        }
    }

    async analyzeCodebase() {
        if (this.isAnalyzing) return;

        this.isAnalyzing = true;
        this.showStatus('🤖 AI is analyzing your codebase for refactorings...');

        try {
            const functions = await this.getAllFunctions();
            
            this.showStatus(`📊 Found ${functions.length} functions. Analyzing...`);
            
            const suggestions = [];
            const functionsToAnalyze = functions.slice(0, 15);

            for (let i = 0; i < functionsToAnalyze.length; i++) {
                const func = functionsToAnalyze[i];
                this.showStatus(`🔍 Analyzing ${i+1}/${functionsToAnalyze.length}: ${func.name}...`);
                
                try {
                    const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/suggest/${encodeURIComponent(func.name)}`, {
                        method: 'POST'
                    });
                    
                    if (response.ok) {
                        const data = await response.json();
                        if (data.suggestions && data.suggestions.length > 0) {
                            suggestions.push({
                                function_name: func.name,
                                file: func.file,
                                type: func.type,
                                parent: func.parent,
                                suggestions: data.suggestions,
                                analyzed_at: new Date().toISOString()
                            });
                        }
                    }
                } catch (e) {
                    console.error(`Error analyzing ${func.name}:`, e);
                }
                
                await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 500));
            }

            this.suggestions = suggestions;
            this.saveSuggestions();
            this.renderSuggestions();
            this.showStatus(`✅ Analysis complete! Found ${suggestions.length} functions with suggestions.`, 'success');
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Analysis failed:', error);
            this.showStatus('❌ Analysis failed. Please try again.', 'error');
        } finally {
            this.isAnalyzing = false;
            setTimeout(() => this.hideStatus(), 3000);
        }
    }

    async getAllFunctions() {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/search/functions?query=&limit=100`);
            const data = await response.json();
            return data.functions || [];
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Error fetching functions:', error);
            return [];
        }
    }

    showStatus(message, type = 'info') {
        const statusDiv = document.getElementById('aiStatus');
        const messageDiv = statusDiv?.querySelector('.status-message');
        
        if (statusDiv) {
            statusDiv.style.display = 'block';
            if (messageDiv) {
                messageDiv.textContent = message;
                messageDiv.className = `status-message status-${type}`;
            }
        }
    }

    hideStatus() {
        const statusDiv = document.getElementById('aiStatus');
        if (statusDiv) {
            setTimeout(() => {
                statusDiv.style.display = 'none';
            }, 2000);
        }
    }

    saveSuggestions() {
        localStorage.setItem(AI_REFACTOR_STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(this.suggestions));
        localStorage.setItem(`${AI_REFACTOR_STORAGE_KEY}_timestamp`, new Date().toISOString());
    }

    loadSavedSuggestions() {
        const saved = localStorage.getItem(AI_REFACTOR_STORAGE_KEY);
        if (saved) {
            this.suggestions = JSON.parse(saved);
            this.renderSuggestions();
            const timestamp = localStorage.getItem(`${AI_REFACTOR_STORAGE_KEY}_timestamp`);
            if (timestamp) {
                this.showStatus(`📋 Loaded ${this.suggestions.length} suggestions from ${new Date(timestamp).toLocaleString()}`, 'info');
                setTimeout(() => this.hideStatus(), 2000);
            }
        } else {
            this.renderEmpty();
        }
    }

    clearSuggestions() {
        if (confirm('Clear all AI refactoring suggestions?')) {
            this.suggestions = [];
            localStorage.removeItem(AI_REFACTOR_STORAGE_KEY);
            localStorage.removeItem(`${AI_REFACTOR_STORAGE_KEY}_timestamp`);
            this.renderEmpty();
            this.showStatus('🗑️ All suggestions cleared', 'info');
            setTimeout(() => this.hideStatus(), 1500);
        }
    }

    renderEmpty() {
        const container = document.getElementById('aiSuggestionsList');
        if (container) {
            container.innerHTML = `
                <div class="info-message">
                    💡 No refactoring suggestions yet.<br>
                    Click "Analyze Codebase" to get AI-powered recommendations.
                </div>
            `;
        }
    }

    renderSuggestions() {
        const container = document.getElementById('aiSuggestionsList');
        if (!container) return;

        if (!this.suggestions || this.suggestions.length === 0) {
            this.renderEmpty();
            return;
        }

        let totalSuggestions = 0;
        let html = '<div style="margin-bottom: 15px;"><strong>🎯 Refactoring Suggestions:</strong></div>';

        for (const item of this.suggestions) {
            for (const suggestion of item.suggestions) {
                totalSuggestions++;
                html += this.renderSuggestionCard(item, suggestion);
            }
        }

        if (totalSuggestions === 0) {
            this.renderEmpty();
            return;
        }

        container.innerHTML = html;
        this.attachCardHandlers();
    }

    renderSuggestionCard(item, suggestion) {
        const difficultyClass = (suggestion.difficulty || 'medium').toLowerCase();
        const typeIcon = this.getTypeIcon(suggestion.type);
        const typeName = (suggestion.type || 'refactoring').replace(/_/g, ' ').toUpperCase();
        
        return `
            <div style="background: white; border: 1px solid #e0e0e0; border-radius: 10px; padding: 15px; margin-bottom: 15px;">
                <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; margin-bottom: 12px; flex-wrap: wrap; gap: 8px;">
                    <span style="padding: 4px 12px; border-radius: 20px; font-size: 0.8rem; background: ${difficultyClass === 'easy' ? '#d4edda' : difficultyClass === 'medium' ? '#fff3cd' : '#f8d7da'}; color: ${difficultyClass === 'easy' ? '#155724' : difficultyClass === 'medium' ? '#856404' : '#721c24'};">${typeIcon} ${typeName}</span>
                    <span>📊 ${suggestion.difficulty || 'Medium'} Difficulty</span>
