                </div>
                <div><strong>🎯 Function:</strong> ${item.function_name} ${item.parent ? `(${item.parent})` : ''}</div>
                <div><strong>📁 File:</strong> ${item.file?.split('/').pop() || 'Unknown'}</div>
                <div><strong>💡 Reason:</strong> ${suggestion.reason || 'Improve code quality'}</div>
                ${suggestion.affected_lines ? `<div><strong>📍 Lines:</strong> ${suggestion.affected_lines}</div>` : ''}
                <div style="margin-top: 12px; display: flex; gap: 10px;">
                    <button class="btn-preview-suggestion" data-function="${item.function_name}" data-type="${suggestion.type}" data-suggestion='${JSON.stringify(suggestion)}' style="padding: 6px 12px; background: #6c757d; color: white; border: none; border-radius: 6px; cursor: pointer;">👁️ Preview</button>
                    <button class="btn-generate-suggestion" data-function="${item.function_name}" data-type="${suggestion.type}" data-suggestion='${JSON.stringify(suggestion)}' style="padding: 6px 12px; background: #28a745; color: white; border: none; border-radius: 6px; cursor: pointer;">🔨 Generate Plan</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    }

    getTypeIcon(type) {
        const icons = {
            'extract_method': '📦',
            'inline_function': '🔄',
            'add_parameter': '➕',
            'remove_parameter': '➖',
            'rename_function': '✏️'
        };
        return icons[type] || '🔧';
    }

    attachCardHandlers() {
        document.querySelectorAll('.btn-preview-suggestion').forEach(btn => {
            btn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
                const functionName = btn.dataset.function;
                const type = btn.dataset.type;
                const suggestion = JSON.parse(btn.dataset.suggestion);
                await this.previewRefactoring(functionName, type, suggestion);
            });
        });

        document.querySelectorAll('.btn-generate-suggestion').forEach(btn => {
            btn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
                const functionName = btn.dataset.function;
                const type = btn.dataset.type;
                const suggestion = JSON.parse(btn.dataset.suggestion);
                await this.generatePlan(functionName, type, suggestion);
            });
        });
    }

    async previewRefactoring(functionName, type, suggestion) {
        const modalBody = document.getElementById('modalBody');
        const taskModal = document.getElementById('taskModal');
        
        if (!modalBody || !taskModal) return;
        
        modalBody.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">Generating preview...</div>';
        taskModal.style.display = 'block';

        try {
            let plan = null;
            
            if (type === 'extract_method') {
                const lines = suggestion.affected_lines?.split('-') || ['0', '0'];
                const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/plan/extract-method`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({
                        function_name: functionName,
                        start_line: parseInt(lines[0]),
                        end_line: parseInt(lines[1]),
                        new_method_name: suggestion.suggested_name || '_extracted'
                    })
                });
                plan = await response.json();
            } else if (type === 'inline_function') {
                const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/plan/inline-function`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ function_name: functionName })
                });
                plan = await response.json();
            }
            
            if (plan && plan.changes) {
                this.showPlanPreview(plan);
            } else {
                modalBody.innerHTML = '<div class="info-message">Failed to generate preview</div>';
            }
        } catch (error) {
            modalBody.innerHTML = `<div class="info-message">Error: ${error.message}</div>`;
        }
    }

    async generatePlan(functionName, type, suggestion) {
        const modalBody = document.getElementById('modalBody');
        const taskModal = document.getElementById('taskModal');
        
        if (!modalBody || !taskModal) return;
        
        modalBody.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">Generating plan...</div>';
        taskModal.style.display = 'block';

        try {
            let plan = null;
            
            if (type === 'extract_method') {
                const lines = suggestion.affected_lines?.split('-') || ['0', '0'];
                const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/plan/extract-method`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({
                        function_name: functionName,
                        start_line: parseInt(lines[0]),
                        end_line: parseInt(lines[1]),
                        new_method_name: suggestion.suggested_name || '_extracted'
                    })
                });
                plan = await response.json();
            } else if (type === 'inline_function') {
                const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/plan/inline-function`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ function_name: functionName })
                });
                plan = await response.json();
            }
            
            if (plan) {
                this.showPlanPreview(plan);
            } else {
                modalBody.innerHTML = '<div class="info-message">Failed to generate plan</div>';
            }
        } catch (error) {
            modalBody.innerHTML = `<div class="info-message">Error: ${error.message}</div>`;
        }
    }

    showPlanPreview(plan) {
        const modalBody = document.getElementById('modalBody');
        if (!modalBody) return;
        
        let changesHtml = '';
        for (const change of plan.changes) {
            changesHtml += `
                <div style="margin: 15px 0; padding: 12px; background: #f8f9fa; border-radius: 8px; border-left: 3px solid #667eea;">
                    <div style="font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 8px; color: #667eea;">📄 ${(change.file_path || '').split('/').pop()}</div>
                    <div style="margin-bottom: 8px;">${change.description || 'Code change'}</div>
                    <div style="font-family: monospace; font-size: 0.8rem;">
                        <div style="color: #c7254e; background: #f9f2f4; padding: 4px; margin: 2px 0;">- ${(change.before || '').split('\n')[0].substring(0, 100)}</div>
                        <div style="color: #3c763d; background: #dff0d8; padding: 4px; margin: 2px 0;">+ ${(change.after || '').split('\n')[0].substring(0, 100)}</div>
                    </div>
                    <button class="copy-plan-btn" data-before="${this.escapeHtml(change.before || '')}" data-after="${this.escapeHtml(change.after || '')}" style="margin-top: 8px; padding: 4px 8px; background: #007bff; color: white; border: none; border-radius: 4px; cursor: pointer;">📋 Copy Code Change</button>
                </div>
            `;
        }
        
        modalBody.innerHTML = `
            <div>
                <h3>Refactoring Plan</h3>
                <div style="display: flex; gap: 10px; margin-bottom: 15px; flex-wrap: wrap;">
                    <div>🎯 Target: ${plan.target_function || 'Unknown'}</div>
                    <div>📝 Type: ${plan.refactor_type || 'Unknown'}</div>
                    <div>🎯 Confidence: ${Math.round((plan.confidence || 0) * 100)}%</div>
                    <div>${plan.requires_review ? '⚠️ Requires Review' : '✅ Auto-approved'}</div>
                </div>
                <h4>Changes (${plan.changes?.length || 0} files):</h4>
                ${changesHtml}
            </div>
        `;
        
        document.querySelectorAll('.copy-plan-btn').forEach(btn => {
            btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                const text = `# BEFORE:\n${this.unescapeHtml(btn.dataset.before)}\n\n# AFTER:\n${this.unescapeHtml(btn.dataset.after)}`;
                navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
                btn.textContent = '✅ Copied!';
                setTimeout(() => {
                    btn.textContent = '📋 Copy Code Change';
                }, 2000);
            });
        });
    }

    escapeHtml(str) {
        if (!str) return '';
        return str.replace(/[&<>]/g, function(m) {
            if (m === '&') return '&amp;';
            if (m === '<') return '&lt;';
            if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
            return m;
        });
    }

    unescapeHtml(str) {
        if (!str) return '';
        return str.replace(/&amp;/g, '&').replace(/&lt;/g, '<').replace(/&gt;/g, '>');
    }
}

// Initialize when DOM is ready
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    window.aiRefactorModalAgent = new AIRefactorModalAgent();
});

# ========================================
# FILE: .\frontend\static\js\chat.js
# ========================================

document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {

    const STORAGE_KEY = "idm_dev_agent_chat";

    const chatWindow =
        document.getElementById("chat-window");

    const input =
        document.getElementById("chat-input");

    const button =
        document.getElementById("send-button");

    const newChatButton =
        document.getElementById("new-chat-button");

    let history = [];

    function saveHistory() {

        localStorage.setItem(

            STORAGE_KEY,

            JSON.stringify(history)

        );

    }

    function scrollBottom() {

        chatWindow.scrollTop =
            chatWindow.scrollHeight;

    }

    function renderMessage(role, text, metadata = null) {

        const wrapper =
            document.createElement("div");

        wrapper.className =
            role === "user"
                ? "user-message"
                : "assistant-message";

        const avatar =
            document.createElement("div");

        avatar.className = "avatar";

        avatar.textContent =
            role === "user"
                ? "👤"
                : "🤖";

        const bubble =
            document.createElement("div");

        bubble.className = "bubble";

        if (role === "assistant") {

            bubble.innerHTML =
                marked.parse(text);

            bubble.querySelectorAll("pre code")
                .forEach(block => {

                    hljs.highlightElement(block);

                });

            const copy =
                document.createElement("button");

            copy.className =
                "copy-button";

            copy.textContent = "Copy";

            copy.onclick = () => {

                navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).catch(console.error);

                copy.textContent = "Copied!";

                setTimeout(() => {

                    copy.textContent = "Copy";

                }, 1500);

            };

            bubble.prepend(copy);

            if (metadata && metadata.metrics) {

                const details =
                    document.createElement("details");

                details.className = "diagnostics";

                const summary =
                    document.createElement("summary");

                summary.textContent =
                    "Diagnostics";

                details.appendChild(summary);

                const table =
                    document.createElement("table");

                table.innerHTML = `

                        <tr>

                        <td class="metric-label">Intent</td>

                        <td>${metadata.intent}</td>

                        </tr>

                        <tr>

                        <td class="metric-label">Resolved Symbol</td>

                        <td>${metadata.symbol}</td>

                        </tr>

                        <tr>

                        <td class="metric-label">Context Size</td>

                        <td>${metadata.metrics.context_chars} chars</td>

                        </tr>

                        <tr>

                        <td class="metric-label">Prompt Size</td>

                        <td>${metadata.metrics.prompt_chars} chars</td>

                        </tr>

                        <tr>

                        <td class="metric-label">Model</td>

                        <td>${metadata.metrics.model}</td>

                        </tr>

                        <tr>

                        <td class="metric-label">LLM Time</td>

                        <td>${metadata.metrics.llm_ms} ms</td>

                        </tr>

                        <tr>

                        <td class="metric-label">Total Time</td>

                        <td>${metadata.metrics.total_ms} ms</td>

                        </tr>

                        `;

                details.appendChild(table);

                bubble.appendChild(details);

            }

        }
        else {

            bubble.textContent = text;

        }

        wrapper.appendChild(avatar);

        wrapper.appendChild(bubble);

        chatWindow.appendChild(wrapper);

        scrollBottom();

    }

    function redrawConversation() {

        chatWindow.innerHTML = "";

        if (history.length === 0) {

            renderMessage(

                "assistant",

                "# Welcome\n\nAsk me anything about your project."

            );

            return;

        }

        history.forEach(msg => {

            renderMessage(

                msg.role,

                msg.text,

                msg.metadata || null

            );

        });

    }

    async function sendMessage() {

        const message =
            input.value.trim();

        if (!message)
            return;

        history.push({

            role: "user",

            text: message

        });

        saveHistory();

        renderMessage(

            "user",

            message

        );

        input.value = "";

        const loadingWrapper =
            document.createElement("div");

        loadingWrapper.className =
            "assistant-message";

        loadingWrapper.innerHTML =

            '<div class="avatar">🤖</div><div class="bubble">Thinking...</div>';

        chatWindow.appendChild(

            loadingWrapper

        );

        scrollBottom();

        try {

            const response =
                await fetch(

                    "/agent/chat",

                    {

                        method: "POST",

                        headers: {

                            "Content-Type":

                                "application/json"

                        },

                        body: JSON.stringify({

                            message

                        })

                    }

                );

            const data =
                await response.json();

            loadingWrapper.remove();

            history.push({

                role: "assistant",

                text: data.answer,

                metadata: {

                    intent: data.intent,

                    symbol: data.symbol,

                    metrics: data.metrics

                }

            });

            saveHistory();

            renderMessage(
                "assistant",
                data.answer,
                data
            );

        }
        catch {

            loadingWrapper.remove();

            history.push({

                role: "assistant",

                text: "**Error contacting agent.**"

            });

            saveHistory();

            renderMessage(

                "assistant",

                "**Error contacting agent.**"

            );

        }

    }

    button.onclick = sendMessage;

    input.addEventListener(

        "keydown",

        e => {

            if (

                e.key === "Enter"

                &&

                !e.shiftKey

            ) {

                e.preventDefault();

                sendMessage();

            }

        }

    );

    newChatButton.onclick = () => {

        if (

            confirm(

                "Start a new conversation?"

            )

        ) {

            history = [];

            saveHistory();

            redrawConversation();

        }

    };

    const stored =
        localStorage.getItem(
            STORAGE_KEY
        );

    if (stored) {

        try {
            history = JSON.parse(stored);
        }
        catch {
            history = [];
        }

    }

    redrawConversation();

});

# ========================================
# FILE: .\frontend\static\js\refactor.js
# ========================================

class RefactoringAgent {
    constructor() {
        this.apiBase = '/api/refactor';
        this.currentPlan = null;
        this.selectedFunction = null;
        this.currentFunction = null;
        this.init();
    }

    init() {
        this.createUI();
        this.attachEventListeners();
    }

    createUI() {
        const taskBoard = document.querySelector('.task-board-container');
        if (!taskBoard) return;

        const panel = document.createElement('div');
        panel.className = 'refactoring-panel';
        panel.innerHTML = `
            <div class="refactoring-header">
                <h3>🔧 Deep Refactoring Agent</h3>
                <button class="close-panel">&times;</button>
            </div>
            <div class="refactoring-content">
                <div class="function-search">
                    <input type="text" placeholder="Search function to refactor..." id="func-search">
                    <div class="search-results" id="search-results"></div>
                </div>
                <div class="function-info" id="function-info" style="display:none;">
                    <h4 id="func-name"></h4>
                    <p id="func-location"></p>
                    <div class="func-stats">
                        <span class="badge" id="caller-count">0 callers</span>
                        <span class="badge" id="param-count">0 parameters</span>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="refactor-type-selector">
                    <label>Refactoring Type:</label>
                    <select id="refactor-type">
                        <option value="">Select refactoring...</option>
                        <option value="add_parameter">➕ Add Parameter</option>
                        <option value="remove_parameter">➖ Remove Parameter</option>
                        <option value="rename_function">✏️ Rename Function</option>
                        <option value="extract_method">📦 Extract Method (LLM)</option>
                        <option value="inline_function">🔄 Inline Function (LLM)</option>
                    </select>
                </div>
                <div id="refactor-params" style="display:none;"></div>
                <div class="action-buttons">
                    <button id="analyze-impact" class="btn-secondary">📊 Analyze Impact</button>
                    <button id="generate-plan" class="btn-primary">🔨 Generate Plan</button>
                </div>
                <div id="impact-analysis" style="display:none;" class="impact-box"></div>
                <div id="plan-preview" style="display:none;" class="plan-preview"></div>
            </div>
        `;

        taskBoard.insertBefore(panel, taskBoard.firstChild);
    }

    attachEventListeners() {
        const searchInput = document.getElementById('func-search');
        if (searchInput) {
            let debounceTimer;
            searchInput.addEventListener('input', (e) => {
                clearTimeout(debounceTimer);
                debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => this.searchFunctions(e.target.value), 300);
            });
        }

        const refactorType = document.getElementById('refactor-type');
        if (refactorType) {
            refactorType.addEventListener('change', (e) => this.showRefactorParams(e.target.value));
        }

        const analyzeBtn = document.getElementById('analyze-impact');
        if (analyzeBtn) {
            analyzeBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.analyzeImpact());
        }

        const generateBtn = document.getElementById('generate-plan');
        if (generateBtn) {
            generateBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.generatePlan());
        }

        const closeBtn = document.querySelector('.close-panel');
        if (closeBtn) {
            closeBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                document.querySelector('.refactoring-panel').style.display = 'none';
            });
        }
    }

    async searchFunctions(query) {
        if (!query || query.length < 2) {
            document.getElementById('search-results').style.display = 'none';
            return;
        }

        const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/search/functions?query=${encodeURIComponent(query)}&limit=10`);
        const data = await response.json();

        const resultsDiv = document.getElementById('search-results');
        if (data.functions && data.functions.length > 0) {
            resultsDiv.innerHTML = data.functions.map(f => `
                <div class="search-result" data-name="${f.name}" data-file="${f.file}" data-type="${f.type}">
                    <strong>${f.name}</strong>
                    <small>${f.type} · ${f.file.split('/').pop()}</small>
                </div>
            `).join('');
            resultsDiv.style.display = 'block';

            document.querySelectorAll('.search-result').forEach(el => {
                el.addEventListener('click', () => this.selectFunction(el.dataset.name));
            });
        } else {
            resultsDiv.innerHTML = '<div class="no-results">No functions found</div>';
            resultsDiv.style.display = 'block';
        }
    }

    async selectFunction(functionName) {
        this.selectedFunction = functionName;
        document.getElementById('func-search').value = functionName;
        document.getElementById('search-results').style.display = 'none';

        const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/analyze/function/${encodeURIComponent(functionName)}`);
        this.currentFunction = await response.json();

        document.getElementById('function-info').style.display = 'block';
        document.getElementById('func-name').textContent = this.currentFunction.name;
        document.getElementById('func-location').textContent = `${this.currentFunction.file_path.split('/').pop()}:${this.currentFunction.line_start}-${this.currentFunction.line_end}`;
        document.getElementById('caller-count').textContent = `${this.currentFunction.caller_count} caller${this.currentFunction.caller_count !== 1 ? 's' : ''}`;
        document.getElementById('param-count').textContent = `${this.currentFunction.parameters.length} parameter${this.currentFunction.parameters.length !== 1 ? 's' : ''}`;
    }

    showRefactorParams(refactorType) {
        const paramsDiv = document.getElementById('refactor-params');
        if (!refactorType) {
            paramsDiv.style.display = 'none';
            return;
        }

        let html = '';
        switch (refactorType) {
            case 'add_parameter':
                html = `
                    <h4>Add Parameter</h4>
                    <input type="text" id="param-name" placeholder="Parameter name" required>
                    <input type="text" id="param-type" placeholder="Type hint (optional)">
                    <input type="text" id="param-default" placeholder="Default value (optional)">
                    <label><input type="checkbox" id="param-required"> Required (no default)</label>
                `;
                break;
            case 'remove_parameter':
                if (this.currentFunction?.parameters) {
                    html = `
                        <h4>Remove Parameter</h4>
                        <select id="remove-param">
                            <option value="">Select parameter to remove...</option>
                            ${this.currentFunction.parameters.map(p => `<option value="${p.name}">${p.name}</option>`).join('')}
                        </select>
                    `;
                }
                break;
            case 'rename_function':
                html = `
                    <h4>Rename Function</h4>
                    <input type="text" id="new-name" placeholder="New function name" required>
                `;
                break;
            case 'extract_method':
                html = `
                    <h4>Extract Method</h4>
                    <input type="number" id="start-line" placeholder="Start line number" required>
                    <input type="number" id="end-line" placeholder="End line number" required>
                    <input type="text" id="new-method-name" placeholder="New method name" required>
                    <small class="warning">⚠️ This uses AI and requires careful review</small>
                `;
                break;
            case 'inline_function':
                html = `
                    <h4>Inline Function</h4>
                    <small class="warning">⚠️ This will replace all calls with function body. High complexity.</small>
                `;
                break;
        }

        paramsDiv.innerHTML = html;
        paramsDiv.style.display = 'block';
    }

    async analyzeImpact() {
        const refactorType = document.getElementById('refactor-type').value;
        if (!this.selectedFunction || !refactorType) {
            alert('Please select a function and refactoring type');
            return;
        }

        let endpoint = '';
        let payload = { function_name: this.selectedFunction };

        switch (refactorType) {
            case 'add_parameter':
                endpoint = '/impact/add-parameter';
                payload.new_parameter = {
                    name: document.getElementById('param-name').value,
                    type_hint: document.getElementById('param-type').value || null,
                    default_value: document.getElementById('param-default').value || null,
                    is_required: document.getElementById('param-required').checked
                };
                payload.default_value = document.getElementById('param-default').value || null;
                break;
            case 'remove_parameter':
                endpoint = '/impact/remove-parameter';
                payload.parameter_name = document.getElementById('remove-param').value;
                break;
            case 'rename_function':
                endpoint = '/impact/rename-function';
                payload.new_name = document.getElementById('new-name').value;
                break;
            default:
                alert('Impact analysis not available for this refactoring type yet');
                return;
        }

        const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}${endpoint}`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify(payload)
        });

        const impact = await response.json();

        const impactDiv = document.getElementById('impact-analysis');
        impactDiv.innerHTML = `
            <h4>Impact Analysis</h4>
            <div class="impact-level impact-${impact.impact_level}">
                Level: ${impact.impact_level.toUpperCase()}
            </div>
            <div class="impact-stats">
                <div>📁 Affected Files: ${impact.affected_files.length}</div>
                <div>📞 Total Callers: ${impact.total_callers}</div>
                <div>⚠️ Breaking Changes: ${impact.breaking_changes ? 'Yes' : 'No'}</div>
                <div>📊 Complexity Score: ${(impact.complexity_score * 100).toFixed(0)}%</div>
            </div>
            <div class="impact-warnings">
                ${impact.warnings.map(w => `<div class="warning">⚠️ ${w}</div>`).join('')}
            </div>
            <div class="impact-suggestions">
                ${impact.suggestions.map(s => `<div class="suggestion">💡 ${s}</div>`).join('')}
            </div>
        `;
        impactDiv.style.display = 'block';
    }

    async generatePlan() {
        const refactorType = document.getElementById('refactor-type').value;
        if (!this.selectedFunction || !refactorType) {
            alert('Please select a function and refactoring type');
            return;
        }

        let endpoint = '';
        let payload = { function_name: this.selectedFunction };

        switch (refactorType) {
            case 'add_parameter':
                endpoint = '/plan/add-parameter';
                payload.new_parameter = {
                    name: document.getElementById('param-name').value,
                    type_hint: document.getElementById('param-type').value || null,
                    default_value: document.getElementById('param-default').value || null,
                    is_required: document.getElementById('param-required').checked
                };
                payload.default_value = document.getElementById('param-default').value || null;
                break;
            case 'remove_parameter':
                endpoint = '/plan/remove-parameter';
                payload.parameter_name = document.getElementById('remove-param').value;
                break;
            case 'rename_function':
                endpoint = '/plan/rename-function';
                payload.new_name = document.getElementById('new-name').value;
                break;
            case 'extract_method':
                endpoint = '/plan/extract-method';
                payload.start_line = parseInt(document.getElementById('start-line').value);
                payload.end_line = parseInt(document.getElementById('end-line').value);
                payload.new_method_name = document.getElementById('new-method-name').value;
                break;
            case 'inline_function':
                endpoint = '/plan/inline-function';
                break;
            default:
                alert('Plan generation not available for this refactoring type');
                return;
        }

        const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}${endpoint}`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify(payload)
        });

        this.currentPlan = await response.json();

        const previewDiv = document.getElementById('plan-preview');
        previewDiv.innerHTML = `
            <h4>Refactoring Plan</h4>
            <div class="plan-meta">
                <div>🎯 Target: ${this.currentPlan.target_function}</div>
                <div>📝 Type: ${this.currentPlan.refactor_type}</div>
                <div>🎯 Confidence: ${(this.currentPlan.confidence * 100).toFixed(0)}%</div>
                <div>${this.currentPlan.requires_review ? '⚠️ Requires Review' : '✅ Auto-approved'}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="changes-list">
                <h5>Changes (${this.currentPlan.changes.length} files):</h5>
                ${this.currentPlan.changes.map((change, idx) => `
                    <div class="change-item">
                        <div class="change-header">
                            <strong>📄 ${change.file_path.split('/').pop()}</strong>
                            <span class="change-type">${change.change_type}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="change-description">${change.description}</div>
                        <div class="diff-view">
                            <div class="diff-before">- ${change.before.split('\n')[0].substring(0, 100)}...</div>
                            <div class="diff-after">+ ${change.after.split('\n')[0].substring(0, 100)}...</div>
                        </div>
                        <button class="copy-change" data-before="${this.escapeHtml(change.before)}" data-after="${this.escapeHtml(change.after)}">
                            📋 Copy to Clipboard
                        </button>
                    </div>
                `).join('')}
            </div>
        `;
        previewDiv.style.display = 'block';

        document.querySelectorAll('.copy-change').forEach(btn => {
            btn.addEventListener('click', () => this.copyChange(btn.dataset));
        });
    }

    async copyChange(data) {
        const text = `# BEFORE:\n${this.unescapeHtml(data.before)}\n\n# AFTER:\n${this.unescapeHtml(data.after)}`;
        await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
        
        event.target.textContent = '✅ Copied!';
        setTimeout(() => {
            event.target.textContent = '📋 Copy to Clipboard';
        }, 2000);
    }

    escapeHtml(str) {
        return str.replace(/[&<>]/g, function(m) {
            if (m === '&') return '&amp;';
            if (m === '<') return '&lt;';
            if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
            return m;
        });
    }

    unescapeHtml(str) {
        return str.replace(/&amp;/g, '&').replace(/&lt;/g, '<').replace(/&gt;/g, '>');
    }
}

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    window.refactoringAgent = new RefactoringAgent();
});

# ========================================
# FILE: .\frontend\static\js\task_board.js
# ========================================

// API Base URL
const API_BASE = '/api/task-board';

// State
let allTasks = [];
let currentTaskId = null;

// Wait for DOM to be fully loaded
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    initializeElements();
    attachEventListeners();
    loadTasks();
    loadStats();
    loadProjectBadge();
});

// Initialize DOM element references
let taskListEl, statusFilter, priorityFilter, categoryFilter, sourceFilter, searchFilter;
let generateBtn, refreshBtn, modal, modalTitle, modalBody, closeModal;
let settingsBtn, settingsModal, closeSettings, cancelSettingsBtn, saveSettingsBtn, generateAIBtn;
let modalMarkPending, modalMarkProgress, modalMarkDone, modalMarkIgnored, modalMarkDeferred, modalGetExplanation;

function initializeElements() {
    taskListEl = document.getElementById('taskList');
    statusFilter = document.getElementById('statusFilter');
    priorityFilter = document.getElementById('priorityFilter');
    categoryFilter = document.getElementById('categoryFilter');
    sourceFilter = document.getElementById('sourceFilter');
    searchFilter = document.getElementById('searchFilter');
    generateBtn = document.getElementById('generateTasksBtn');
    refreshBtn = document.getElementById('refreshTasksBtn');
    modal = document.getElementById('taskModal');
    modalTitle = document.getElementById('modalTitle');
    modalBody = document.getElementById('modalBody');
    closeModal = document.querySelector('.close');
    settingsBtn = document.getElementById('settingsBtnHeader') || document.getElementById('settingsBtn');
    settingsModal = document.getElementById('settingsModal');
    closeSettings = document.querySelector('.close-settings');
    cancelSettingsBtn = document.getElementById('cancelSettingsBtn');
    saveSettingsBtn = document.getElementById('saveSettingsBtn');
    generateAIBtn = document.getElementById('generateAIBtn');
    modalMarkPending = document.getElementById('modalMarkPending');
    modalMarkProgress = document.getElementById('modalMarkProgress');
    modalMarkDone = document.getElementById('modalMarkDone');
    modalMarkIgnored = document.getElementById('modalMarkIgnored');
    modalMarkDeferred = document.getElementById('modalMarkDeferred');
    modalGetExplanation = document.getElementById('modalGetExplanation');
    aiRefactorBtn = document.getElementById('aiRefactorBtn');
    aiRefactorModal = document.getElementById('aiRefactorModal');
    closeAiModal = document.querySelector('.close-ai-modal');
    closeAiModalBtn = document.getElementById('closeAiModalBtn');
}

function attachEventListeners() {
    if (statusFilter) statusFilter.addEventListener('change', filterTasks);
    if (priorityFilter) priorityFilter.addEventListener('change', filterTasks);
    if (categoryFilter) categoryFilter.addEventListener('change', filterTasks);
    if (sourceFilter) sourceFilter.addEventListener('change', filterTasks);
    if (searchFilter) searchFilter.addEventListener('input', filterTasks);

    if (generateBtn) generateBtn.addEventListener('click', generateTasks);
    if (refreshBtn) refreshBtn.addEventListener('click', () => { loadTasks(); loadStats(); });
    if (closeModal) closeModal.addEventListener('click', () => { if (modal) modal.style.display = 'none'; });
    if (generateAIBtn) generateAIBtn.addEventListener('click', generateAITasks);

    if (settingsBtn) settingsBtn.addEventListener('click', openSettingsModal);
    if (closeSettings) closeSettings.addEventListener('click', () => { if (settingsModal) settingsModal.style.display = 'none'; });
    if (cancelSettingsBtn) cancelSettingsBtn.addEventListener('click', () => { if (settingsModal) settingsModal.style.display = 'none'; });
    if (saveSettingsBtn) saveSettingsBtn.addEventListener('click', saveSettings);

    if (modalMarkPending) modalMarkPending.addEventListener('click', () => updateTaskStatus('pending'));
    if (modalMarkProgress) modalMarkProgress.addEventListener('click', () => updateTaskStatus('in_progress'));
    if (modalMarkDone) modalMarkDone.addEventListener('click', () => updateTaskStatus('done'));
    if (modalMarkIgnored) modalMarkIgnored.addEventListener('click', () => updateTaskStatus('ignored'));
    if (modalMarkDeferred) modalMarkDeferred.addEventListener('click', () => updateTaskStatus('deferred'));
    if (modalGetExplanation) modalGetExplanation.addEventListener('click', getExplanation);

    if (aiRefactorBtn) {
        aiRefactorBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            if (aiRefactorModal) aiRefactorModal.style.display = 'block';
        });
    }

    if (closeAiModal) {
        closeAiModal.addEventListener('click', () => {
            if (aiRefactorModal) aiRefactorModal.style.display = 'none';
        });
    }

    if (closeAiModalBtn) {
        closeAiModalBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            if (aiRefactorModal) aiRefactorModal.style.display = 'none';
        });
    }

    window.addEventListener('click', (e) => { if (modal && e.target === modal) modal.style.display = 'none'; });
}

async function loadProjectBadge() {
    const badge = document.getElementById('projectBadge');
    if (!badge) return;

    try {
        const response = await fetch('/projects/');
        const projects = await response.json();
        const activeProject = projects.find(p => p.active === true);
        if (activeProject) {
            badge.textContent = `📁 ${activeProject.project_id}`;
        } else {
            badge.textContent = 'No active project';
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error loading project:', error);
        badge.textContent = 'Error loading project';
    }
}

async function loadTasks() {
    if (!taskListEl) return;

    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/tasks`);
        allTasks = await response.json();
        filterTasks();
        updateRuleBasedBadge();
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error loading tasks:', error);
        taskListEl.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">Error loading tasks. Make sure server is running.</div>';
    }
}

function updateRuleBasedBadge() {
    const badge = document.getElementById('ruleBasedCount');
    if (badge && allTasks) {
        badge.textContent = allTasks.length;
    }
}

async function loadStats() {
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/summary`);
        const stats = await response.json();

        const totalTasksEl = document.getElementById('totalTasks');
        const criticalTasksEl = document.getElementById('criticalTasks');
        const highTasksEl = document.getElementById('highTasks');
        const mediumTasksEl = document.getElementById('mediumTasks');
        const pendingTasksEl = document.getElementById('pendingTasks');
        const inProgressTasksEl = document.getElementById('inProgressTasks');
        const doneTasksEl = document.getElementById('doneTasks');

        if (totalTasksEl) totalTasksEl.textContent = stats.total_tasks || 0;
        if (criticalTasksEl) criticalTasksEl.textContent = stats.by_priority?.critical || 0;
        if (highTasksEl) highTasksEl.textContent = stats.by_priority?.high || 0;
        if (mediumTasksEl) mediumTasksEl.textContent = stats.by_priority?.medium || 0;
        if (pendingTasksEl) pendingTasksEl.textContent = stats.by_status?.pending || 0;
        if (inProgressTasksEl) inProgressTasksEl.textContent = stats.by_status?.in_progress || 0;
        if (doneTasksEl) doneTasksEl.textContent = stats.by_status?.done || 0;
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error loading stats:', error);
    }
}

function filterTasks() {
    if (!allTasks) return;

    const status = statusFilter ? statusFilter.value : 'all';
    const priority = priorityFilter ? priorityFilter.value : 'all';
    const category = categoryFilter ? categoryFilter.value : 'all';
    const source = sourceFilter ? sourceFilter.value : 'all';
    const search = searchFilter ? searchFilter.value.toLowerCase() : '';

    let filtered = [...allTasks];

    if (status !== 'all') {
        filtered = filtered.filter(t => t.status === status);
    }
    if (priority !== 'all') {
        filtered = filtered.filter(t => t.priority === priority);
    }
    if (category !== 'all') {
        filtered = filtered.filter(t => t.category === category);
    }
    if (source !== 'all') {
        filtered = filtered.filter(t => t.evidence?.[0]?.source === source);
    }
    if (search) {
        filtered = filtered.filter(t => t.title.toLowerCase().includes(search));
    }

    renderTasks(filtered);
}

function renderTasks(tasks) {
    if (!taskListEl) return;

    if (tasks.length === 0) {
        taskListEl.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">No tasks found. Click "Generate Rule-Based Tasks" to create tasks from code analysis.</div>';
        return;
    }

    taskListEl.innerHTML = tasks.map(task => {
        const source = task.evidence?.[0]?.source || 'rule_based';
        const sourceIcon = source === 'llm' ? '🤖' : '📊';
        const sourceLabel = source === 'llm' ? 'AI-Discovered' : 'Rule-Based';

        return `
        <div class="task-card ${task.priority}" onclick="window.openTaskModal('${task.id}')">
            <div class="task-header">
                <span class="task-title">${escapeHtml(task.title)}</span>
                <div style="display: flex; gap: 5px; flex-wrap: wrap;">
                    <span class="task-badge ${task.priority}">${task.priority.toUpperCase()}</span>
                    <span class="task-badge ${task.status}">${task.status.replace('_', ' ')}</span>
                    <span class="task-badge source-badge ${source}">${sourceIcon} ${sourceLabel}</span>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="task-description">${escapeHtml(task.description.substring(0, 150))}${task.description.length > 150 ? '...' : ''}</div>
            <div class="task-meta">
                <span>📁 ${task.category}</span>
                <span>📊 ${task.evidence?.[0]?.metric_type || 'N/A'}: ${task.evidence?.[0]?.metric_value || 0}</span>
            </div>
        </div>
    `}).join('');
}

window.openTaskModal = async function (taskId) {
    currentTaskId = taskId;

    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/tasks/${taskId}`);
        const task = await response.json();

        if (modalTitle) modalTitle.textContent = task.title;

        const evidence = task.evidence?.[0] || {};
        const evidenceHtml = `
            <div class="evidence-block">
                <strong>Evidence:</strong><br>
                Symbol: ${escapeHtml(evidence.symbol || 'N/A')}<br>
                Metric: ${evidence.metric_type || 'N/A'} = ${evidence.metric_value || 0}<br>
                File: ${escapeHtml(evidence.file_path || 'N/A')}
                ${evidence.callers?.length ? `<br>Callers (first 5): ${evidence.callers.slice(0, 5).join(', ')}` : ''}
                ${evidence.callees?.length ? `<br>Callees (first 5): ${evidence.callees.slice(0, 5).join(', ')}` : ''}
            </div>
        `;

        const suggestedFixHtml = task.suggested_fix ? `
            <div class="suggested-fix">
                <strong>💡 Suggested Fix:</strong><br>
                ${escapeHtml(task.suggested_fix)}
            </div>
        ` : '';

        const impactHtml = task.impact_analysis ? `
            <div class="impact-analysis">
                <strong>🤖 AI Impact Analysis:</strong><br>
                ${escapeHtml(task.impact_analysis)}
            </div>
        ` : '';

        if (modalBody) {
            modalBody.innerHTML = `
                <p><strong>Description:</strong></p>
                <p>${escapeHtml(task.description)}</p>
                ${evidenceHtml}
                ${suggestedFixHtml}
                ${impactHtml}
            `;
        }

        if (modal) modal.style.display = 'block';
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error loading task details:', error);
        alert('Error loading task details');
    }
};

async function updateTaskStatus(status) {
    if (!currentTaskId) return;

    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/tasks/${currentTaskId}`, {
            method: 'PATCH',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ status: status })
        });

        if (response.ok) {
            if (modal) modal.style.display = 'none';
            loadTasks();
            loadStats();
        } else {
            alert('Error updating task status');
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error updating task:', error);
        alert('Error updating task');
    }
}

async function getExplanation() {
    if (!currentTaskId) return;

    const explanationBtn = document.getElementById('modalGetExplanation');
    if (!explanationBtn) return;

    const originalText = explanationBtn.textContent;
    explanationBtn.textContent = '⏳ Generating...';
    explanationBtn.disabled = true;

    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/tasks/${currentTaskId}/explanation`);
        const data = await response.json();

        const impactDiv = document.createElement('div');
        impactDiv.className = 'impact-analysis';
        impactDiv.innerHTML = `<strong>🤖 AI Impact Analysis:</strong><br>${escapeHtml(data.impact_analysis)}`;

        const existingImpact = modalBody?.querySelector('.impact-analysis');
        if (existingImpact) existingImpact.remove();
        if (modalBody) modalBody.appendChild(impactDiv);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error getting explanation:', error);
        alert('Error generating AI explanation');
    } finally {
        explanationBtn.textContent = originalText;
        explanationBtn.disabled = false;
    }
}

async function generateTasks() {
    if (!generateBtn) return;

    generateBtn.disabled = true;
    generateBtn.textContent = '⏳ Starting generation...';

    let includeLlm = true;
    try {
        const configResponse = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/config`);
        const config = await configResponse.json();
        includeLlm = config.llm_enabled;
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('Error checking LLM config:', e);
    }

    try {
        const startResponse = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/tasks/generate-async?include_llm=${includeLlm}`, {
            method: 'POST'
        });
        const startResult = await startResponse.json();

        const jobId = startResult.job_id;
        generateBtn.textContent = '⏳ Generating tasks (this may take a few minutes)...';

        let completed = false;
        let pollCount = 0;
        const maxPolls = 120;

        while (!completed && pollCount < maxPolls) {
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));

            const statusResponse = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/tasks/generate-status/${jobId}`);
            const status = await statusResponse.json();

            if (status.status === 'completed') {
                completed = true;
                alert(`Task generation complete!\nRule-based: ${status.result.rule_based_tasks}\nAI-discovered: ${status.result.llm_discovered_tasks}`);
                loadTasks();
                loadStats();
            } else if (status.status === 'failed') {
                completed = true;
                alert(`Task generation failed: ${status.error}`);
            }

            pollCount++;
        }

        if (!completed) {
            alert('Task generation is taking longer than expected. Check back later.');
        }

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error generating tasks:', error);
        alert('Error starting task generation');
    } finally {
        generateBtn.disabled = false;
        generateBtn.textContent = '🔄 Generate Rule-Based Tasks';
    }
}

function escapeHtml(text) {
    if (!text) return '';
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    div.textContent = text;
    return div.innerHTML;
}

async function openSettingsModal() {
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/config`);
        const config = await response.json();

        const fanOutMedium = document.getElementById('fanOutMedium');
        const fanOutHigh = document.getElementById('fanOutHigh');
        const fanOutCritical = document.getElementById('fanOutCritical');
        const fanInMedium = document.getElementById('fanInMedium');
        const fanInHigh = document.getElementById('fanInHigh');
        const fanInCritical = document.getElementById('fanInCritical');
        const llmEnabled = document.getElementById('llmEnabled');
        const llmMaxTasks = document.getElementById('llmMaxTasks');

        if (fanOutMedium) fanOutMedium.value = config.fan_out_medium;
        if (fanOutHigh) fanOutHigh.value = config.fan_out_high;
        if (fanOutCritical) fanOutCritical.value = config.fan_out_critical;
        if (fanInMedium) fanInMedium.value = config.fan_in_medium;
        if (fanInHigh) fanInHigh.value = config.fan_in_high;
        if (fanInCritical) fanInCritical.value = config.fan_in_critical;
        if (llmEnabled) llmEnabled.checked = config.llm_enabled;
        if (llmMaxTasks) llmMaxTasks.value = config.llm_max_tasks;

        if (settingsModal) settingsModal.style.display = 'block';
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error loading config:', error);
        alert('Error loading settings');
    }
}

async function saveSettings() {
    const config = {
        fan_out_medium: parseInt(document.getElementById('fanOutMedium')?.value || 5),
        fan_out_high: parseInt(document.getElementById('fanOutHigh')?.value || 10),
        fan_out_critical: parseInt(document.getElementById('fanOutCritical')?.value || 20),
        fan_in_medium: parseInt(document.getElementById('fanInMedium')?.value || 5),
        fan_in_high: parseInt(document.getElementById('fanInHigh')?.value || 10),
        fan_in_critical: parseInt(document.getElementById('fanInCritical')?.value || 20),
        llm_enabled: document.getElementById('llmEnabled')?.checked || false,
        llm_max_tasks: parseInt(document.getElementById('llmMaxTasks')?.value || 10)
    };

    try {
        await fetch(`${API_BASE}/config`, {
            method: 'PUT',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify(config)
        });

        if (generateBtn) {
            generateBtn.disabled = true;
            generateBtn.textContent = '⏳ Regenerating...';
        }

        const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/tasks/generate-with-config?include_llm=${config.llm_enabled}`, {
            method: 'POST'
        });

        const result = await response.json();

        if (settingsModal) settingsModal.style.display = 'none';
        alert(`Settings saved! ${result.message}\nRule-based: ${result.rule_based_tasks}\nAI-discovered: ${result.llm_discovered_tasks}`);

        loadTasks();
        loadStats();

        if (generateBtn) {
            generateBtn.disabled = false;
            generateBtn.textContent = '🔄 Generate Rule-Based Tasks';
        }

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error saving settings:', error);
        alert('Error saving settings');
    }
}

async function generateAITasks() {
    if (!generateAIBtn) return;

    generateAIBtn.disabled = true;
    generateAIBtn.textContent = '🤖 Starting AI generation...';

    try {
        const startResponse = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/tasks/generate-ai-only-async`, {
            method: 'POST'
        });
        const startResult = await startResponse.json();

        const jobId = startResult.job_id;
        generateAIBtn.textContent = '🤖 AI generating tasks (may take a few minutes)...';

        let completed = false;
        let pollCount = 0;
        const maxPolls = 120;

        while (!completed && pollCount < maxPolls) {
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));

            const statusResponse = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/tasks/generate-status/${jobId}`);
            const status = await statusResponse.json();

            if (status.status === 'completed') {
                completed = true;
                alert(`AI task generation complete!\nAdded ${status.result.ai_tasks_added} new AI-discovered tasks\nTotal tasks: ${status.result.total_tasks}`);
                loadTasks();
                loadStats();
                if (sourceFilter) sourceFilter.value = 'llm';
                filterTasks();
            } else if (status.status === 'failed') {
                completed = true;
                alert(`AI task generation failed: ${status.error}`);
            }

            pollCount++;
        }

        if (!completed) {
            alert('AI task generation is taking longer than expected. Check back later.');
        }

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error generating AI tasks:', error);
        alert('Error starting AI task generation');
    } finally {
        generateAIBtn.disabled = false;
        generateAIBtn.textContent = '🤖 Generate AI Tasks Only';
    }
}

# ========================================
# FILE: .\frontend\templates\graph.html
# ========================================

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>

<head>
    <title>Code Graph</title>
    <script src="https://d3js.org/d3.v7.min.js"></script>

    <style>
        body {
            margin: 0;
            font-family: Arial;
        }

        svg {
            width: 100vw;
            height: 100vh;
            background: #0f172a;
        }

        .node circle {
            fill: #4CAF50;
            stroke: white;
            stroke-width: 1.5px;
        }

        .node text {
            fill: white;
            font-size: 12px;
            pointer-events: none;
        }

        .link {
            stroke: #94a3b8;
            stroke-opacity: 0.6;
        }
    </style>
</head>

<body>

    <div style="
    position: absolute;
    top: 10px;
    left: 10px;
    z-index: 10;
">
        <input id="searchBox" placeholder="Search function/class..." style="padding:8px; width:250px;" />
    </div>

    <svg></svg>

    <script>
        let node, link;
        async function loadGraph() {
            const res = await fetch('/graph/data');
            const data = await res.json();

            const nodesMap = {};
            const links = [];

            // build nodes + links
            for (const [source, targets] of Object.entries(data.calls)) {
                nodesMap[source] = true;

                for (const t of targets) {
                    nodesMap[t] = true;
                    links.push({ source, target: t });
                }
            }

            const nodes = Object.keys(nodesMap).map(id => ({ id }));

            const svg = d3.select("svg");
            const width = window.innerWidth;
            const height = window.innerHeight;

            const simulation = d3.forceSimulation(nodes)
                .force("link", d3.forceLink(links).id(d => d.id).distance(80))
                .force("charge", d3.forceManyBody().strength(-200))
                .force("center", d3.forceCenter(width / 2, height / 2));


            link = svg.append("g")
                .selectAll("line")
                .data(links)
                .enter()
                .append("line")
                .attr("class", "link");

            node = svg.append("g")
                .selectAll("g")
                .data(nodes)
                .enter()
                .append("g")
                .attr("class", "node")
                .call(d3.drag()
                    .on("start", dragstarted)
                    .on("drag", dragged)
                    .on("end", dragended)
                );

            node.append("circle")
                .attr("r", 8)
                .on("click", (event, d) => {
                    alert(d.id);
                });

            node.append("text")
                .attr("x", 10)
                .attr("y", 3)
                .text(d => d.id);

            simulation.on("tick", () => {
                link
                    .attr("x1", d => d.source.x)
                    .attr("y1", d => d.source.y)
                    .attr("x2", d => d.target.x)
                    .attr("y2", d => d.target.y);

                node.attr("transform", d => `translate(${d.x},${d.y})`);
            });

            function dragstarted(event, d) {
                if (!event.active) simulation.alphaTarget(0.3).restart();
                d.fx = d.x;
                d.fy = d.y;
            }

            function dragged(event, d) {
                d.fx = event.x;
                d.fy = event.y;
            }

            function dragended(event, d) {
                if (!event.active) simulation.alphaTarget(0);
                d.fx = null;
                d.fy = null;
            }
        }

        loadGraph();
        document.getElementById("searchBox").addEventListener("input", function (e) {
            const value = e.target.value.trim().toLowerCase();

            node.style("opacity", d => {
                if (!value) return 1;
                return d.id.toLowerCase().includes(value) ? 1 : 0.1;
            });

            link.style("opacity", d => {
                if (!value) return 1;
                return (
                    d.source.id.toLowerCase().includes(value) ||
                    d.target.id.toLowerCase().includes(value)
                ) ? 1 : 0.05;
            });
        });
    </script>

</body>

</html>

<div class="chat-wrapper">
    <div id="chat-container" class="chat-container">
        <div class="message ai-message"><strong>Agent:</strong> Standing by to troubleshoot IDM Crawler source routines. Provide a query or class/method reference symbol.</div>
    </div>

    <div class="input-area">
        <input type="text" id="symbol-input" style="max-width: 150px;" placeholder="Symbol (Optional)" />
        <input type="text" id="user-input" placeholder="Ask a debugging question about your codebase..." />
        <button id="send-btn">Analyze</button>

<script>
    document.getElementById('send-btn').addEventListener('click', async () => {
        const inputEl = document.getElementById('user-input');
        const symbolEl = document.getElementById('symbol-input');
        const sendBtn = document.getElementById('send-btn');
        const chatContainer = document.getElementById('chat-container');

        const question = inputEl.value.trim();
        const symbol = symbolEl.value.trim();

        if (!question) return;

        // Render user question to UI
        chatContainer.innerHTML += `<div class="message user-message"><strong>You:</strong> ${question} ${symbol ? `(Symbol: ${symbol})` : ''}</div>`;
        
        // Reset and lock elements during active execution
        inputEl.value = '';
        sendBtn.disabled = true;
        chatContainer.scrollTop = chatContainer.scrollHeight;

        // Build container block for real-time string token parsing
        const aiBubble = document.createElement('div');
        aiBubble.className = 'message ai-message';
        aiBubble.innerHTML = '<strong>Agent:</strong> <span class="content"></span>';
        chatContainer.appendChild(aiBubble);
        const contentTarget = aiBubble.querySelector('.content');

        try {
            const params = new URLSearchParams({ question: question, symbol_name: symbol });
            const response = await fetch(`http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/agent/stream?${params.toString()}`);
            
            if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP network error state: ${response.status}`);

            const reader = response.body.getReader();
            const decoder = new TextDecoder('utf-8');

            while (true) {
                const { value, done } = await reader.read();
                if (done) break;

                const token = decoder.decode(value, { stream: true });
                contentTarget.textContent += token;
                chatContainer.scrollTop = chatContainer.scrollHeight;
            }
        } catch (error) {
            contentTarget.textContent = `[Streaming Pipeline Execution Failure: ${error.message}]`;
        }

        sendBtn.disabled = false;
        inputEl.focus();
    });
</script>

</body>
</html>

# FILE: .\scripts\build_call_graph.py
# ========================================

# scripts/build_call_graph.py

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Build call graph from indexed symbols.
Run: python scripts/build_call_graph.py [--project PROJECT_ID] [--force]
"""

import sys
import json
import argparse
from pathlib import Path
from collections import defaultdict

# Add project root to path
project_root = Path(__file__).parent.parent
sys.path.insert(0, str(project_root))

from backend.services.project_service import ProjectService
from backend.services.graph.call_graph_service import CallGraphService
from config import INDEX_DIR


def build_call_graph(project_id: str, force: bool = False):
    """Build call graph for a project"""
    print(f"\n🔨 Building Call Graph for Project: {project_id}")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    index_path = INDEX_DIR / project_id
    symbols_file = index_path / "symbols.json"
    call_graph_file = index_path / "call_graph.json"
    
    # Check if symbols exist
    if not symbols_file.exists():
        print(f"❌ symbols.json not found at {symbols_file}")
        print("   Please index the project first:")
        print(f"   python scripts/index_project.py --project {project_id}")
        return False
    
    # Check if we need to rebuild
    if call_graph_file.exists() and not force:
        print(f"⚠️  call_graph.json already exists")
        response = input("   Overwrite? (y/N): ")
        if response.lower() != 'y':
            print("   Skipping...")
            return True
    
    # Load symbols
    print(f"📖 Loading symbols from {symbols_file}...")
    with open(symbols_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        symbols = json.load(f)
    
    print(f"   Found {len(symbols)} symbols")
    
    # Build call graph
    print("🔗 Building call relationships...")
    calls = defaultdict(list)
    called_by = defaultdict(list)
    
    # Track statistics
    functions_with_calls = 0
    total_calls = 0
    
    for sym in symbols:
        sym_type = sym.get("type")
        if sym_type not in ["function", "method"]:
            continue
            
        func_name = sym.get("name")
        calls_list = sym.get("calls", [])
        
        if calls_list:
            functions_with_calls += 1
            total_calls += len(calls_list)
            
            for callee in calls_list:
                calls[func_name].append(callee)
                called_by[callee].append(func_name)
    
    # Convert to regular dict for JSON serialization
    call_graph = {
        "calls": dict(calls),
        "called_by": dict(called_by),
        "statistics": {
            "total_functions": functions_with_calls,
            "total_call_edges": total_calls,
            "functions_without_calls": len([s for s in symbols if s.get("type") in ["function", "method"]]) - functions_with_calls
        }
    }
    
    # Save call graph
    print(f"💾 Saving call graph to {call_graph_file}...")
    call_graph_file.write_text(
        json.dumps(call_graph, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False),
        encoding="utf-8"
    )
    
    # Display statistics
    print("\n📊 Call Graph Statistics:")
    print(f"   • Functions with calls: {call_graph['statistics']['total_functions']}")
    print(f"   • Total call edges: {call_graph['statistics']['total_call_edges']}")
    print(f"   • Functions without calls: {call_graph['statistics']['functions_without_calls']}")
    
    # Find functions with most callers (popular functions)
    if called_by:
        popular = sorted(called_by.items(), key=lambda x: len(x[1]), reverse=True)[:5]
        if popular:
            print("\n⭐ Most Called Functions (Top 5):")
            for func, callers in popular:
                print(f"   • {func}: called by {len(callers)} function(s)")
    
    # Find functions that call many others (busy functions)
    if calls:
        busy = sorted(calls.items(), key=lambda x: len(x[1]), reverse=True)[:5]
        if busy:
            print("\n🔧 Most Active Functions (Top 5):")
            for func, callees in busy:
                print(f"   • {func}: calls {len(callees)} function(s)")
    
    print("\n✅ Call graph built successfully!")
    
    # Invalidate cache in service
    try:
        service = CallGraphService(str(index_path))
        service.invalidate_cache()
        print("   Service cache invalidated")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   Note: Could not invalidate cache: {e}")
    
    return True


def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Build call graph from indexed symbols")
    parser.add_argument("--project", help="Project ID (uses active project if not specified)")
    parser.add_argument("--force", action="store_true", help="Force rebuild even if exists")
    
    args = parser.parse_args()
    
    # Get project ID
    project_id = args.project
    if not project_id:
        try:
            project_service = ProjectService()
            active_project = project_service.get_active_project()
            if not active_project:
                print("❌ No active project found and no project ID provided")
                print("   Please either:")
                print("   1. Set an active project: python scripts/manage_project.py --active <project_id>")
                print("   2. Provide project ID: python scripts/build_call_graph.py --project <project_id>")
                sys.exit(1)
            project_id = active_project["project_id"]
            print(f"📌 Using active project: {project_id}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"❌ Error getting active project: {e}")
            sys.exit(1)
    
    # Build call graph
    success = build_call_graph(project_id, args.force)
    
    if not success:
        sys.exit(1)
    
    # Optional: Show sample for a specific function
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("💡 Next Steps:")
    print("   1. Re-run impact scanner: python scripts/test_impact_scanner.py")
    print("   2. Check callers for run_crawl:")
    print(f"      python -c \"from backend.services.graph.call_graph_service import CallGraphService; from config import INDEX_DIR; cg = CallGraphService(str(INDEX_DIR / '{project_id}')); print(cg.get_dependents('run_crawl'))\"")
    print("=" * 60)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

# FILE: .\scripts\diagnose_impact_scanner.py

# scripts/diagnose_impact_scanner.py

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Diagnose why Impact Scanner isn't finding callers"""

import sys
from pathlib import Path

project_root = Path(__file__).parent.parent
sys.path.insert(0, str(project_root))

from backend.services.refactor.impact_scanner import ImpactScanner
from backend.services.graph.call_graph_service import CallGraphService
from backend.services.project_service import ProjectService
import json


def diagnose():
    print("🔍 Impact Scanner Diagnostic Tool")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # Get project
    project_service = ProjectService()
    active_project = project_service.get_active_project()
    
    if not active_project:
        print("❌ No active project found")
        return
    
    project_id = active_project["project_id"]
    print(f"\n✅ Project ID: {project_id}")
    
    # Check index directory
    from config import INDEX_DIR
    index_path = INDEX_DIR / project_id
    print(f"\n📁 Index Path: {index_path}")
    print(f"   Exists: {index_path.exists()}")
    
    # Check symbols.json
    symbols_file = index_path / "symbols.json"
    print(f"\n📄 symbols.json: {symbols_file}")
    print(f"   Exists: {symbols_file.exists()}")
    
    if symbols_file.exists():
        with open(symbols_file, 'r') as f:
            symbols = json.load(f)
        print(f"   Functions count: {len([s for s in symbols if s.get('type') in ['function', 'method']])}")
        
        # Find run_crawl
        run_crawl = None
        for sym in symbols:
            if sym.get('name') == 'run_crawl':
                run_crawl = sym
                break
        
        if run_crawl:
            print(f"\n🎯 Found 'run_crawl':")
            print(f"   File: {run_crawl.get('file')}")
            print(f"   Lines: {run_crawl.get('start_line')}-{run_crawl.get('end_line')}")
            print(f"   Type: {run_crawl.get('type')}")
            print(f"   Parent: {run_crawl.get('parent', 'None')}")
        else:
            print(f"\n❌ 'run_crawl' not found in symbols.json")
            print("   Available functions (first 10):")
            for sym in symbols[:10]:
                if sym.get('type') in ['function', 'method']:
                    print(f"     - {sym.get('name')} ({sym.get('file', 'unknown')})")
    
    # Check call_graph.json
    call_graph_file = index_path / "call_graph.json"
    print(f"\n📊 call_graph.json: {call_graph_file}")
    print(f"   Exists: {call_graph_file.exists()}")
    
    if call_graph_file.exists():
        with open(call_graph_file, 'r') as f:
            call_graph = json.load(f)
        
        called_by = call_graph.get('called_by', {})
        print(f"   Functions in call graph: {len(called_by)}")
        
        # Check callers for run_crawl
        if 'run_crawl' in called_by:
            callers = called_by['run_crawl']
            print(f"\n📞 'run_crawl' callers: {len(callers)}")
            for caller in callers[:5]:
                print(f"     - {caller}")
        else:
            print(f"\n⚠️  'run_crawl' has no recorded callers in call graph")
            print("   This could mean:")
            print("     1. The function is never called")
            print("     2. Call graph wasn't built with -r (recursive) flag")
            print("     3. The function is called from outside the project")
    
    # Test CodeAnalyzer directly
    print(f"\n🔧 Testing CodeAnalyzer directly...")
    from backend.services.refactor.code_analyzer import CodeAnalyzer
    
    analyzer = CodeAnalyzer(project_id)
    func_detail = analyzer.get_function_detail('run_crawl')
    
    if func_detail:
        print(f"✅ Function found:")
        print(f"   Name: {func_detail.name}")
        print(f"   File: {func_detail.file_path}")
        print(f"   Parameters: {len(func_detail.parameters)}")
        print(f"   Callers from analyzer: {len(func_detail.callers)}")
        
        if func_detail.callers:
            print("   Callers:")
            for caller in func_detail.callers[:5]:
                print(f"     - {caller.calling_function} ({caller.file_path}:{caller.line_number})")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Function 'run_crawl' not found by CodeAnalyzer")
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("Recommendations:")
    
    if symbols_file.exists() and not call_graph_file.exists():
        print("  • Build call graph: python scripts/build_call_graph.py")
    elif call_graph_file.exists() and 'run_crawl' not in called_by:
        print("  • Rebuild call graph with recursive analysis")
        print("  • Check if run_crawl is actually called anywhere")
    elif not symbols_file.exists():
        print("  • Index your project first: python scripts/index_project.py")
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    diagnose()

# Quick test script to verify call graph
# scripts/test_call_graph.py

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Test call graph functionality"""

import sys
from pathlib import Path

project_root = Path(__file__).parent.parent
sys.path.insert(0, str(project_root))

from backend.services.graph.call_graph_service import CallGraphService
from config import INDEX_DIR
from backend.services.project_service import ProjectService

# Get project
project_service = ProjectService()
active_project = project_service.get_active_project()
project_id = active_project["project_id"]

# Initialize service
index_path = INDEX_DIR / project_id
cg_service = CallGraphService(str(index_path))

# Build graph
graph = cg_service.build_graph()

print(f"\n📊 Call Graph for {project_id}")
print("=" * 60)

# Check run_crawl
dependents = cg_service.get_dependents("run_crawl")
print(f"\n🎯 Function: run_crawl")
print(f"   Callers: {len(dependents)}")
if dependents:
    print("   Called by:")
    for caller in dependents[:5]:
        print(f"     - {caller}")

# Check some statistics
calls = graph.get("calls", {})
called_by = graph.get("called_by", {})

print(f"\n📈 Graph Statistics:")
print(f"   Total functions that call others: {len(calls)}")
print(f"   Total functions that are called: {len(called_by)}")

# Find a function with callers for testing
print(f"\n🔍 Functions with callers (sample):")
functions_with_callers = [(f, len(callers)) for f, callers in called_by.items() if callers]
functions_with_callers.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)

for func, count in functions_with_callers[:10]:
    print(f"   • {func}: {count} caller(s)")

print("\n" + "=" * 60)
