# scripts/test_change_engine.py - FIXED VERSION

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Test Change Engine - Phase 3"""

import sys
from pathlib import Path

project_root = Path(__file__).parent.parent
sys.path.insert(0, str(project_root))

from backend.services.refactor.change_engine import ChangeEngine
from backend.models.refactor import Parameter, RefactorType


def print_changes(plan):
    """Pretty print refactoring plan changes"""
    print(f"\n📋 Refactoring Plan: {plan.id[:8]}...")
    print(f"   Function: {plan.target_function}")
    print(f"   Type: {plan.refactor_type}")
    print(f"   Confidence: {plan.confidence * 100:.0f}%")
    print(f"   Requires Review: {'Yes' if plan.requires_review else 'No'}")
    
    if plan.warning:
        print(f"   ⚠️  Warning: {plan.warning}")
    
    print(f"\n📁 Affected Files: {len(plan.affected_files)}")
    for f in plan.affected_files[:3]:
        print(f"   • {Path(f).name}")
    
    print(f"\n📝 Changes: {len(plan.changes)}")
    for i, change in enumerate(plan.changes[:5], 1):
        print(f"\n   Change {i}:")
        print(f"   • Type: {change.change_type.value}")
        print(f"   • File: {Path(change.file_path).name}")
        print(f"   • Lines: {change.line_start}-{change.line_end}")
        print(f"   • Description: {change.description}")
        print(f"   • Before: {change.before[:80]}...")
        print(f"   • After:  {change.after[:80]}...")


def test_add_parameter():
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST 1: Add Parameter")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    engine = ChangeEngine()
    
    new_param = Parameter(
        name="timeout",
        type_hint="Optional[int]",
        default_value="None"
    )
    
    # FIXED: Use 'new_param' instead of 'new_parameter'
    plan = engine.generate_add_parameter(
        function_name="run_crawl",
        new_param=new_param,  # Changed from new_parameter to new_param
        default_value="30"
    )
    
    print_changes(plan)
    return plan


def test_remove_parameter():
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST 2: Remove Parameter")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    engine = ChangeEngine()
    
    plan = engine.generate_remove_parameter(
        function_name="run_crawl",
        parameter_name="start_url"
    )
    
    print_changes(plan)
    return plan


def test_rename_function():
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST 3: Rename Function")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    engine = ChangeEngine()
    
    plan = engine.generate_rename_function(
        function_name="run_crawl",
        new_name="run_crawl_v2"
    )
    
    print_changes(plan)
    return plan


def test_add_parameter_without_default():
    """Test adding a required parameter (breaking change)"""
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST 4: Add Required Parameter (Breaking)")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    engine = ChangeEngine()
    
    new_param = Parameter(
        name="required_param",
        type_hint="str",
        is_required=True
    )
    
    plan = engine.generate_add_parameter(
        function_name="run_crawl",
        new_param=new_param,  # No default value provided
    )
    
    print_changes(plan)
    return plan


def main():
    print("\n🚀 Change Engine Test Suite - Phase 3")
    print("Deep Refactoring Agent - Sprint 33")
    
    try:
        # Test 1: Add parameter with default
        plan1 = test_add_parameter()
        
        # Test 2: Remove parameter
        plan2 = test_remove_parameter()
        
        # Test 3: Rename function
        plan3 = test_rename_function()
        
        # Test 4: Add required parameter (breaking)
        plan4 = test_add_parameter_without_default()
        
        # Summary
        print("\n" + "=" * 60)
        print("✅ TEST SUMMARY")
        print("=" * 60)
        print(f"   Add Parameter (with default): {len(plan1.changes)} changes, {plan1.confidence:.0%} confidence")
        print(f"   Remove Parameter: {len(plan2.changes)} changes, {plan2.confidence:.0%} confidence")
        print(f"   Rename Function: {len(plan3.changes)} changes, {plan3.confidence:.0%} confidence")
        print(f"   Add Required Parameter: {len(plan4.changes)} changes, {plan4.confidence:.0%} confidence")
        
        # Verify expected behavior
        print("\n📊 Validation:")
        print(f"   ✓ Add with default should be non-breaking: {not plan1.breaking_changes if hasattr(plan1, 'breaking_changes') else 'N/A'}")
        print(f"   ✓ Remove parameter is breaking: {plan2.breaking_changes if hasattr(plan2, 'breaking_changes') else 'N/A'}")
        print(f"   ✓ Rename function is breaking: {plan3.breaking_changes if hasattr(plan3, 'breaking_changes') else 'N/A'}")
        
        print("\n✅ All tests completed! Ready for Phase 4 (API endpoints).")
        
        # Show sample change details
        if plan1.changes:
            print("\n💡 Sample Change (Add Parameter):")
            print(f"   File: {Path(plan1.changes[0].file_path).name}")
            print(f"   Before: {plan1.changes[0].before}")
            print(f"   After:  {plan1.changes[0].after}")
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"\n❌ Error: {e}")
        import traceback
        traceback.print_exc()


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Test CodeAnalyzer with call graph"""

import sys
from pathlib import Path

project_root = Path(__file__).parent.parent
sys.path.insert(0, str(project_root))

from backend.services.refactor.code_analyzer import CodeAnalyzer

def test_function(function_name: str):
    print(f"\n🔍 Testing CodeAnalyzer for: {function_name}")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    analyzer = CodeAnalyzer()  # Uses active project
    
    func_detail = analyzer.get_function_detail(function_name)
    
    if not func_detail:
        print(f"❌ Function '{function_name}' not found")
        return
    
    print(f"\n✅ Function found:")
    print(f"   Name: {func_detail.name}")
    print(f"   File: {func_detail.file_path}")
    print(f"   Lines: {func_detail.line_start}-{func_detail.line_end}")
    print(f"   Type: {'Method' if func_detail.is_method else 'Function'}")
    if func_detail.class_name:
        print(f"   Class: {func_detail.class_name}")
    print(f"   Parameters: {[p.name for p in func_detail.parameters]}")
    print(f"   Callers: {len(func_detail.callers)}")
    
    if func_detail.callers:
        print(f"\n📞 Callers:")
        for caller in func_detail.callers:
            print(f"   • {caller.calling_function} ({caller.file_path}:{caller.line_number})")
            print(f"     Call: {caller.source_line[:100]}")
            print(f"     Arguments: {caller.arguments}")
    
    return func_detail

if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Test run_crawl
    test_function("run_crawl")
    
    # Test with other functions
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    test_function("_run_crawl_with_cleanup")

# ========================================
# FILE: .\scripts\test_crawler_review.py
# ========================================

import sys
import os

sys.path.append(os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..")))

from backend.services.indexing.index_service import IndexService
from backend.services.graph.call_graph_service import CallGraphService
from backend.services.analysis.crawler_review_service import CrawlerReviewService
from backend.services.project_service import ProjectService


def run_test():

    project_root = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), ".."))
    project_service = ProjectService()
    project_config = project_service.get_active_project()

    # ----------------------------
    # INDEX
    # ----------------------------
    index_service = IndexService(project_config)
    index_result = index_service.build_index()

    # ----------------------------
    # GRAPH (still using disk-based for now)
    # ----------------------------
    graph_service = CallGraphService.__new__(CallGraphService)
    graph_service.symbols = index_result["symbols"]
    
    def build_graph_override():
        from collections import defaultdict

        graph = defaultdict(list)
        reverse = defaultdict(list)

        for sym in graph_service.symbols:
            caller = sym["name"]
            for callee in sym.get("calls", []):
                graph[caller].append(callee)
                reverse[callee].append(caller)

        return {
            "calls": dict(graph),
            "called_by": dict(reverse)
        }

    # ----------------------------
    # REVIEW
    # ----------------------------
    graph_service.build_graph = build_graph_override

    review_service = CrawlerReviewService(
        index_service=type("X", (), {"get_index": lambda self: index_result})(),
        graph_service=graph_service
    )

    result = review_service.build_review_context()

    print("\n===== ARCHITECTURE SUMMARY =====\n")
    print(result.get("architecture_summary"))

    print("\n===== HOTSPOTS =====\n")
    for h in result.get("hotspots", [])[:10]:
        print(h)

    print("\n===== MODULES =====\n")
    print(result.get("modules")[:20])

if __name__ == "__main__":
    run_test()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Simple test for extract method with smaller block"""

import sys
from pathlib import Path

project_root = Path(__file__).parent.parent
sys.path.insert(0, str(project_root))

from backend.services.refactor.llm_refactor_engine import LLMRefactorEngine
from backend.services.refactor.code_analyzer import CodeAnalyzer

def test_extract_simple():
    print("\nTesting Extract Method with smaller block")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    analyzer = CodeAnalyzer()
    func = analyzer.get_function_detail("run_crawl")
    
    if not func:
        print("Function not found")
        return
    
    print(f"Function lines: {func.line_start}-{func.line_end}")
    
    # Extract just 3 lines from the beginning of function body
    start = func.line_start + 1  # Skip def line
    end = min(start + 3, func.line_end - 1)
    
    print(f"Extracting lines {start}-{end}")
    
    # Show the lines being extracted
    lines = func.source_code.split('\n')
    start_idx = start - func.line_start
    end_idx = end - func.line_start
    print("\nCode to extract:")
    print("```")
    for i in range(start_idx, end_idx):
        print(f"{start + i - start_idx}: {lines[i][:80]}")
    print("```")
    
    engine = LLMRefactorEngine()
    
    plan = engine.generate_extract_method(
        function_name="run_crawl",
        start_line=start,
        end_line=end,
        new_method_name="_extracted_validation"
    )
    
    if plan:
        print(f"\n✅ Plan generated successfully!")
        print(f"   Changes: {len(plan.changes)}")
        for change in plan.changes:
            print(f"\n   📄 {Path(change.file_path).name}")
            print(f"   {change.description}")
            if change.after:
                print(f"   After preview: {change.after[:150]}...")
    else:
        print("\n❌ Failed to generate plan")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    test_extract_simple()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Test script for Impact Scanner
Run: python scripts/test_impact_scanner.py
"""

import sys
import os
from pathlib import Path

# Add project root to path
project_root = Path(__file__).parent.parent
sys.path.insert(0, str(project_root))

from backend.services.refactor.impact_scanner import ImpactScanner
from backend.models.refactor import Parameter
from backend.services.project_service import ProjectService


def print_section(title):
    """Print a formatted section header"""
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print(f"  {title}")
    print("=" * 60)


def test_add_parameter(scanner, function_name):
    """Test adding a parameter to a function"""
    print_section(f"Testing ADD PARAMETER on '{function_name}'")
    
    # Create new parameter
    new_param = Parameter(
        name="timeout",
        type_hint="Optional[int]",
        default_value="None",
        is_required=False
    )
    
    print(f"\n📝 Adding parameter: {new_param.name} (type: {new_param.type_hint})")
    
    # Analyze impact
    impact = scanner.analyze_add_parameter(function_name, new_param)
    
    # Display results
    print(f"\n📊 Impact Analysis Results:")
    print(f"  • Impact Level: {impact.impact_level.value.upper()}")
    print(f"  • Total Callers: {impact.total_callers}")
    print(f"  • Breaking Changes: {'⚠️ YES' if impact.breaking_changes else '✅ NO'}")
    print(f"  • Complexity Score: {impact.complexity_score:.2f}")
    print(f"  • Affected Files: {len(impact.affected_files)} file(s)")
    
    if impact.affected_files:
        print(f"\n📁 Affected files:")
        for f in impact.affected_files[:5]:  # Show first 5
            print(f"    • {f}")
        if len(impact.affected_files) > 5:
            print(f"    ... and {len(impact.affected_files) - 5} more")
    
    if impact.warnings:
        print(f"\n⚠️  Warnings:")
        for w in impact.warnings:
            print(f"    • {w}")
    
    if impact.suggestions:
        print(f"\n💡 Suggestions:")
        for s in impact.suggestions:
            print(f"    • {s}")
    
    return impact


def test_remove_parameter(scanner, function_name, param_name):
    """Test removing a parameter from a function"""
    print_section(f"Testing REMOVE PARAMETER from '{function_name}'")
    
    print(f"\n🗑️  Removing parameter: {param_name}")
    
    # Analyze impact
    impact = scanner.analyze_remove_parameter(function_name, param_name)
    
    # Display results
    print(f"\n📊 Impact Analysis Results:")
    print(f"  • Impact Level: {impact.impact_level.value.upper()}")
    print(f"  • Total Callers Affected: {impact.total_callers}")
    print(f"  • Breaking Changes: {'⚠️ YES' if impact.breaking_changes else '✅ NO'}")
    print(f"  • Complexity Score: {impact.complexity_score:.2f}")
    
    if impact.warnings:
        print(f"\n⚠️  Warnings:")
        for w in impact.warnings:
            print(f"    • {w}")
    
    if impact.suggestions:
        print(f"\n💡 Suggestions:")
        for s in impact.suggestions:
            print(f"    • {s}")
    
    return impact


def test_rename_function(scanner, function_name, new_name):
    """Test renaming a function"""
    print_section(f"Testing RENAME FUNCTION")
    
    print(f"\n✏️  Renaming: '{function_name}' → '{new_name}'")
    
    # Analyze impact
    impact = scanner.analyze_rename_function(function_name, new_name)
    
    # Display results
    print(f"\n📊 Impact Analysis Results:")
    print(f"  • Impact Level: {impact.impact_level.value.upper()}")
    print(f"  • Total Callers: {impact.total_callers}")
    print(f"  • Breaking Changes: {'⚠️ YES' if impact.breaking_changes else '✅ NO'}")
    print(f"  • Complexity Score: {impact.complexity_score:.2f}")
    
    if impact.warnings:
        print(f"\n⚠️  Warnings:")
        for w in impact.warnings:
            print(f"    • {w}")
    
    if impact.suggestions:
        print(f"\n💡 Suggestions:")
        for s in impact.suggestions:
            print(f"    • {s}")
    
    return impact


def list_available_functions(scanner):
    """Try to get available functions from the project"""
    print_section("Available Functions in Project")
    
    try:
        # Try to load symbols
        symbols = scanner.analyzer._load_symbols()
        
        functions = []
        for sym in symbols:
            if sym.get("type") in ["function", "method"]:
                func_name = sym.get("name")
                file_path = sym.get("file", "unknown")
                functions.append((func_name, file_path))
        
        if functions:
            print(f"\n📚 Found {len(functions)} functions/methods:")
            for func_name, file_path in functions[:10]:  # Show first 10
                print(f"  • {func_name} ({Path(file_path).name})")
            if len(functions) > 10:
                print(f"  ... and {len(functions) - 10} more")
        else:
            print("\n⚠️  No functions found. Make sure you have indexed your project.")
            
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"\n⚠️  Could not load symbols: {e}")
        print("   Make sure you have run indexing first.")


def test_with_diagnostic_info(scanner, function_name):
    """Provide diagnostic info when no callers found"""
    func_detail = scanner.analyzer.get_function_detail(function_name)
    
    if func_detail and len(func_detail.callers) == 0:
        print("\n" + "⚠️ " * 20)
        print("NOTE: No callers found for this function")
        print("⚠️ " * 20)
        print("\nPossible reasons:")
        print("  1. The function is never called in the codebase")
        print("  2. Call graph hasn't been built yet")
        print("  3. Call graph was built without recursive analysis")
        print("\nTo fix:")
        print("  • Run: python scripts/build_call_graph.py --recursive")
        print("  • Or rebuild index: python scripts/index_project.py --force")
        print("\n" + "⚠️ " * 20 + "\n")
        
        return False
    return True

def main():
    """Main test function"""
    print("\n🚀 Impact Scanner Test Suite")
    print("Phase 2: Deep Refactoring Agent - Sprint 33")
    
    # Get active project
    try:
        project_service = ProjectService()
        active_project = project_service.get_active_project()
        
        if not active_project:
            print("\n❌ No active project found!")
            print("   Please set an active project first:")
            print("   python scripts/manage_project.py --active <project_id>")
            return
        
        project_id = active_project["project_id"]
        print(f"\n✅ Active Project: {project_id}")
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"\n❌ Error getting active project: {e}")
        print("   Make sure your project is properly configured.")
        return
    
    # Initialize scanner
    try:
        scanner = ImpactScanner(project_id)
        print("✅ Impact Scanner initialized")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Failed to initialize scanner: {e}")
        return
    
    # List available functions
    list_available_functions(scanner)
    
    # Get function name from user or use default
    print("\n" + "-" * 60)
    print("Please enter a function name to test (or press Enter for demo):")
    
    # Try common function names from your codebase
    demo_functions = ["process_data", "main", "run", "execute", "handle_request", "get_data"]
    
    function_name = input("Function name: ").strip()
    
    if not function_name:
        # Try to find a function from symbols
        symbols = scanner.analyzer._load_symbols()
        for sym in symbols:
            if sym.get("type") in ["function", "method"]:
                function_name = sym.get("name")
                if function_name and not function_name.startswith('_'):
                    break
        
        if not function_name:
            print("\n❌ No function found. Please index your project first.")
            print("   Run: python scripts/index_project.py")
            return
        
        print(f"   Using demo function: {function_name}")
    
    # Run tests
    print(f"\n🔍 Analyzing function: {function_name}")
    
    # Test 1: Add parameter
    impact1 = test_add_parameter(scanner, function_name)
    
    # Test 2: Remove parameter (try to find a parameter first)
    func_detail = scanner.analyzer.get_function_detail(function_name)
    if func_detail and func_detail.parameters:
        param_to_remove = func_detail.parameters[0].name
        impact2 = test_remove_parameter(scanner, function_name, param_to_remove)
    else:
        print(f"\n⚠️  Could not find parameters for '{function_name}', skipping remove test")
        impact2 = None
    
    # Test 3: Rename function
    new_name = f"{function_name}_v2"
    impact3 = test_rename_function(scanner, function_name, new_name)
    
    # Summary
    print_section("TEST SUMMARY")
    print(f"\n📈 Results:")
    if impact1:
        print(f"  • Add Parameter: {impact1.impact_level.value}")
    if impact2:
        print(f"  • Remove Parameter: {impact2.impact_level.value}")
    if impact3:
        print(f"  • Rename Function: {impact3.impact_level.value}")
    
    print("\n✅ Impact Scanner tests completed!\n")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Test LLM Refactor Engine - Phase 4"""

import sys
from pathlib import Path

project_root = Path(__file__).parent.parent
sys.path.insert(0, str(project_root))

from backend.services.refactor.llm_refactor_engine import LLMRefactorEngine


def test_suggest_refactorings():
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST 1: Suggest Refactorings (LLM)")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    engine = LLMRefactorEngine()
    
    try:
        suggestions = engine.suggest_refactorings("run_crawl")
        print(f"\n✅ Suggestions received: {len(suggestions)}")
        for s in suggestions:
            print(f"   • Type: {s.get('type')}")
            print(f"     Reason: {s.get('reason', 'N/A')[:100]}")
            print(f"     Difficulty: {s.get('difficulty', 'N/A')}")
            print()
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Error: {e}")


def test_extract_method():
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST 2: Extract Method (LLM)")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    engine = LLMRefactorEngine()
    
    try:
        from backend.services.refactor.code_analyzer import CodeAnalyzer
        analyzer = CodeAnalyzer()
        func = analyzer.get_function_detail("run_crawl")
        
        if func:
            lines = func.source_code.split('\n')
            print(f"Function lines: {func.line_start}-{func.line_end}")
            print(f"Total lines in function: {len(lines)}")
            
            # Calculate valid line range within the function
            # Use line numbers relative to the file, not array index
            func_body_start = func.line_start + 1  # Skip the def line
            
            # Make sure we don't go beyond function end
            max_end = min(func.line_end, func_body_start + 10)
            
            if func_body_start < max_end:
                start = func_body_start
                end = max_end
                
                print(f"Extracting lines {start}-{end} from run_crawl")
                print(f"New method name: _extracted_helper")
                
                plan = engine.generate_extract_method(
                    function_name="run_crawl",
                    start_line=start,
                    end_line=end,
                    new_method_name="_extracted_helper"
                )
                
                if plan:
                    print(f"\n✅ Plan generated:")
                    print(f"   ID: {plan.id}")
                    print(f"   Confidence: {plan.confidence * 100:.0f}%")
                    print(f"   Changes: {len(plan.changes)}")
                    print(f"   Affected files: {len(plan.affected_files)}")
                    
                    for change in plan.changes:
                        print(f"\n   Change in {Path(change.file_path).name}:")
                        print(f"   {change.description}")
                        print(f"   Before preview: {change.before[:100]}...")
                        print(f"   After preview: {change.after[:100]}...")
                else:
                    print("❌ No plan generated")
            else:
                print(f"⚠️ Function too short for extraction test")
                print(f"   Function lines: {func.line_start}-{func.line_end}")
                print(f"   Calculated start: {func_body_start}, max end: {max_end}")
        else:
            print("❌ Could not find function run_crawl")
            
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Error: {e}")
        import traceback
        traceback.print_exc()


def test_inline_function():
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST 3: Inline Function (LLM)")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    engine = LLMRefactorEngine()
    
    try:
        # Find a function with at least one caller
        from backend.services.refactor.code_analyzer import CodeAnalyzer
        analyzer = CodeAnalyzer()
        func = analyzer.get_function_detail("run_crawl")
        
        if func and len(func.callers) > 0:
            print(f"Inlining function: run_crawl")
            print(f"Callers count: {len(func.callers)}")
            
            plan = engine.generate_inline_function("run_crawl")
            
            if plan:
                print(f"\n✅ Plan generated:")
                print(f"   ID: {plan.id}")
                print(f"   Confidence: {plan.confidence * 100:.0f}%")
                print(f"   Changes: {len(plan.changes)}")
                print(f"   Affected files: {len(plan.affected_files)}")
                
                for change in plan.changes:
                    print(f"\n   Change in {Path(change.file_path).name}:")
                    print(f"   {change.description}")
                    print(f"   Before: {change.before[:100]}...")
                    print(f"   After: {change.after[:100]}...")
            else:
                print("❌ No plan generated")
        else:
            print("⚠️ Function has no callers, skipping inline test")
            
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Error: {e}")


def test_api_endpoints():
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST 4: API Endpoints for LLM Refactor")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    import requests
    
    base_url = "http://localhost:8000/api/refactor"
    
    # Test suggest endpoint
    print("\n📡 POST /suggest/run_crawl")
    try:
        response = requests.post(f"{base_url}/suggest/run_crawl")
        if response.status_code == 200:
            data = response.json()
            print(f"✅ Success: {len(data.get('suggestions', []))} suggestions")
        else:
            print(f"⚠️ Status: {response.status_code}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Connection error: {e}")
        print("   Make sure server is running on port 8000")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("\n🚀 Testing LLM Refactor Engine (Phase 4)")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    test_suggest_refactorings()
    test_extract_method()
    test_inline_function()
    test_api_endpoints()
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("✅ Phase 4 tests completed!")

# ========================================
# FILE: .\scripts\test_prompt_builder.py
# ========================================

from backend.services.agent.prompt_builder import PromptBuilder
from backend.services.analysis.crawler_review_service import CrawlerReviewService
from backend.services.indexing.index_service import IndexService
from backend.services.graph.call_graph_service import CallGraphService


def run_test():
    index_service = IndexService()
    graph_service = CallGraphService()

    crawler = CrawlerReviewService(index_service, graph_service)
    crawler_data = crawler.build_review_context()

    builder = PromptBuilder()

    prompt = builder.build(
        intent="codebase_review",
        symbol_data={
            "symbol": "IDM-CODEBASE",
            "type": "system",
            "file": "ALL",
            "parent": None,
            "reasoning": crawler_data
        },
        question="Review the entire IDM crawler system and suggest improvements",
        history=[]
    )

    print("\n================ PROMPT OUTPUT ================\n")
    print(prompt)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    run_test()

# scripts/test_refactor_api.py

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Test Refactoring API endpoints"""

import requests
import json
from pathlib import Path

# Assuming your API runs on localhost:8000
BASE_URL = "http://localhost:8000/api/refactor"

def test_analyze_function():
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST: Analyze Function")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    response = requests.get(f"{BASE_URL}/analyze/function/run_crawl")
    
    if response.status_code == 200:
        data = response.json()
        print(f"✅ Function: {data['name']}")
        print(f"   File: {data['file_path']}")
        print(f"   Parameters: {len(data['parameters'])}")
        print(f"   Callers: {data['caller_count']}")
        print(f"   Is Async: {data['is_async']}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Error: {response.status_code} - {response.text}")

def test_impact_add_parameter():
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST: Impact Analysis - Add Parameter")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    payload = {
        "function_name": "run_crawl",
        "new_parameter": {
            "name": "timeout",
            "type_hint": "Optional[int]",
            "default_value": "None",
            "is_required": False
        },
        "default_value": "30"
    }
    
    response = requests.post(
        f"{BASE_URL}/impact/add-parameter",
        json=payload
    )
    
    if response.status_code == 200:
        data = response.json()
        print(f"✅ Impact Level: {data['impact_level']}")
        print(f"   Total Callers: {data['total_callers']}")
        print(f"   Breaking Changes: {data['breaking_changes']}")
        print(f"   Complexity Score: {data['complexity_score']}")
        if data['warnings']:
            print(f"   Warnings: {data['warnings'][0]}")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Error: {response.status_code} - {response.text}")

def test_generate_plan_add_parameter():
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST: Generate Plan - Add Parameter")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    payload = {
        "function_name": "run_crawl",
        "new_parameter": {
            "name": "timeout",
            "type_hint": "Optional[int]",
            "default_value": "None",
            "is_required": False
        },
        "default_value": "30"
    }
    
    response = requests.post(
        f"{BASE_URL}/plan/add-parameter",
        json=payload
    )
    
    if response.status_code == 200:
        data = response.json()
        print(f"✅ Plan ID: {data['id'][:8]}...")
        print(f"   Refactor Type: {data['refactor_type']}")
        print(f"   Confidence: {data['confidence'] * 100:.0f}%")
        print(f"   Changes: {len(data['changes'])}")
        print(f"   Affected Files: {len(data['affected_files'])}")
        
        # Show first change
        if data['changes']:
            change = data['changes'][0]
            print(f"\n   Sample Change:")
            print(f"   • File: {Path(change['file_path']).name}")
            print(f"   • Before: {change['before'][:80]}...")
            print(f"   • After:  {change['after'][:80]}...")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Error: {response.status_code} - {response.text}")

def test_search_functions():
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST: Search Functions")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    response = requests.get(f"{BASE_URL}/search/functions?query=crawl&limit=5")
    
    if response.status_code == 200:
        data = response.json()
        print(f"✅ Found {data['total']} functions")
        for func in data['functions'][:5]:
            print(f"   • {func['name']} ({func['type']})")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Error: {response.status_code}")

def test_available_refactorings():
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST: Available Refactorings")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    response = requests.get(f"{BASE_URL}/available-refactorings")
    
    if response.status_code == 200:
        data = response.json()
        print(f"✅ Available refactorings:")
        for ref in data['refactorings']:
            print(f"   • {ref['name']} ({ref['type']})")
            print(f"     {ref['description'][:60]}...")
    else:
        print(f"❌ Error: {response.status_code}")

def main():
    print("\n🚀 Refactoring API Test Suite")
    print("Make sure your FastAPI server is running on port 8000")
    print("\nTo start server: uvicorn main:app --reload --port 8000")
    
    try:
        # Test endpoints
        test_available_refactorings()
        test_search_functions()
        test_analyze_function()
        test_impact_add_parameter()
        test_generate_plan_add_parameter()
        
        print("\n" + "=" * 60)
        print("✅ All API tests completed!")
        print("=" * 60)
        
    except requests.exceptions.ConnectionError:
        print("\n❌ Could not connect to API server!")
        print("   Please start the server first:")
        print("   uvicorn main:app --reload --port 8000")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"\n❌ Error: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

# ========================================
# FILE: .\scripts\test_task_board.py
# ========================================

import sys
import os

sys.path.append(os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..")))

from backend.services.project_service import ProjectService
from backend.services.indexing.index_service import IndexService
from backend.services.graph.call_graph_service import CallGraphService
from backend.services.analysis.crawler_review_service import CrawlerReviewService
from backend.services.task.task_generator import TaskGenerator
from backend.services.task.task_storage import TaskStorage
from config import DATA_DIR, INDEX_DIR


def test_task_board():
    print("=" * 60)
    print("TESTING TASK BOARD SYSTEM")
    print("=" * 60)

    # Get project
    project = ProjectService().get_active_project()
    project_id = project["project_id"]
    print(f"\nProject: {project_id}")

    # Initialize services
    index_path = INDEX_DIR / project_id
    index_service = IndexService(project)
    graph_service = CallGraphService(index_path)
    crawler_service = CrawlerReviewService(index_service, graph_service)
    task_storage = TaskStorage(project_id, DATA_DIR)
    task_generator = TaskGenerator(crawler_service, graph_service)

    # Generate tasks
    print("\n[1] Generating tasks from codebase analysis...")
    tasks = task_generator.generate_tasks()
    print(f"    Generated {len(tasks)} tasks")

    # Display tasks
    print("\n[2] Task List:")
    for i, task in enumerate(tasks, 1):
        print(f"\n    {i}. [{task.priority.value.upper()}] {task.title}")
        print(f"       Category: {task.category.value}")
        print(f"       Evidence: {task.evidence[0].metric_type} = {task.evidence[0].metric_value}")
        if task.suggested_fix:
            print(f"       Fix available: Yes ({len(task.suggested_fix)} chars)")

    # Save tasks
    print("\n[3] Saving tasks to disk...")
    task_storage.save_tasks(tasks)
    print(f"    Saved to: {task_storage.tasks_file}")

    # Load and verify
    print("\n[4] Loading tasks from disk...")
    loaded = task_storage.load_tasks()
    print(f"    Loaded {len(loaded)} tasks")

    # Summary
    print("\n[5] Task Summary:")
    by_priority = {}
    for task in tasks:
        by_priority[task.priority.value] = by_priority.get(task.priority.value, 0) + 1
    print(f"    By priority: {by_priority}")

    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TASK BOARD TEST COMPLETE")
    print("=" * 60)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    test_task_board()
